Tahchunhnak ah:Na fa phone hman caan he aa tlaiin ri na khiahpiak maw?Zoh awkah aa tlak lomi pawl a thup khomi setting cu hmual a ngei tuk lo ti kha na hngal maw?Na fa nih a hmanmi phone kong kha na hngalh ahcun fimkhur tein hman awkah na bawmh khawh deuh lai.Baibal phunglam: “Hngalhnak a ngeimi cu thazaang a ngeimi nakin a ṭhawng deuh.”—Phungthlukbia 24:5.  Dingrep chiahpiak hna. Nawl na awnhmi le awnh lomi kong he aa tlaiin biakhiahnak tuah. Tahchunhnak ah:Rawl einak cabuai ah phone put dingin nawl na awnh lai maw, chungkhar asiloah hawikom pawl he nan lenṭi lioah phone put dingin nawl na awnh lai maw?A ihnak khaan ah phone i put dingin nawl na awnh lai maw?Zei bantuk app hna dah hman dingin nawl na awnh?Phone kha zei can dah na hmanter lai?Nikhat ah suimilam zeizat hman ding tiin ri na khiahpiak maw?Dingrep na chiahpiakmi hna kha hngalhter hna. Mah ningin an zulh lo ahcun zei tiang dah ka chimhhrinh hna lai timi kong he aa tlaiin timhtuahnak ngei.Baibal phunglam: “Ngakchia chimhhrin cu i sum hlah.”—Phungthlukbia 23:13.  Na fa phone kha check. Na fa phone password kha hngalh i zuam law a herh tik caan paohah a phone kha check. Ca an i kuatmi, app a hmanmi, hmanthlak le a zohmi website pawl zong kha check.“Chimh cia loin a herh caan paohah na phone kan check lai tiah kan fanu kha kan chimh. Dingrep ningin na hman lo ahcun phone na hman caan kan ṭhumh deuh lai tiah kan ti.”—Lorraine.Nulepa cu fale phone an hman ning kong he aa tlaiin hngalhnak nawl an ngei.Baibal phunglam: “Ngakchia hmanh nih a tuahmi a ṭhat le a din kha a tuahnak in amah lila nih a langhter ko.”—Phungthlukbia 20:11.  Phunglam kha cawnpiak. A hmaanmi thil tuah a duh nakhnga cawnpiak. Cutin tuah awkah zeicah a biapit? Ngakchia cheukhat cu tuah an duh tukmi thil pakhatkhat a um ahcun nulepa hngalh loin an tuah tawn caah a si.*Dinfel awk, i sum awk le a tuahmi thil ruangah a chuakmi kha ṭuanvo lak awk ti bantuk a ṭhami sining pawl kha sunsak dingin cawnpiak. A dingfelmi ngakchia nih cun phone kha fimkhur tein a hman.Baibal phunglam: “Upa ... cu chia le ṭha thleidan khawhnak a ngei cangmi an si.”—Hebru 5:14.Zoh a nuammi video i telin lung a nuamhter lomi thawngpang hna kha TV, phone, tablet le computer hna ah atu le atu kan hmuh cang hna.Mah thawngpang hna kha ngakchia pawl zong nih an zoh.Thawngpang chia hna ruangah lungdong in an um nakhnga lo na fale kha zeitindah na bawmh khawh hna?Thawngpang nih na fale kha zeitindah a hnorsuan khawh hna?Thawngpang ruangah na fale lungrethei in an um nakhnga lo zeitindah na bawmh khawh hna?Na fa nih ngaihchiat awk a simi thil a hmuh ah tah zeitin?Ngakchia tampi cu ngaihchiat awk a simi thil an hmuh tikah an lung a dong. Ngakchia cheukhat nih cun an intuarnak kong kha an chim lo nain ngaihchiat awk a simi thawngpang ruangah an lung a dong tuk.* Nulepa an lungre a theih deuh ahcun an lungre a thei deuh ve. Thawngpang an theihmi ruangah fale nih a pingin khua an ruah khawh. Tahchunhnak ah, fale cheukhat nih an hmuhmi thawngpang ningin an chungkhar cungah a cang lai tiah an ruah. Cucaah lung a nuamhter lomi thawngpang atu le atu a zohmi ngakchia pakhat nih mah bantuk lawngte a cang peng tiah a ruah khawh men. Thawngpang ningin a taktak ah thil sining a ṭhat le ṭhat lo kha ngakchia nih an hngalthiam men lai lo. Ngakchia pawl nih an theih rih lomi cu thawngpang a thlahtu hna caah a zohtu an tam deuh paohah a miak an hmuh deuh timi kha a si.  Cucaah lung a cawlcanghtermi thawngpang a si khawh nakhnga a zohtu hna nih zoh an duh chinmi phun in an tuah peng.Lung a nuamhter lomi thawngpang zoh awkah a caan kha rikhiahpiak hna. Mah cu na fale nih vawleicung ah a cangmi kong kha an hngalh a hau lo tinak a si lo. Asinain lung a nuamhter lomi thawngpang lawngte theih cu a ṭha lomi a si.“A caan ah kan nuva in thawngpang chia kong kha a dikthliar in kan i ruah tawn. Mah kong an theihmi nih kan fale a hnorsuan hna ti kha kan rak hngal lo.”—Maria.Baibal phunglam: “Lungretheihnak nih minung cu lunglawm loin a tuah.”—Phungthlukbia 12:25.  Lungsau tein ngaihpiak hna law zawnruahnak he lehrulh hna. Na fa nih a cangmi kong kha chim awkah aa harh ahcun hmanthlak in suaiter. Thinphannak a ngeihmi kha a ṭhat deuh nakhnga bia sawhsawh tein chim. A herh lo ahcun a konglam kha a dikthliar in chim hlah.“A pawngah ṭhu in a bia kan ngaihpiak tikah kan fanu cu aa nuam deuhmi a lo. ‘Mah hna cu a cang lengmangmi a si ko, zeidah a poi’ tiah kan ti ahcun aa nuam lai lo.”—Sarahi.Baibal phunglam: “Biachim lei ... cun a khul a nuarmi si u.”—Jeim 1:19. A cang taktakmi thawngpang kong kha an hngalh nakhnga bawm hna. Tahchunhnak ah, tangka hmuh duh ah mi pakhat an tlaih timi thawngpang nih a taktak ah a cangmi nakin thil sining cu a chia deuh tiah a ruahter khawh. Cucaah ṭhatlonak a ton nakhnga lo na huhphenhmi a si timi kong kha fiang tein chim. Cun a cang bal tuk lomi a si caah aa phundangmi thawngpang a sinak a si ti zong kha philhhlah.Na fale kha lungthinlei zongin bawm hna. Ruahnak hnuah intuarnak nih a zulh caah a ṭhami thil ah lungthin an pek nakhnga na fale kha bawm hna. Cutin nan tuah ahcun an hun i nuam lai.”—Lourdes.Baibal phunglam: “Mifim nih cun bia a chim hlanah a ruah hmasa, cucaah a chimmi cu hmual a ngei.”—Phungthlukbia 16:23Zohchunh awk ṭhami nulepa hna cu an fale an cawnpiak hna ningin an nung. Tahchunhnak ah, chawnh na duh lomi pakhatkhat nih aan leng hei ti u sih. Mah tikah na fa kha “inn ah a um lo tiah va ti” ti bantukin na chimter ahcun biatak chim awkah na cawnpiak kho lai lo.“‘Ka chim ningin tuah, ka tuah bantukin tuah hlah’ tiah an ti tawn. Asinain mah cu fale caah san a tlai lo. Annih cu ti a dawp khomi thil bantuk an si. Kan chimmi le kan tuahmi paohpaoh kha an i zohchunh, kan cawnpiakmi hna ningin kan nun lo ahcun kan chimmi kha an ngai duh lai lo.”—David.BAIBAL PHUNGLAM: “‘Fir hlah u,’ tiah phung a chimtu hna, zeicahdah nan fir kun?”—Rom 2:21.Ngakchia le kumhra fai mi hna cungah nulepa cu ṭhirual pawl le midang nakin huham an ngei deuh. Cucaah nulepa nih an chimmi ningin an tuah ahcun fale kha lam dik zulh awkah a hruai khotu an si lai.“Kan fale kha atu le atu kan cawnpiak hna caah a ngaih tal an ngai hnga maw tiah kan ruah khawh. Asinain voikhat te kan chimmi ningin kan tuah lo tikah mah kha kan fale nih an hngalh. Kan tuahmi an hngal lo tiah kan ruah tik hmanhah kan tuahmi thil kip kha ṭha tein an zoh.”—Nicole.BAIBAL PHUNGLAM: “Cunglei in a rami fimnak cu ... a zer zong a zer lo.”—Jeim 3:17.Na zulhmi phunglam kha dothlat. Zei bantuk nuamhsaihnak dah na zoh? Na innchunghawi le na fale zeitindah na pehtlaih hna? Ahote dah na komh hna? Midang cungah zawnruahnak na ngei maw? Na fale siter na duhmi hna phun in na um maw?“Kan nuva in kan zulh khawh lomi phunglam kha zulh awkah kan fale kan hnek hna lo.”—Christine.Na palh tikah ngaihthiam hal hna. Na fale nih mitlinglo na si ti kha an hngalh. Palhnak na tuah tikah na innchunghawi le na fale sinah “ka ngaithiam” timi bia na chim ahcun dinfelnak le toidornak ngeih awkah na cawnpiak khawh hna lai.“Kan fale nih palhnak kan tuah tikah kan phuanmi le ngaihthiamnak kan halmi hna kha an theih a hau. Cutin kan tuah lo ahcun palhnak thuh awkah kan cawnpiakmi hna bantuk a si lai.”—Robin.Na fa cu inn ah a um, tuah awk zong zeihmanh a ngei lo i “ka umhar tuk” tiah a ti. TV asiloah video game i celh tiah na ti hlanah mah a kong pawl hi ruat.Nuamhsaihnak caah hmanmi caan le tuahmi phun nih thil sining kha a chiatter chin. Pa pakhat a simi Robert nih hitin a ti: “Ngakchia cheukhat caah TV zoh asiloah video game celh he tahchunh tikah nifatin an nunnak cu umhar tuk a si.”A nupi Barbara zong nih a hna a tla i hitin a ti ve: “Nunnak taktak ahcun ruahnak le i zuamnak ngeih a hau i a phichuak cu a hnu lawngah hmuh a si. Cucaah TV a zohmi asiloah video game aa celhmi ngakchia hna caah cun mah cu umhartertu a si.” Social media lawng hmannak nih a ṭhalomi ruahnak a ngeihter khawh. An hawile taarmi hmanthlak le video pawl zohnak nih ka nunnak cu umhar tuk a si timi ruahnak a ngeihter khawh hna. Beth timi nu pakhat nih “midang an i nuamh tuk hna lioah kei bal cu inn ah ka um” tiah a ti.Social media hmannak ah a caan tamtuk peknak nih um a harter chin. Chris timi mino pa pakhat nih “ka rian cu a tam ngai ko, asinain zeidah ka tuah timi hmuhsak awk cu ka ngei lo” tiah a ti. Umharnak kha caan ṭha siter. Nu pakhat a simi Katherine nih umharnak cu ngakchia pawl caah thil tuah khawhnak caan ṭha a si kho tiah a ti. Tahchunhnak ah, “a sawhsawhte a simi bawm pakhat cu philh khawh lomi thilri pawl khonnak, mawṭaw, tilawng asiloah vanlawng zong a hung si kho. Ṭhutdan, cabuai pawl kha puan pakhat in an khuh tikah thlam pakhat zong a hung si kho.”Lungthin lei a hlathlaitu siibawi Sherry Turkle nih umharnak cu “thil ṭha tuahnak caan ṭha” a si kho tiah a ti.* Umhar cu a ṭha lo tinak a si lo. Disconnected timi cauk nih hitin a ti: “Thilrit cawinak nih kan tha a ṭhawnter bantukin umharnak nih khuaruah khawhnak a ṭhatter.”A biapimi a kong: Ngakchia pawl nih umharnak kha buaibainak in an hmuh nakhnga lo khuaruah khawhnak an ngeih chin nakhnga bawm hna.A si khawh ahcun na fale kha a lengah lente celhter hna. A hmasa ah langhtermi Barbara nih hitin a ti: “Nitlang le thli thiang nih umharnak kha a tlauter khawh. Ngakchia pawl cu a leng i lente an i celh ahcun khuaruah khawhnak an ngeihmi kha an hun hman deuh lai.”Baibal phunglam: “Zeizong vialte caah hin caan a um cio, ... nih caan [le] lam caan a um.”—Phungchimtu 3:1,4.Ruah awk a simi: Ka fale nih inn leng i lentecelhnak in hmuhtonnak an ngeih nakhnga zei caan ṭha dah ka pek hna? Inn lengah lente celh dingin a si khawh lo ahcun innchung ah celh khawhmi zei lentecelhnak phun dah ka tuahpiak khawh hna? Midang ca ruahpiak dingin na fale kha bawm hna. Nu pakhat a simi Lillian nih hitin a ti: “Kum upa kan hawile pawl belh phawipiak, thinghnah pawl charpiak, pakhatkhat chuanpiak le an dam le dam lo hal ti bantuk hna kha tuah. Midang ca thil tuahpiaknak nih lawmhnak taktak a chuahter.”Baibal phunglam: “Nun va siang law na rum lai, midang kha va bawm hna law an in bawmh ve lai.”—Phungthlukbia 11:25.Ruah awk a simi: Na fale kha midang bawmhnak in lawmhnak hmuh awkah zeitindah na bawmh khawh hna?  Zohchunhawk ṭha chia. Nifatin na ṭuanmi rian kong he aa tlaiin na chim ning cu na fale cungah huham a ngei kho. Nu pakhat a simi Sarah nih hitin a ti: “Nunnak cu um a har tuk ti phun in na chim ahcun na fale zong nih cutin an ruah ve lai. Nuam tein na um ahcun an i nuam ve lai.”Baibal phunglam: “Lung aa lawmmi hna caah cun nunnak hi a nuam zungzal ko.”—Phungthlukbia 15:15.Ruah awk a simi: Inn rian kong he aa tlaiin zeitindah ka chim? Ka fale nih ka um a har caan ah zei ka tuahmi dah an ka hmuh?Ruahnak cheuhnak: Na fale kha khuaruah khawhnak ngeih awkah bawm hna. Allison timi nu pakhat nih “bawm pakhat chia u law chungkharmi pakhat cio nih nan ruahnak kha ṭial u law sanh u” tiah a ti.Chungkhar hram a thawktu Jehovah Pathian nih fale zohkhenh hna awkah nulepa kha rian a pek hna. (Kolose 3:20) Ngakchia hna nih Jehovah Pathian an dawt nakhnga le ṭuanvo a la khomi upa an si khawh nakhnga nulepa nih nan cawnpiak hna awk a si. (2Timote 1:5; 3:15) Mah lengah fale hna i an lungthin ah zeidah a um ti zong hngalh khawh nan i zuam lai. Nan biachim le nan tuahsernak hna cu ngakchia caah a biapi tuk. Jehovah Pathian Bia kha a hmasa bikah na lung chungah na chiah ahcun ngakchia hna kha ṭha tein na cawnpiak khawh hna lai.—Salm 40:8.BAIBAL CHIMMI: ‘Bia theih duhnaklei ah a khul a rangmi si u law biachimnaklei ah a khul a nuarmi si u.’ (Jeim 1:19) Ngakchia hna kha nulepa sinah zalawng tein lung chungah a ummi bia chim khawh a si ti kha hngalhter na duh ko hna lai. Lung chungah a ummi bia chim an duh tikah nangmahlei in ngaihpiak hna awkah timhcia na si kha an hngalh a herh. Nangmahlei in chimh ngam dingin na um lawngah anmahlei in zalawng tein chim awkah a fawiter lai. (Jeim 3:18) Aw hrangpi in biachim a hmangmi asiloah sualnak kawl a hmangmi a si tiah an in ruah ahcun an lung chung i a ummi bia kha an in chim ngam ti lai lo. Cucaah na fale cungah na lungsau law zeitlukin dah na dawt hna ti kha atu le atu chim hna.—Matthai 3:17; 1Korin 8:1.NA TUAH KHAWHMI:Ngakchia hna nih biachim an duh tikah ngaihpiak hnaBuaibainak a chuah tik lawngah ngakchia hna he bia i ruah tibantuk si loin hmaan tein bia ruah peng hnaBAIBAL CHIMMI: “Thil pakhat kha a hngalthiammi nih cun hlawhtlinnak a hmuh lai.” (Phungthlukbia 16:20, NW) A caancaan ah ngakchia hna i an intuarnak taktak kha hngalh khawh awkah an chim duhmi kha hngalhthiam i zuam a herh. Zeicahtiah mino hna cu biaperh asiloah ruatsetsai loin biachim an hman caah a si. “Bia na leh hlanah ngai hmasa, cu ti na tuah lo ahcun na hruh a si.” (Phungthlukbia 18:13) Cucaah ngakchia hna cungah na thinhung colh hlah.—Phungthlukbia 19:11.NA TUAH KHAWHMI:Ngakchia hna nih zei an chim paohah lungcawlcangh in lehrulh colh asiloah an bia tan tibantuk tuah lo awkah biakhiakNangmah zong anmah ṭhi na si lioah zeibantuk ruahnak dah na rak ngeih ti le zei hna dah na caah a biapi tiah na rak ruah ti kha philhhlahBAIBAL CHIMMI: “Ka fapa, na pa cawnpiaknak cu ngai law na nu ṭhithruainak cu hlaw hlah.” (Phungthlukbia 1:8) Jehovah Pathian nih ngakchia zohkhenh hna awkah nulepa kha rian a pek hna. Cucaah ngakchia hna nih upatnak le nawlngaihnak an ngeih nakhnga nulepa hna nih cawnpiak hna u.(Efesa 6:1-3) Nulepa hna “lungnge tein” le “lungthin khat” tein nan um lo ahcun mah kha ngakchia hna nih an hngalh khawh. (1Korin 1:10) Nan lung aa khah lo hmanhah ngakchia hna kha theihter hna hlah u.Mah lawngah ngakchia hna nih an in upat khawh hna lai.NA TUAH KHAWHMI:Ngakchia hna kha zeitindah kan cawnpiak hna lai ti kha i ruahṭi u law mah ningin tuah uNgakchia hna cawnpiaknak kong he aa tlaiin nan hmuhnak aa khah lo ahcun innchung hawi i a hmuhnak kha hngalhthiam i zuamBAIBAL CHIMMI: “A zulh awk a simi lam kha ngakchia cu cawnpiak.” (Phungthlukbia 22:6) Ngakchia hna cu anmah tein fimnak an hung ngei lai lo. Timhtuahnak ngeih in na cawnpiak hna an hau. Mah ah chimhhrinhnak zong aa tel. (Salm 127:4; Phungthlukbia 29:17) Chimhhrinh timi cu dantat men lawng kha a chim duhmi a si lo. Mah ah an caah dingrep na chiahpiak hnanak a ruang kha an theihthiam nakhnga chimh hna zong aa tel. (Phungthlukbia28:7) Mah lengah Jehovah Pathian i a Bia kha an duh nakhnga le a lamhruainak hna kha an theihthiam nakhnga cawnpiak hna. (Salm 1:2) Mah lawngah an chiaṭha thleidannak lungthin a ṭhangcho lai.—Hebru 5:14.NA TUAH KHAWHMI:Pathian cu bochan khawhmi a si ti kha ngakchia hna nih an hmuhthiam nakhnga cawnpiak hnaInternet in hawikom i ser tibantuk ziaza a rawhter khomi thil ṭihnung hna kha hngalthiam in an hrial khawh nakhnga ngakchia hna kha cawnpiak hna. Nupa sinaklei in a miak a kawlmi hna kha zeitindah hrial khawh an si ti kha an hngalh nakhnga cawnpiak hnaNa fa cu caankhat khat ah sunghnak asiloah lungdongh awk a simi thil hna a tong kho. Mah kha a tei khawh nakhnga zeitindah na bawmh khawh hna?Na hngalh awk a simiNa tuah khawhmiSunghnak cu mikip nih kan tonmi a si. Baibal nih “kan dihlak hin palhnak kan tuah cio tawn” tiah a ti. (Jeim 3:2) Cucaah fale zong nih palhnak an tuah ve. Asinain a ṭhatnak cu harnak a tongmi ngakchia pawl cu lungṭhawnnak an ngei deuh. Mah cu an i chuahpimi a si lo caah lungṭhawnnak an ngeih nakhnga cawnpiak an hau. Laura timi nu pakhat nih hitin a ti: “A cangmi thil kha i theihter loin um canah sungnak kha cohlan thiam awkah fale cawnpiak cu a ṭha deuhmi a si ti kha kan nuva in kan hngalh. An i ruahchanmi ningin thil a can lo tikah zeitindah tawnghtham ding a si ti kha kan fale nih an hngalh.”Ngakchia tampi nih sunghnak kha cohlan awkah an i harh. Fale cheukhat nih sunghnak cohlan awkah an i harhnak a ruang cu nulepa nih an runven peng hna caah a si. Tahchunhnak ah, an fa cu ca a thiam lo ahcun saya/ sayamah te kha sual an phawt hna. An hawile he an i sik tikah an hawile tu kha sual an phawt colh hna.Nulepa nih thil sining kip ah an runven hna ahcun fale nih an palhnak kha zeitindah ṭuanvo an lak khawh ti lai?An tuahsernak ningin an zun lai ti kha na fale cawnpiak hna.Baibal chimmi: “Mi nih a tuhmi cu a zun ko lai.”—Galati 6:7.Kan tuahsernak kip ah a phichuak a um. Thil pakhat kha kan hrawh sual ahcun remh man a um. Cu bantukin palhnak kan tuah ahcun ṭhatlonak kan tong lai. A ruang a um caah a phichuak a ummi a si, fale nih kan tuahmi thil cu kanmah nih ṭuanvo kan lak awk a si ti kha an hngalh a hau. Cucaah na fa nih palhnak a tuah tikah runven in midang kha sual phaw hna hlah. Mah canah an kum he aa tlakin an tuahsernak cu zun ko hna seh. A ṭha lomi an tuahsernak ruangah ṭhatlonak an tonmi a si ti kha fiang tein hngalhter hna. Tawnghtham ning hngalh awkah na fale kha bawm hna.Baibal phunglam: “Miṭha mi cu voi sarih tiang tlu hmanh sehlaw a tho ṭhan zau lai.”—Phungthlukbia 24:16.Sunghnak cu ngaihchiat awk thil a si ko nain mah cu kan nunnak a donghnak a si rih lo. A ding lomi a si timi ruahnak ruangah lungsi loin um canah tawnghtham ning tu kha kawl awkah na fa kha bawm. Tahchunhnak ah, na fapa cu camipuai a sung hei ti u sih. A sungh ṭhan nakhnga lo ca i zuam awkah bawm. (Phungthlukbia 20:4) Na fanu cu a hawile he an i si hei ti u sih. Amah palhnak a si lo hmanhah ngaihthiamnak bia chim in i rem ṭhan khawh ning kong kha cawnpiak.—Rom 12:18; 2Timote 2:24. Toidornak ngeih awkah na fale kha cawnpiak hna.Baibal phunglam: “Hi bia hi nan dihlak sinah ka chim: Nanmahle nanmah kha a sang tuk ah i ruat hlah u.”—Rom 12:3.Na fa kha “a thiam bik” na si tiah na timi cu aa tlak lomi a si i ṭhatnak zong a um lo. A thiam taktakmi ngakchia hmanh nih sianginn ah pakhatnak an hmu zungzal lo. Zaanglente celh a thiammi hna zong nih teinak an hmu zungzal lo. Anmahle anmah a tlari tein aa hmuthiammi ngakchia pawl nih sunghnak le lungretheihnak hna kha an cohlan thiam.Baibal nih harnak kan tonmi nih kan lungthin a ṭhawnter i inkhawhnak ngeih awkah a kan bawmh tiah a ti. (Jeim 1:2-4) Cucaah sunghnak le lungretheihnak hna cu a cang tawnmi a si tiah an cohlan khawh nakhnga na fale kha bawm hna.A dang fimthiamnak cawnpiak bantukin lungthin ṭhawnnak an ngeih nakhnga cawnpiak awkah a caan le thazaang pek a hau. Asinain kumhra fai an si tikah ṭhatnak an hmu lai. “Buaibainak a tawngtham khomi kumhra fai pawl cu lungretheihnak an ton tikah hrut ngaiin thil tuah awkah a ruang a tlawm deuh. An i ruahchan lomi thil a can tik zongah thil sining he aa tlak in an um kho” tiah Letting Go With Love and Confidence timi cauk nih a ti. Lungthin ṭhawn dingin cawnpiaknak nih an upat tiang ṭhatnak a pek hna.Ruahnak cheuhnak: Zohchunh awk ṭha chia. Na fale kha na tonmi lungretheinak hna na tawnghtham ningin na cawnpiak khawh hna ti kha i cinken.Na fa cu sianginn ca zoh a huam lo, inn ah tuah dingmi ca kha a tuah lo i ca zong a ciah lo. Cucaah a mark a ṭum i a ziaza zong a hun rawk. Na fa kha a mark a ṭhat deuh nakhnga zeitindah na bawmh khawh?Hngalh awk a simiNa tuah khawhmiHneknak nih thil sining kha a chiatter chin. Na hnek tuk ahcun na fa cu sianginn le inn ah lungrethei in a um kho. A lungretheihnak a zor deuh nakhnga lih a hun chim men lai, a mark a ṭummi kha chim loin a um men lai, sianginn mark cazin ah na minthut deu kha a hman men lai asiloah sianginn hmanh a tli men lai. Cuticun thil sining cu a chia chin.Laksawng peknak nih aa ralkahmi thil a chuahter khawh. Pa pakhat a simi Andrew nih hitin a ti: “Kan fanu kha i zuam seh ti kan duh caah a mark a ṭhat deuh tikah laksawng kan pek. Mah tikah kan fanu nih laksawng hmuh ding lawng kha a hun ruah. A mark a tlawm deuh tikah a mark a tlawm caah si loin laksawng a hmuh lo ca tu ah a ngaih a chia deuh.”Saya/ Sayamah te sualphawt cu na fa caah a ṭhahnem lo. Na fa nih ka mark a ṭhat deuh nakhnga i zuam a hau lo tiah a ruah khawh men. Midang kha sual a phawt men hna lai, cun a tonmi buaibainak kha tawnghthampiak awkah midang kha a hun i bochan men hna lai. A tawinak in chim ahcun a upat tikah a biapimi rian hna kha ṭuanvo a la kho lai lo.Na intuarnak kha i uk. Na thin a hun lioah na fa he a mark kong kha i ruahceihṭi hlah u. Pa pakhat a simi Brett nih “kan lung a daih lio caan ah i ruahceihṭi cu kan nuva caah a ṭha bikmi a si” tiah a ti.Baibal phunglam: “Bia theih duhnak lei ah cun a khul a rangmi si u law biachimnak lei le thinhunnak lei ah cun a khul a nuarmi si u.”—Jeim 1:19.Buaibainak taktak kha hngalh i zuam. Midang nih nehsawhnak, sianginn i ṭhialnak, camipuai ṭihnak, chungkhar buaibainak, i hngilh khawh lonak, ṭha tein cazin ngei lonak le lungthin pek khawh lonak ti bantuk ruangah a mark a ṭummi a si men lai. A tha a thut tuk caah a si tiah ruat hlah.Baibal phunglam: “An in cawnpiakmi kha ṭha tein ruat law khuaawng na tong lai.”—Phungthlukbia 16:20.Ca zoh khawh awkah a daimi pawngkam kha timhtuahpiak. Inn ah tuah dingmi ca tuahnak le ca ciahnak caah cazin tuahpiak. Ca zohnak in na fa a lung a vaivuanhter khomi thil (TV le phone i telin) hna a um lonak hmun kha timhtuahpiak. Ca zohnak caah a caan tawite in ri khiahpiak law lungthin a pek khawh nakhnga bawm. Germany ram i pa pakhat a simi Hector nih hitin a ti: Camipuai a naih tikah camipuai ni a phanh dengmang tiang hngak loin nikhat ah tlawmpal tete in kan zohpi ṭhan.”Baibal phunglam: “Zeizong vialte caah hin caan a um cio.”—Phungchimtu 3:1.Cawn duhnak ngeih dingin thape. Na fa nih sianginn kai a ṭhatnak kong hna kha ṭha tein a hngalh ahcun cawn duhnak a ngei deuh lai. Tahchunhnak ah, kanan a thiam ahcun changreu cawknak ca tangka tuak dan a thiam lai.Baibal phunglam: “Fimnak kha cawng. Hngalhthiamnak kha cawng. ... Na lung chungah i chiah.”—Phungthlukbia 4:5, NW,8.Ruahnak cheuhnak: Inn ah tuah dingmi ca kha zohpi, asinain a ca kha nangmah nih tuahpiak hlah. Andrew nih hitin a ti: “Kan fanu nih amah thluak kha hmang loin kanmah lawngte a kan hal.” Cucaah na fa kha amah tein ca zoh ning kha cawnpiak.Na fapa nih sianginn ah nehsawhnak ka tong tiah a ti. Zeidah na tuah khawh? A nehsawhtu kha dantatpiak awkah sianginn kha na chim hna lai maw? Na fa kha teirul cham awkah na cawnpiak lai maw? Biakhiahnak na tuah hlanah nehsawhnak he aa tlaiin a kong cheukhat kha ruat.*Nehsawhnak kong he aa tlaiin zeidah ka hngalh awk a si?Zeitindah ka bawmh khawh?Nehsawhnak timi cu zeidah a si? Nehsawhnak timi cu hramhram in pumsalei le lungthinlei ah harnak pek kha a si. Cucaah serhsatnak asiloah ralchanhnak paohpaoh cu nehsawhnak a si lo.Zeicah a biapit: Mi cheukhat nih thil hmete a si hmanhah midang ngaih a chiattermi tuahsernak vialte caah “nehsawhnak” timi biafang kha an hman. Asinain thil hmetete kha thil nganpi na siter ahcun na fa kha atu le hmailei caah a herhmi sining le bia alnak hna tawnghtham awkah sining a tlinh nakhnga lo na cawnpiakmi bantuk a si lai.Baibal phunglam: “Na thin sum khawh kha i zuam.”—Phungchimtu 7:9.A biapimi kong: Thil sining cheukhat cu nangmah nih tawnghthampiak a hau men lai nain thil sining cheukhat tu ahcun na fa kha buaibainak tawnghtham thiam awk le mi pawl he rem tein um awkah cawn dingin caanṭha na pek khawh.—Kolose 3:13.Asinain na fa nih hramhram in serhsat ka si tiah a ti ah tah zeitin?Na fa nih a chimmi kha lungsau tein ngaihpiak. (1) Zeidah a cang ti le (2) zeicah nehsawhnak a ton ti kha hngalh awkah i zuam. Thil sining na hngalh dih hlan cu biakhiahnak tuah hlah. Hitin i hal, ‘Ka hngalh rih lomi zeidah a um kho rih?’ Thil sining dihlak na hngalh dih cang a si ahcun na fa i a saya/sayamah asiloah na fa a nehsawhtu i a nu le a pa he bia nan i ruah a hau kho men.Baibal phunglam: “Bia na leh hlanah ngai hmasa, cuti na tuah lo ahcun na hruh a si hleiah bia na lehmipa zei i na rel lo zong a si.”—Phungthlukbia 18:13.  Na fa nih nehsawhnak a ton ahcun a lehrulh ning nih thil sining a ṭhatter khawh bantukin a chiat zong a chiatter khawh ti kha hngalhthiam awkah bawm. Tahchunhnak ah, Baibal nih “lehnak neem nih thinhunnak a damter, sihmanhsehlaw biahrang nih cun thin a phawh” tiah a ti. (Phungthlukbia 15:1) Teirul chamnak nih nehsawhnak a tonmi kha zorter loin a zualter chin khawh.Baibal phunglam: “Ṭhatlonak kha ṭhatlonak in lehrul hlah u, volhpamhnak kha volhpamhnak in lehrul fawn hlah u.”—1 Peter 3:9.  Na fa kha teirul cham loin um cu thazaang der a si lo ti kha chim. Midang ukmi sinak a tei khawhmi cu a ṭhawn caah a si. Phundang cun nehsawhnak a tei khawhmi a si.Na fa nih online hmangin nehsawhnak a ton ahcun mah hi a hleiin aa cinken a hau. Online in pakhat le pakhat i doh lengmang cu nehsawhnak ton peng rih awk asiloah nehsawhnak ton awkah lam awnpiak bantuk a si. Cucaah a caan ah a ṭha bikmi lehrulh ning cu lehrulh loin um kha a si. Mah nih nehsawhnak kha a zorter deuh lai.Baibal phunglam: “Thing a um lo ahcun mei cu a mit.”—Phungthlukbia 26:20.  Thil sining cheukhat ah na fa nih nehsawhnak a chuahter khomi minung le hmun kha a hrial khawh hna. Tahchunhnak ah, nehsawh a hmangmi pakhatkhat asiloah mibu an umnak hmun kha a hngalh ahcun lam dang in a hrial khawh.Baibal phunglam: “Mifim nih cun harnak a rat kha a hmuh tikah hrial khawhnak aa zuam, sihmanhsehlaw mihrut nih cun a pahchih thluahmah ko i a hnuah aa ngaichih.”—Phungthlukbia 22:3.Na fa i a saya, sayamah asiloah na fa a nehsawhtu i a nu le a pa he bia nan i ruah a hau kho menMAH HI TUAHCHUNH: Aa thimmi thil ruangah a chuakmi ṭhatnak le chiatnak kha ruah khawh awkah na fa kha bawm. Tahchunhnak ah:Nehsawhnak kha zei rel loin a um ahcun zeidah a cang kho?Nehsawh lo awkah hlangfang tein a ti hna ah tah zeitin?Nehsawhnak a tonmi kong kha sianginn ah a phuan hna ah tah zeitin?Nehsawhnak kha i hawikomhnak asiloah capo saihnak in a “tei” kho lai maw?Nehsawhnak a tonmi cu hmaitonh in a si ah, online in a si ah thil sining cu aa lo lo. Cucaah na fa he zulh awk a tlakmi tawnghtham khawhning kha kawlṭi u. Kaan bawmh peng lai tiah na fa kha chim.Baibal phunglam: “Hawikom nih cun zeitik paohah dawt zungzal a si, u le nau cu harnak i hrawm awkah hrin kan si.”—Phungthlukbia 17:17.Nulepa hna, nan fale kha ṭihnungmi thil sining in huhphenh hna u!“Kan fanu kum ruk a si lioah zu kong he aa tlaiin a hmasa bik kan rak chimh. Kan ruahnak lengin a hngalh deuh caah kan khuaruah a har.”—Alexander.Hngalh awk a simiNa tuah khawhmiZu kong he aa tlaiin Baibal chimmiFale zu kong chimh cu a biapimi a si. Na fa cu kumhra fai a si tiang hngak hlah. “Kan fapa kha zu a zafang in dinnak kong he aa tlaiin a ngakchiat deuh lioah rak chim u sih law a ṭha tuk hnga” tiah Russia ram ah a ummi Khamit nih a ti. “Cutin chimh a biapitnak cu a hnu lawngah ka hngalh. Atu cu kum 13 a simi kan fapa cu zu a ding peng cang.”Mah kong cu zeicah biapi ah na chiah awk a si?  Sianginn kaiṭihawi, thanhlaar le TV program hna cu zu kong he aa tlaiin na fale an hmuhning cungah huham an ngei kho.  US i Zawtnak Khamhnak le Kilvennak ningin United States ah zu a dingmi zatuak in 11 cu kumtling lo an siNulepa nih fale an ngakchiat lioin zu kong chimh awkah siilei fimthiamnak a ngeimi hna nih an forhmi hna cu khuaruahhar awk a si lo. Zeitindah na tuah khawh?Na fa biahalnak kha leh awkah i timchung. Ngakchia pawl nih zei paoh hngalh an duh, a hleiin mino pawl nih hngalh duhnak an ngei. Cucaah an halmi paoh leh khawh awkah ṭha tein i timtuah. Tahchunhnak ah:  Na fa nih zu a thawtnam kong he aa tlaiin hngalh a duh ahcun wine cu a thur i beer cu a kha tiah chim.  Na fa nih zu din chun a duh ahcun ngakchia pum caah zu din cu a ṭha lo ti kha na chimh khawh. Zu dinnak nih mi a hrimhter asinain tam tuk dinnak nih lung a mihter i a hnuah i ngaihchih dingmi bia a chimter khawh ti kha chim.—Phungthlukbia 23:29-35.Nangmah theng nih hlathlai. Baibal nih hitin a ti: “Mifim cu a fim i zei thil paoh kha a thuhphenh.” (Phungthlukbia 13:16) Zu dinnak he aa tlaiin hngalhnak ngei. Cun zu he aa tlaiin nan ram upadi le ri an khiahmi kha hlathlai. Cutin na tuah ahcun na fale kha ṭha tein na bawmh khawh hna lai.Zu kong he aa tlaiin nangmah nih chim hmasa hna. Britain ram i Mark timi pa pakhat nih hitin a ti:  “Zu dinnak nih ngakchia pawl kha an lung a tuaiter khawh hna. Kum riat a simi ka fapa kha zu din hi a ṭha maw asiloah a ṭha lo dah tiah ka hal. Caan a rem lioah a hmuh ning kha ka hal caah zalong tein a ka chimh.Zu kong he aa tlaiin caanṭha kan ngeih fatin kan chimh hna ahcun an i cinken ko lai. Na fale an kum cungah i hngat in zu kong lawng si loin mawṭaw le lam kong he aa tlaimi dingrep zong kha chim hna. Cun nupa sinak kong zong kha chim hna.Zohchunhawk ṭha si. Ngakchia pawl cu ti a dopmi thil bantuk an si caah an pawngkam ah a ummi thil sining hna kha an cawn. Cucaah nulepa cu an fale cungah huham an ngei tuk tiah hlathlaitu hna nih an ti. Na lungretheihnak zorter awkah zu a dingmi na si ahcun na fale nih zu cu thadamnak caah dinmi sawhsawh in an hmuh lai. Cucaah zohchunhawk ṭha si. Zu kha a zafang lawngin ding.Kumhra fai fale cheukhat cu nulepa nih ri khiahpiakmi caan kha zei ah an rel lo. Cheukhat nih an nu le an pa kha an hlen hna. An hawile he i ton awkah inn in a thli tein an chuak. Kumhra fai na fa nih zumhawktlak loin a um tikah zeidah na tuah khawh?Kumhra fai ka fa cu ralchanhtu a si maw?Kumhra fai ka fa nih a ka hleng maw?Ahodah mawhchiat awk a si?Kumhra fai ka fa nih ka zumhnak a hmuh ṭhan khawh nakhnga zeitindah ka bawmh khawh?Nulepa chimmiA si lo. Baibal nih “ngakchia nih hin hruhnak thil le thil ṭhalo hi an tuah tawn phung a si” tiah a ti. Kumhra fai pawl nih mah bia a hmaan ti kha an langhter lengmang. (Phungthlukbia 22:15) Dr.Laurence Steinberg nih hitin a ti: “Kumhra fai pawl nih khulrang in le hrut ngaiin biakhiahnak cheukhat an tuah tawn. Cucaah palhnak cheukhat an tuah lai ti kha i ruahchan.”*Kumhra fai na fa nih na bia kha hramhram in a ngaih duh lomi a si tiah ruat hlah. Kumhra fai hna i an tuahsernak cu aa phun dang nain an nu le an pa nih zeitindah a kan hmuh timi tu cu biapi ah an chiah tiah mifim pawl nih an ti. Kumhra fai fale nih mah kha an langhter lo nain an tuah sualmi thil le nulepa lungre an in theihter hna caah an ngaih a chia men ko lai.*A kiakmi ruh cu a dam ṭhan ahcun a hlan bantukin a ṭhawng ṭhan kho. Zumhawktlak loin umnak zong cutin a si khoA pawngkam maw? Baibal nih hitin a ti: “Hawi ṭhalo nih ziaza ṭha a hrawh.” (1Korin 15:33) Kumhra fai pawl cu an hawile pawl nih an cungah fakpi in huham an ngeih khawh hna ti cu a hmaan ko. Mah lengah social media le thanhlaar hna zong an um rih. Mah pawl hna ruangah hmuhtonnak a ngei lomi kumhra fai pawl nih zeicah hrut ngaiin biakhiahnak an tuah ti kha fiang tein kan hngalh khawh. Asinain an biakhiahnak i a phichuak kha cohlan awkah an cawn a hau. Mah lawngah nutling patling le bochan awk a tlakmi upa an hung si lai.Keimah palh a si maw? Dingrep ka chiah tuk ahcun ka  fa cu a zia a rawk lai tiah na ruah men lai. Asiloah ka thlahdorh tuk ahcun kumhra fai ka fa nih zalonnak tam tuk a hmuh sual lai tiah na ruah men lai. Nangmahlei in palhnak ka tuah sual lai tiah thinphan canah zeitindah ka bawmh khawh lai timi tu kha ruat.Na lehrulh ning kha i ralring. Kumhra fai na fa nih na thin a hung lai ti kha a hngalh ko men lai. Mah tikah na thin i sum. Lungdai tein um law kumhra fai na fa he buaibainak a chuahnak a ruang kha i ruahṭi u. Hngalh a duh caah a si maw? A um a har caah a si maw? A li a len caah a si maw? A hawile a ṭih hna caah a si maw? Mah cu buainaknak a chuahnak a ruang taktak cu a si lo nain zeicah buaibainak a chuah ti kha hngalhthiam awkah kumhra fai na fa kha a bawmh khawh.Baibal phunglam: “Bia theih duhnak lei ah cun a khul a rangmi si u law biachimnak lei le thinhunnak lei ah cun a khul a nuarmi si u.”—Jeim 1:19. Kumhra fai na fa kha a cangmi thil kong tuaktan thiam awkah bawm. Mah hmuhtonnak in zeidah na cawn khawh? A hnuah mah bantuk thil na ton ahcun zeitindah na tawnghtham lai? ti bantuk biahalnak hna kha tuah. Cu bantuk biahalnak nih kumhra fai na fa kha a ṭhami biakhianak tuah awkah a bawmh khawh.Baibal phunglam: “Chimhhrin a herh ahcun chimhring hna, a nawl in nawl a herh ahcun nawl hna law lungsau thinfual in cawnpiak hna.”—2Timote 4:2. A tuahsernak ruangah a phichuak a um ti kha a hngalh nakhnga bawm. Nulepa nih dingrep nan chiahmi kha chim ṭhan. Mah nih a palhnak kha hngalh awkah a bawmh lai. Tahchunhnak ah, kumhra fai na fa cu a hawile he sianginn an tlik ahcun caan caankhat tiang a hawile he i ton lo awkah ri na khiahpiak khawh.Baibal phunglam: “Ahohmanh nih Pathian cu an deh kho lo. Mi nih a tuhmi cu a zun ko lai.”—Galati 6:7. Zumh ṭhan khawh awkah zeitindah ka tuah lai timi kha biapi ah chia. A caan lak a hau ti cu a hmaan ko. Asinain a caan lak ahcun zumh ṭhan khawh awkah tuah khawh a si ti kha kumhra fai na fa nih a hngalh awk a si. Cun na fa kha na zumhnak a hmu ṭhan kho ti kha hngalhter. Kumhra fai na fa nih na zumhnak ka hmu ṭhan ti bal lai lo tiah a ruah ahcun aa zuam ti lai lo.Baibal phunglam: “Nulepa hna, nan fale kha an ing puanter hna hlah u, an hnabei a dong sual lai.”—Kolose 3:21.Hngalh awk a simiNa tuah khawhmiNulepa chimmiNunphung cheukhat ahcun fale cu nulepa he a ṭhami pehtlaihnak an ngei i nulepa lamhruainak zong an zulh. Asinain nunphung cheukhat tu ahcun fale nih an ṭhirual pawl sin tu ah ruahnak cheuhnak an hal hna.An ṭhirual pawl sinah ruahnak cheuhnak a halmi ngakchia pawl cu an nu le an pa nawl an ngai duh ti lo. Cu bantuk ngakchia pawl cu kumhra fai an hung si tikah uk khawh an si ti lo tiah nulepa nih an ruah. Mah cu khuaruahhar awk a si lo. Ngakchia pawl cu an hawile he caan tam tuk an hmanṭi tikah nulepa nih zohkhenh si loin an hawile he pakhat le pakhat an i zohkhenhmi bantuk a si.Ngakchia pawl caah an nu le an pa nakin an ṭhirual pawl he i komh cu zeicah a fawi deuh? A tanglei kong hna hi ruathmanh. Sianginn. Ngakchia pawl cu sianginn ah an hawile he caan tampi an hmangṭi, cucaah an nu le an pa ruahnak nakin an ṭhirual pawl ruahnak tu kha an hun duh deuh. Kumhra fai an si tikah mah an ruahnak cu a hung ṭhawng chinchin.Ngakchia pawl nih an sianginn kaiṭihawi nakin nulepa cohlanmi si kha biapi ah an chiah deuh awk a si A caan pek khawh lonak. Innchungkhar tampi ah nulepa cu rian an ṭuan caah an fale sianginn an ṭin tikah inn ah ahohmanh an um lomi a si kho men. Kumhra fai nunphung. Ngakchia pawl cu kumhra fai an si tikah an hawile hrukaih ning, biachim ning le an tuahsernak ningin tuah le um kha an hun duh ve. Nulepa nih zeitindah an kan ruah timi nakin an hawile nih zeitindah an kan ruah timi tu kha biapi deuh ah an chiah. Thanhlaar. Chawlettu pawl nih kum upa caah si loin mino pawl caah thilri pawl kha an chuah i thanhlaar an tuah. Mah nih nulepa le fale kha pakhat le pakhat i hngalhthiam awkah a harter chin. Dr.Robert Epstein nih “kumhra fai nunphung a tlau ahcun dollar nuai tampi dih in tuahmi chawlehnak hna cu an rawk dih lai” tiah a ti.*Na fale he a ṭhami pehtlaihnak ngeih awkah i zuam.Baibal chimmi: “Nihin ah kaan pekmi bia hi na lung chungah an riak lai i na fale kha fel tein na cawnpiak hna lai i, na innchung i na ṭhut ah siseh, lam i na kal ah siseh, na ih ah siseh, na thawh ah siseh, na chimh lengmang hna lai.”—Deuteronomi 6:6,7.Na fale cu an ṭhirual pawl he hawikom an si kho ko, asinain nulepa bantukin lamhruainak tu cu an ṭhirual pawl nih an pe kho hna lai lo. Asinain na lungdong hlah: Mifim pawl nih ngakchia tam deuh le kumhra fai hna nih an nu le an pa upat le an lung lawmhter kha an duh tiah an ti. Cucaah na fale he a ṭhami pehtlaihnak na ngeih peng ahcun an ṭhirual pawl nakin an cungah huham na ngei deuh lai.“Na fale he nifatin tuahmi rawlchuan, thianhhlimhnak le inn ah tuah dingmi ca hna kha tuahṭi u. Cun game celhnak, TV asiloah video zohnak tibantuk nuamhnak hna zong kha tuahṭi u. ‘Man a ngeimi’ hawikomhnak tuah awkah sulmillam pakhat, pahnih lawng a hau tiah ruat hlah. A caan a za in nan hmanṭi lo ahcun a ṭhami pehtlaihnak nan ngei kho lai lo.”—Lorraine. An ṭhirual pawl he lawng komhter hna hlah.Baibal chimmi: “Ngakchia nih hin hruhnak thil le thil ṭhalo hi an tuah tawn phung a si.”—Phungthlukbia 22:15.Nulepa cheukhat cu an fale hawikom tampi an ngeihmi an hmuh tikah an i nuam. Asinain anmah he an kum aa khatmi hawikom tampi a ngeimi an si hmanhah nutling, patling an si khawh nakhnga anmah he an kum aa khat lomi hawikom tampi zong an ngeih a hau. A ṭhirual pawl nih mino pakhat kha a herhmi lamhruainak an pe kho lo nain dawtnak a ngeimi nulepa nih cun a ṭha bikin an pek khawh.“A ṭhirual pawl cu thil cheukhat he aa tlaiin fimnak an ngei ko lai, asinain hngalhnak, hmuhtonnak le an hawile mino pawl nih a ṭhami biakhiahnak an tuah khawh nakhnga bawmh awkah fimnak cu an ngei lo. Mino pawl nih an nu le an pa lamhruainak an zulh tikah an kum he aa tlak in nutling, patling an hung si.”—Nadia. A ṭhami lamhruainak pe hna.Baibal chimmi: “Mifim mi hna sinah i chawk ve lengmang law na fim lai.”—Phungthlukbia 13:20.An kum a upat tik hmanhah na fale cu nangmah he caan nan hmanṭinak thawngin ṭhathnemhnak an hmu lai. An caah zohchunh awk ṭha chia.“Fale caah zohchunhawk a ṭha bikmi cu nulepa an si. Nulepa dawt dingin cawnpiak a simi fale cu an upat tikah an nu le an pe he i lawh an duh.”—Katherine.Na fa cu sianginn ca zoh a huam lo, inn ah tuah dingmi ca kha a tuah lo i ca zong a ciah lo. Cucaah a mark a ṭum i a ziaza zong a hun rawk. Na fa kha a mark a ṭhat deuh nakhnga zeitindah na bawmh khawh?Hngalh awk a simiNa tuah khawhmiHneknak nih thil sining kha a chiatter chin. Na hnek tuk ahcun na fa cu sianginn le inn ah lungrethei in a um kho. A lungretheihnak a zor deuh nakhnga lih a hun chim men lai, a mark a ṭummi kha chim loin a um men lai, sianginn mark cazin ah na minthut deu kha a hman men lai asiloah sianginn hmanh a tli men lai. Cuticun thil sining cu a chia chin.Laksawng peknak nih aa ralkahmi thil a chuahter khawh. Pa pakhat a simi Andrew nih hitin a ti: “Kan fanu kha i zuam seh ti kan duh caah a mark a ṭhat deuh tikah laksawng kan pek. Mah tikah kan fanu nih laksawng hmuh ding lawng kha a hun ruah. A mark a tlawm deuh tikah a mark a tlawm caah si loin laksawng a hmuh lo ca tu ah a ngaih a chia deuh.”Saya/ Sayamah te sualphawt cu na fa caah a ṭhahnem lo. Na fa nih ka mark a ṭhat deuh nakhnga i zuam a hau lo tiah a ruah khawh men. Midang kha sual a phawt men hna lai, cun a tonmi buaibainak kha tawnghthampiak awkah midang kha a hun i bochan men hna lai. A tawinak in chim ahcun a upat tikah a biapimi rian hna kha ṭuanvo a la kho lai lo.Na intuarnak kha i uk. Na thin a hun lioah na fa he a mark kong kha i ruahceihṭi hlah u. Pa pakhat a simi Brett nih “kan lung a daih lio caan ah i ruahceihṭi cu kan nuva caah a ṭha bikmi a si” tiah a ti.Baibal phunglam: “Bia theih duhnak lei ah cun a khul a rangmi si u law biachimnak lei le thinhunnak lei ah cun a khul a nuarmi si u.”—Jeim 1:19.Buaibainak taktak kha hngalh i zuam. Midang nih nehsawhnak, sianginn i ṭhialnak, camipuai ṭihnak, chungkhar buaibainak, i hngilh khawh lonak, ṭha tein cazin ngei lonak le lungthin pek khawh lonak ti bantuk ruangah a mark a ṭummi a si men lai. A tha a thut tuk caah a si tiah ruat hlah.Baibal phunglam: “An in cawnpiakmi kha ṭha tein ruat law khuaawng na tong lai.”—Phungthlukbia 16:20.Ca zoh khawh awkah a daimi pawngkam kha timhtuahpiak. Inn ah tuah dingmi ca tuahnak le ca ciahnak caah cazin tuahpiak. Ca zohnak in na fa a lung a vaivuanhter khomi thil (TV le phone i telin) hna a um lonak hmun kha timhtuahpiak. Ca zohnak caah a caan tawite in ri khiahpiak law lungthin a pek khawh nakhnga bawm. Germany ram i pa pakhat a simi Hector nih hitin a ti: Camipuai a naih tikah camipuai ni a phanh dengmang tiang hngak loin nikhat ah tlawmpal tete in kan zohpi ṭhan.”Baibal phunglam: “Zeizong vialte caah hin caan a um cio.”—Phungchimtu 3:1.Cawn duhnak ngeih dingin thape. Na fa nih sianginn kai a ṭhatnak kong hna kha ṭha tein a hngalh ahcun cawn duhnak a ngei deuh lai. Tahchunhnak ah, kanan a thiam ahcun changreu cawknak ca tangka tuak dan a thiam lai.Baibal phunglam: “Fimnak kha cawng. Hngalhthiamnak kha cawng. ... Na lung chungah i chiah.”—Phungthlukbia 4:5, NW,8.Ruahnak cheuhnak: Inn ah tuah dingmi ca kha zohpi, asinain a ca kha nangmah nih tuahpiak hlah. Andrew nih hitin a ti: “Kan fanu nih amah thluak kha hmang loin kanmah lawngte a kan hal.” Cucaah na fa kha amah tein ca zoh ning kha cawnpiak.A um, Baibal nih Pathian a um ti fiang tein a langhtermi thil hna kha a kan chimh. Biaknak cawnpiaknak ruangah Pathian a um tiah zumh thlorh in zumh si loin “tuaktan khawhnak” le “hngalhnak” kha hmangin zumh awkah Baibal nih a kan forh. (Rom 12:1, NW; 1Johan 5:20) Baibal ah hram aa bunhmi a tanglei kong hna hi ruathmanh:  Thilnung pawl i telin van le vawlei ningcang tein ser a simi nih Sertu a um ti kha an langhter. Baibal nih hitin a ti: “Nan hngalh cio bangin inn cu mi nih an sak taktak—zeizong vialte a satu bel Pathian a si.” (Hebru 3:4) Mah ruahnak cu a sawhsawh te a si ko nain mifim tampi nih sullam a ngei tukmi a si ti kha an hngalh.*  Minung nih nunnak sullam le aa tinhnak kong kha hngalh duhnak lungput kan ngei, a hlawh a tlingmi hmanh nih mah kong kha hngalh an duh. Cutin hngalh kan duhmi cu “thlarau ah mi chambau kan si” ti kan i hngalh a si tiah Baibal nih a ti. Mah ah Pathian hngalh duhnak le biak duhnak lungput aa tel. (Matthai 5:3; Biathlam 4:11) Mah nih Pathian a um ti lawng si loin kan herhmi pek a duhmi, dawtnak a ngeimi Sertu a si ti zong a langhter.—Matthai 4:4.  Kumzabu tampi lioah rak ṭialmi Baibal chimchungbia hna cu a dikthliar in a tling. A hmaan i a neknok tiangin chimchungmi mah bia hna nih minung nakin a ṭhawng deuhmi sinin a rami an si kha fiang tein an langhter.—2Peter 1:21.  Baibal ṭialtu hna cu an chan mi hna nakin science lei fimnak an ngei. Tahchunhnak ah, hlanlio chan i mi tampi nih vui, ngal asiloah cawtum ti bantuk saram pakhatkhat nih vawlei kha a phorh tiah an zumh. Asinain Pathian nih “vawlei cu zeihmanh lo chungah a thlai” tiah Baibal nih a ti. (Job 26:7) Cu bantukin vawlei pungsan he aa tlai zongin Baibal nih “vawlei pum” tiah hmaan tein a rak langhter. (Isaiah 40:22, NW) Baibal ṭialtu hna nih cu bantuk hngalhthiamnak hna cu Pathian sinin an hmuhmi a si tiah mi tampi nih an cohlanmi cu aa tlakmi a si.  Baibal nih a harmi biahalnak tampi kha a phi a pek, cu bantuk biahalnak i a phi kha lungtling lak in an hmuh lo tikah Pathian a um lo timi zumhnak a ngeihter hna. Tahchunhnak ah: Pathian cu dawtnak a ngeimi le a ṭhawngmi a si ahcun zeicah vawleicung ah harnak le ṭhatlonak hna a um? Biaknak nih zeicah mi kha thilṭha nakin thilṭhalo a tuahter deuh hna?—Titas 1:16.Pathian nih zeizong vialte kha a hmuh khawh dih i khoika hmun paohah a duh ningin thil a tuah khawh. (Phungthlukbia 15:3; Hebru 4:13) Asinain Baibal nih Pathian cu khoika hmun paohah a um tiah a chim lo. Mah canah Pathian cu mi pakhat a si i a umnak hmun pakhat a um tiah a ti. Pathian muisam: Pathian cu thlarau pum a si. (Johan 4:24) Minung nih Pathian kha kan hmu kho lo. (Johan 1:18) Baibal tuanbia i langhnak hna ah Pathian cu hmun pakhat ah a ummi in an langhter zungzal. Pathian kha khoika hmun paohah a ummi in an langhter bal lo.—Isaiah 6:1,2; Biathlam 4:2,3,8. Pathian umnak hmun: Mit in hmuh khawh lonak thlarau pum pawl umnak hmun ah Pathian cu a um. Cuka ah Pathian “umnak hmun van” a um. (1Siangpahrang 8:30) Voikhat cu thlarau pum a ngeimi vancungmi hna cu ‘Pathian hmaiah’ an chuak tiah Baibal nih a ti caah Pathian nih umnak hmun pakhat a ngei ti kha kan hngalh.—Job 1:6.Pathian cu khoika hmun paohah a ummi a si lo ahcun pumpak pakhat cio kha a kan zohkhenh kho lai maw?Pathian nih pumpak pakhat cio kha ṭha tein a kan zohkhenh khawh. Pathian cu van ah a um ko nain a duhnak a tuahmi hna kha a hmuh hna i an ca ṭhatnak kha a tuahpiak hna. (1Siangpahrang 8:39; 2Chanrelnak 16:9) Jehovah nih lungtak tein amah a biami a zohkhenh hna ning hi ruathmanh: Thla cam tikah: Thla kan cam tikah Jehovah nih a kan ngaihpiak.—2 Chanrelnak 18:31. Lungretheih tuk tikah: “Lung a dongmi kha BAWIPA nih a umpi hna i ruahchannak a ngei lomi kha a khamh hna.”—Salm 34:18. Lamhruainak a herh tikah: Jehovah nih a bia, Baibal hmangin ‘kan zulh awk hnga lam kha a kan hmuhsak lai.’—Salm 32:8.Khoika hmun paohah a um timi kong he aa tlaiin a hmaan lomi ruahnak hnaA hmaan lomi ruahnak: Pathian cu a thil sermi khoika hmun paohah a um.A hmaanmi: Pathian cu vawleicung ah le mit in hmuh khawhnak van le vawlei i khoika hmun hmanhah a um lo. (1Siangpahrang 8:27) Arfi le a dang sermi thil hna nih ‘Pathian sunparnak fiang tein an langhter’ ti cu a hmaan ko. (Salm 19:1) Zuk suaitu pakhat cu a suaimi zuk chungah a um lo bantukin Pathian zong a sermi thil hna chungah a um lo. Zuk suaimi nih a suaitu kong a kan hngalhter khawh bantukin hmuh khawhmi sermi thil hna nih Sertu i a ṭhawnnak, a fimnak le a dawtnak ti bantuk “hmuh khawh a si lomi a sining” hna a kan hngalhter.—Rom 1:20.A hmaan lomi ruahnak: Pathian nih zeizong vialte a hngalh khawh nakhnga le a tuah khawh nakhnga khoika hmun paohah a um a hau.A hmaanmi: Pathian thiang thlarau cu zeizong vialte a tuah khotu Pathian ṭhawnnak kha a si. Pathian cu a thiang thlarau thawngin zeitik caan paoh le khoika hmun paohah a cangmi thil vialte kha a hngalh dih i a tuah khawh, cuka theng ah um a hau lo.—Salm 139:7.A hmaan lomi ruahnak: Salm 139:8 nih “vancung ah khin hung kai ning tiah, cuka ah cun na rak um ko lai, mithi khua ah khin vung it ning tiah, cuka zongah cun na rak um ṭhiamṭhiam ko lai” a ti caah Pathian cu khoika hmun paohah a um tinak a si.A hmaanmi: Mah Baibal caang nih Pathian umnak hmun kong kha a chimmi a si lo. Minung bawmh awkah Pathian caah aa hlat tuknak hmun a um lo ti kha biazai phun in a langhtermi a si.Khrihfa tampi nih Pathian cu thumkomh pathian a si tiah an cawnpiak hna. Asinain Encyclopædia Britannica timi cauk nih hitin a ti: “Biakam Thar Baibal ah Thumkomh pathian timi biafang le mah zumhnak kong a langhtermi a um lo . . . Mah zumhnak cu kumzabu tampi hnuah a hung um i bia-alnak tampi a chuahter.”Baibal ah Pathian cu Thumkomh pathian cheubang a si tiah a langhter bal lo. Mah Baibal caang hna hi zohhmanh:“Jehovah Pathian cu pakhat lawnglawng a simi Pathian a si.”—Deuteronomi 6:4, NW.“Nangmah lawnglawng hi BAWIPA [Jehovah, NW] na si le vawlei dihlak uktu Cungnung Bik na si kha hngal hna seh!”—Salm 83:18.“Cun Pathian taktak a simi nangmah hngalh le nangmah nih na thlahmi Jesuh Khrih hngalh hi zungzal nunnak cu a si.”—Johan 17:3.“Pathian cu pakhat lawng a si.”—Galati 3:20.Khrihfa tampi nih Pathian cu thumkomh pathian a si tiah zeicah an cawnpiak hna?Thiang thlarau timi cu Pathian a rian ṭuan ṭhawnnak kha a si. (Mikah 3:8; Luka 1:35) Pathian nih a duhnak tlinter awkah khoika hmun paohah a ṭhawnnak a phanhternak thawngin a thlarau kha a thlah.—Salm 104:30; 139:7.Baibal ah “thlarau” tiah lehmi biafang cu Hebru biafang ruʹach le Greek biafang pneuʹma in a rami a si. Mah biafang nih Pathian rian ṭuan ṭhawnnak asiloah thiang thlarau kha a bik in a chim duhmi a si. (Genesis 1:2) Asinain Baibal nih mah biafang kha sullam dang zong in a hman:  Thaw.—Habakkuk 2:19; Biathlam 13:15.  Thli.—Genesis 8:1; Johan 3:8.  Thilnung pawl ngeihmi nunnak thaw.—Job 34:14, 15.  Mi pakhat ngeihmi lungthin.—Nambar 14:24.  Pathian le vancungmi i telin thlarau pum a ngeimi hna.—1Siangpahrang 22:21; Johan 4:24.Mah sullam vialte nih mit in hmuh khawhmi cungah huham a ngeimi mit in hmuh khawh lomi thil kha an langhter. Cu bantukin Pathian thlarau cu “thli bantukin hmuh khawh lomi, thil a si lomi le ṭhawnnak a ngeimi” a si.—An Expository Dictionary of New Testament Words, by W. E.Vine.Baibal nih Pathian thiang thlarau kha Pathian “kut” ti zongin a langhter. (Efesa 2:10; Deuteronomi 26:8; Salm 102:25) Zungthiammi pakhat nih a rianṭuannak caah a kut le a kutdong a hman bantukin Pathian nih a tanglei i langhtermi thil sernak caah a thlarau kha a hman:  Van le vawlei.—Salm 33:6; Isaiah 66:1,2.  Baibal.—2Peter 1:20, 21.  Hlanlio a salle nih an tuahmi khuaruahhar thil le lungtho tein phung an chimnak.—Luka 4:18; Lamkaltu 1:8; 1Korin 12:4-11.  A nawl a ngaimi hna nih an langhtermi sining ṭha pawl.—Galati 5:22, 23.Thiang thlarau cu mi pakhat a si loBaibal nih Pathian thiang thlarau kha “kut,” “kutdong,” asiloah “thaw” in a langhter caah mi pakhat a si lo ti kha kan hngalh khawh. (Exodus 15:8, 10) Zungthiam mi pakhat cu a lung le a pum nih a forhfial ningin a kut nih a tuah; cu bantukin Pathian lamhruainak ning lawngin thiang thlarau nih a ṭuan ve. (Luka 11:13) Cun Baibal nih Pathian thlarau kha ti he a tahchunh i zumhnak le hngalhnak ti bantuk he zong a pehtlaihter. Mah tahchunhnak hna nih thiang thlarau cu mi pakhat a si lo ti kha an langhter.—Isaiah 44:3; Lamkaltu 6:5; 2Korin 6:6.Baibal nih Pathian min kha Jehovah tiin le a Fapa min kha Jesuh Khrih tiin a langhter nain thiang thlarau min tu cu a langhternak pakhat hmanh a um lo. (Isaiah 42:8; Luka 1:31) Khrihfa pakhat a simi Steven nih vancung langhnak ah mi pathum si loin pahnih lawng a hmuh hna. Baibal nih hitin a ti: “Thiang Thlarau in a khatmi Steven nih khan van lei khi a hun zoh i Pathian sunparnak kha a hmuh i Jesuh cu Pathian orhlei kamah a dir ko kha a hmuh.” (Lamkaltu 7:55) Steven nih Pathian rian ṭuan ṭhawnnak a simi thiang thlarau thawngin mah langhnak kha a hmuhmi a si.A hmaan lomi ruahnak: Judson Baibal i 1Johan 5:7,8 ah a langhter bantukin “Thiang Thlarau” cu mi pakhat a si i Thumkomh pathian cheubang a si.A hmaanmi: Judson Baibal i 1Johan 5:7,8 ah hitin a ti: “Vancung ah kan Pa, Bia le Thiang Thlarau tiin tehte pathum an um i an pathum in an i khat dih. Vawleicung zongah . . . tehte pathum an um i an pathum in an i khat dih.” Asinain mah bia hna cu lamkaltu Johan nih a ṭialmi an si lo ti kha Baibal lei mifim pawl nih an hun hngalh. Cucaah mah biafang hna cu a hrampi biafang an si lo. Professor Bruce M. Metzger nih hitin a ṭial: “Mah Baibal caang cu a hrampi Baibal ah aa tel lo caah Biakam Thar cauk ah telh awk a si lo.”—A Textual Commentary on the Greek New Testament.A hmaan lomi ruahnak: Thiang thlarau cu Baibal nih mi pakhat bantukin a langhter caah mi pakhat a si.A hmaanmi: Baibal nih Thiang thlarau kha a caan ah mi pakhat bantukin a langhter tawn. Tahchunhnak ah, Jesuh nih thiang thlarau kha “bawmtu” in a langhter. Mah bawmtu nih fiang tein a langhter lai, aan luhpi hna lai, aan chimh hna lai, a ka thangṭhat lai, aa lak lai tiah a ti. (Johan 16:7-15) Asinain mah bia hna ruangah thiang thlarau cu mi pakhat a si tiah chim khawh a si lo. Baibal nih fimnak, thihnak le sualnak zong kha mi pakhat bantukin a langhter. (Phungthlukbia 1:20; Rom 5:17, 21) Tahchunhnak ah, fimnak nih “tuahsernak” le “fale” a ngei i sualnak nih a lemsoi, a thah, mit thitnak hna a chuahter tiah a ti.—Matthai 11:19; Luka 7:35, NW; Rom 7:8, 11.A hmaan lomi ruahnak: Thiang thlarau min in tipil innak nih mi pakhat a si kha a langhter.A hmaanmi: Baibal nih a caan ah “min” kha nawlngeihnak langhternak caah a hman tawn. (Deuteronomi 18:5, 19-22; Esther 8:10) Mirang holh ah upadi ningin tinak caah “upadi min in” (in the name of the law) timi biafang a hman tawn. Mah nih upadi kha mi pakhat in a langhter duhnak a si lo. Cu bantukin thiang thlarau “min in” tipil in ti tikah Pathian duhnak tlinternak ah thiang thlarau i a ṭhawnnak le a dirhmun cohlan kha a si.—Matthai 28:19.A hmaan lomi ruahnak: Jesuh lamkaltu pawl le a hmasa zultu pawl nih thiang thlarau kha mi pakhat in an zumh.A hmaanmi: Baibal nih cutin a chim lo i tuanbia zongah kan hmu lo. Encyclopædia Britannica nih hitin a ti: “Thiang thlarau cu Pathian pakhat a si timi fianternak kha ... AD 381 ah tuahmi Constantinople meeting ah chuah a rak si.” Mah cu hmanung bik lamkaltu a thih hnu, kum 250 hnuah a chuakmi zumhnak a si.Jehovah cu Baibal ah langhtermi a hmaanmi Pathian, zeizong vialte a Sertu a si. (Biathlam 4:11) Jesuh bantukin profet Abraham le Moses zong nih an biakmi a si. (Genesis 24:27; Exodus 15:1, 2; Johan 20:17) Anih cu miphun pakhat i Pathian lawng si loin “vawleicung vialte” i Pathian a si.—Salm 47:2.Jehovah timi cu Baibal ah langhtermi Pathian min a si. (Exodus 3:15; Salm 83:18) Mah min cu Hebru biafang in a rami a si i “a hung si” timi sullam a ngei. Cun Baibal lei mifim tampi zong nih “A Hung Siter” timi sulllam a ngei tiah an ti. Mah fianternak cu Sertu le aa tinhnak a Tlintertu Jehovah i sining he aa tlak tukmi a si. (Isaiah 55:10, 11) Jehovah timi min hnulei ah a ummi a sining, a hleiin a lang bikmi dawtnak kha hngalh awkah Baibal nih a kan bawmh.—Exodus 34:5-7; Luka 6:35; 1Johan 4:8.Jehovah timi min cu Hebru biafang pali יהוה (YHWH) in lehmi Mirang holh a si. Mah kha Tetragrammaton ti zongin hngalh a si. Hlanlio Hebru holh in Pathian min kha zeitindah aw chuah a si ti cu hngalh a si lo. Asinain “Jehovah” timi biafang cu hlanliopi in Mirang holh ah hman a si. 1530 ah chuahmi William Tyndale lehmi Baibal ah a hmasa bik hmuh a rak si.*Hlanlio Hebru holh in Pathian min aw chuah ning kha zeicah hngalh a si lo?Hlanlio Hebru ca an ṭial tikah cafang aw kha hmang loin cafang tung lawngin an rak ṭial. Hebru holh a hmangmi hna nih ca an rel tikah aa tlakmi cafang aw kha hmangin fawi tein an rel khawh. Asinain Hebru Baibal (“Biakam Hlun”) ṭial dih a si hnuah Judah mi cheukhat nih Pathian min aw chuah in auh cu a palh timi a hmaan lomi zumhnak kha an cohlan. Pathian min aa telmi Baibal caang an rel tikah “Bawipa” asiloah “Pathian” ti bantuk min in an airolh. Kumzabu tampi a rauh tikah mah a hmaan lomi zumhnak cu a karh i hlanlio aw chuah ning zong a tlau.*Mi cheukhat nih Pathian min cu “Yahweh” tiin aw chuah awk a si tiah an ruah. Cheukhat nih phun dang in an ruah ve. A hmasa Greek caṭialtu hna zong nih Iae, I·a·beʹ le I·a·ou·eʹ tiin aw chuah ding a si tiah an ti nain hlanlio Hebru aw chuah ning taktak cu ahohmanh nih an hngal lo.*Pathian min kong he aa tlaiin a hmaan lomi ruahnakA Hmaan Lomi Ruahnak: “Jehovah” timi min a hmangmi Baibal lettu hna nih mah min kha an chapmi a si.A Hmaanmi: Pathian min caah hmanmi Hebru biafang Tetragrammaton cu Baibal ah 7,000 hrawng aa tel.* Baibal lehnak tam deuh ah Pathian min kha an hloh i “Bawipa” ti bantuk upatnak min in an thlen.A Hmaan Lomi Ruahnak: Lianngan Bik Pathian caah min ngeih a herh lo.A Hmaanmi: Pathian theng nih a min kha Baibal ah voi thong tampi ṭial dingin Baibal ṭialtu pawl kha a fial hna. Cun amah a biami hna kha a min hman dingin a fial hna. (Isaiah 42:8; Joel 2:32; Malakhi 3:16; Rom 10:13) Mi nih Pathian min an philh nakhnga aa zuammi profet deu pawl kha Pathian nih a mawhchiat hna.—Jeremiah 23:27.A Hmaan Lomi Ruahnak: Judah mi hna phunglam ningin cun Pathian min kha Baibal in hloh awk a si.A Hmaanmi: Judah mi Baibal tlengtu cheukhat nih Pathian min kha aw chuah in an hmang lo ti cu a hmaan ko. Asinain Pathian min kha Baibal in cun an hlo lo. Zeitin a si hmanhah Pathian nih a nawlbia he aa ralkahmi minung phunglam zulh ding kha a kan duhpiak lo.—Matthai 15:1-3.A Hmaan Lomi Ruahnak: Hebru holh in Pathian min aw chuah a hmaanmi kha fiang tein hngalh a si lo caah Baibal ah telh awk a si lo.A Hmaanmi: Cutin a si ahcun Pathian nih holh a phunphun a hmangmi hna kha a min an auh tikah aw chuah ning phunkhat lawng hman dingin a kan halmi bantuk a si lai. Asinain holh a phunphun a hmangmi hlanlio amah a biami hna nih min pawl kha aw a phunphun in an rak chuah ti kha Baibal nih a langhter.Tahchunhnak ah, Israel mi biaceihtu a simi Joshua kong hi ruathmanh. Kumzabu pakhatnak i Hebru holh a hmangmi Khrihfa hna nih a min kha Yehoh·shuʹaʽ tiah aw an chuah i Greek holh a hmangmi hna nih I·e·sousʹ tiah aw an chuah. Baibal ah Joshua i Hebru a min kha Greek aw chuah ningin ṭial a si. Cucaah Khrihfa hna nih min pawl kha anmahle holh aw chuah cio in an rak hman ti kha mah nih a langhter.—Lamkaltu 7:45; Hebru 4:8.Pathian min holh an leh tik zongah cutin a si ve. Pathian min aw chuah a hmaanmi hngalh nakin Baibal ah Pathian min kha amahle a umnak zawn ah chiah cu a biapi deuh tukmi a si.Pathian nih pumpak min pakhat lawng a ngei. Mah cu Hebru ca in יהוה tiah ṭial a si i Hakha in “Jehovah” tiah an leh tawn.* Pathian nih a profet Isaiah hmangin hitin a ti: “Keimah cu Jehovah ka si. Cucu ka min a si.” (Isaiah 42:8, BAIBAL CATHIANG) Hlanlio kut in ṭialmi Baibal ah mah min cu voi 7,000 hrawng hmuh khawh a si i Pathian caah hmanmi a dang biafang nakin le midang min nakin tam deuh hmuh khawh a si.*Jehovah nih min dang tah a ngei maw?Baibal nih Pathian i pumpak min kha pakhat lawng a langhter nain upatnak min le a sining a langhtermi min tampi a hman. A tanglei i langhtermi upatnak min hna nih Jehovah i a sining le a thilti khawhnak hna kha an langhter.Upatnak minCherhchanmiA sullamAllah(A um lo)Arabic holh in a rami “Allah” timi biafang cu pumpak min si loin “Pathian” ti sullam a ngeimi upatnak min a si. Arabic le a dang holh in lehmi Baibal hna ah Pathian caah “Allah” timi biafang kha an hman.Lianngan BikGenesis 17:1Ahohmanh nih tluk khawh lomi ṭhawnnak a ngei. “Lianngan Bik Pathian” ti sullam a ngeimi Hebru biafang ʼEl Shad·daiʹ kha Baibal ah voi sarih hmuh khawh a si.Alfa le OmegaBiathlam 1:8; 21:6; 22:13“Hmasa bik le hmanung bik” asiloah “hramthawknak le a donghnak” timi sullam cu Jehovah hlanah Lianngan Bik Pathian ahohmanh an um lo i amah hnu zongah ahohmanh an um lai lo tinak a si. (Isaiah 43:10) Alfa le omega cu Greek cafang i a hramthawknak le a donghnak a si.Zungzal in a nungmiDaniel 7:9, 13, 22Pathian cu hramthawknak a ngei lo; ahohmanh asiloah zeithil hmanh an um hlanin a um cangmi a si.—Salm 90:2.PaMatthai 6:9Nunnak petu a si.PathianGenesis 1:1Biak awkah aa tlakmi, a ṭhawngmi a si. ʼElo·himʹ timi Hebru biafang cu a tammi caah hmanmi a si i Jehovah lianngannak, sunparnak le a ṭha bik a sinak kha a langhter.Pathian hna PathianDeuteronomi 10:17Mi cheukhat nih an biakmi “santlai lomi pathian hna” he i ralkah in Jehovah cu a sang bikmi Pathian a si.—Isaiah 2:8, Vawlei Thar Lehnak Baibal.A Ṭha Bik CawnpiaktuIsaiah 30:20, 21A ṭha bikmi cawnpiaknak le lamhruainak petu a si.—Isaiah 48:17, 18.SertuIsaiah 40:28; Salm 149:2Amah nih zeizong vialte kha a ser hna.—Biathlam 4:11.Aa Nuammi Pathian1Timote 1:11, Vawlei Thar Lehnak BaibalAa nuammi le lung aa lawmmi Pathian a si.—Salm 104:31.Thlacamnak a ngaituSalm 65:1Zumhnak he a sinah thla a cammi pumpak pakhat cio i an thlacamnak kha a ngaih.Keimah Cu Keimah Ka Si KoExodus 3:14Aa tinhnak tlinter awkah a herhmi zeipoah a hung si kho. Mah bia kha “Ka Duhmi Zeipoah Ka Hung Si Lai” asiloah “Siter Ka Duhmi Ningin Ka Hung Si Lai” ti zongin an leh. (J.B. Rotherham lehmi The Emphasised Bible; Vawlei Thar Lehnak Baibal) Mah cu a changtu cacaang ah aa telmi Pathian i pumpak min Jehovah a sullam a si.—Exodus 3:15, BAIBAL CATHIANG.NahchuakExodus 34:14Amah lawng biak a duhmi a si. Mah bia kha “a dang pathian biak a duh lomi” tiin le “amah lawng biak dingin a halmi” ti zongin an leh.—God’s Word Bible; Vawlei Thar Lehnak Baibal.Zungzal siangpahrang1 Timote 1:17A uknak cu hramthawknak asiloah donghnak a ngei lo.BawipaSalm 135:5A ngeitu asiloah uktu a si; Hebru biafang ʼA·dhohnʹ le ʼAdho·nimʹ a si.Cungnung BikSalm 47:2A sang bikmi dirhmun a ngeimi a si.A Thiang BikmiPhungthlukbia 9:10 Aho nak hmanhin a thiang (ziazalei ah a thiangmi) deuhmi a si.Um SertuIsaiah 64:8Um Sertu nih tlak cungah nawl a ngeih bantukin Pathian cu pakhat cio le miphun vialte hna cungah nawl a ngeimi a si.—Rom 9:20, 21.Tlanhnak Man A PetuIsaiah 41:14; King James VersionTlanhnak man timi cu thil pakhatkhat cawk ṭhan awkah asiloah thil pakhatkhat i a man caah pekmi kha a si. Sualnak le thihnak in kan luat nakhnga Pathian nih Jesuh Khrih tlanhnak man kha a pek.—Johan 3:16.LungpiSalm 18:2, 46Pathian cu kan dornak le khamhnak hrampi a si.KhamhtuIsaiah 45:21Harnak asiloah rawhnak in a kan khamh.TuukhalSalm 23:1Amah a biami kha a zohkhenh hna.Hebru Baibal chung i a ummi hmun minBaibal i a ummi hmun cheukhat hna min ah Pathian i pumpak min aa tel, asinain mah cu Pathian caah airolh in hmanmi min a si lo.Hmun minCherhchanmiA sullamJehovah-jirehGenesis 22:13, 14“Jehovah Nih A Khan Ko.”Jehovah-nissiExodus 17:15“Jehovah Cu Ka Hmelchunhnak Puanzar A Si.” Jehovah cu a miphun a huppheng khotu le a bawm khotu Pathian a si.—Exodus 17:13-16.Jehovah-shalomBiaceihtu 6:23, 24“Jehovah Cu Daihnak A Si.”Jehovah-shammahEzekiel 48:35“Jehovah cu khika ah a um.”Patian min hngalh awk le hman awk a sinak a ruang  Pathian nih Baibal ah a min kha voi thong tampi a telhnak thawngin pumpak a min Jehovah kha biapi ah a chiah.—Malakhi 1:11.  Pathian Fapa Jesuh nih Pathian min a biapitnak kha atu le atu a rak langhter. Tahchunhnak ah, Jehovah sinah hitin thla a cam: “Na min thiang cu upat si ko seh.”—Matthai 6:9; Johan 17:6.  Pathian min a hung hngal i a hmangmi cu Jehovah he pehtlaihnak ṭha ngeih awkah ke an hlanmi a si. (Salm 9:10; Malakhi 3:16) Cu bantuk pehtlaihnak nih mah Pathian biakam in ṭhatnak a hmuhter hna: “A ka dawmi cu ka khamh hna lai i [ka min] a ka hngalmi cu ka huhphenh hna lai.”—Salm 91:14.  Baibal chimmi: “Vancung ah siseh, vawleicung ah siseh pathian timi cu a um zong an um ko lai, cun pathian timi hna hi le bawipa timi hna hi tampi zong an si ko lai.” (1Korin 8:5,6) Asinain a hmaanmi Pathian i a min cu Jehovah a si ti cu a fiang ko.—Salm 83:18, Vawlei Thar Lehnak Baibal.A si lo. Kum thong tampi chung Baibal kha a rawh a fawimi thilri hna hmangin an rak tlen thluahmah ko nain hlanlio kut in ṭialmi Baibal he tahchunh tikah a hrampi biatak cu aa thleng lo.Hlanlio kut in ṭialmi Baibal thong tampi hmuh a si. Mah ah aa lawh lonak cheukhat a um caah an tlen tikah an palhnak a um ti cu a fiang ko. Aa lawh lonak cu tlawmpal lawng a si i a sullam cu aa thleng lo. Biatak tein aa dannak cheukhat cu Baibal biatak merh a duhmi Baibal tlengtu cheukhat nih hramhram in an telh chihmi bia hna ruangah a si. Tahchunhnak pahnih in zoh hna hmanh u sih: Kuatkhat Johan 5:7 kha hlanlio Baibal lettu cheukhat nih hitin an leh: “Vancung ah kan Pa, Bia le Thiang Thlarau tiin tehte pathum an um i an pathum in an i khat dih.” Asinain zumh awk tlakmi kut in ṭialmi ca he tahchunh tikah mah bia cu a hrampi Baibal ah aa tel lo ti kha kan hngalh. Mah bia cu a hnuah an bet chommi a si.* Cucaah tuchan i zumh awk tlakmi Baibal lehnak hna ahcun an telh ti lo.               Pathian pumpak a min kha hlanlio kut in ṭialmi Baibal ah voi thong tampi aa tel. Asinain Baibal lehnak tampi nih Pathian min canah “Bawipa” asiloah “Pathian” ti bantukin an airolh.Atu ah kut in ṭialmi Baibal tampi an hmuh cang caah palhnak a um maw, um lo ti kha a hlan nakin kawl awkah a fawi deuh cang.* Mah ca hna le atu kan hmanmi Baibal tahchunh tikah Baibal a hmaannak kong he aa tlaiin zeidah kan hngalh?  Hebru Baibal (“Biakam Hlun” tiah auhmi) kong he aa tlaiin Baibal lei mifim William H. Green nih hitin a ti: “Baibal bantukin a hmaan ning tein tlenmi hlanlio kut in ṭialmi ca a um lo tiah ka chim ngam.”  Khrihfa Greek Baibal asiloah “Biakam Thar” kong he aa tlaiin Baibal lei mifim F.F.Bruce nih hitin a ṭial: “Biakam Thar Baibal cu Greek le Rom caṭialtu hna an ca nakin a let tampi in a hmaan deuh. Asinain Greek le Rom ca a hmaannak kong he aa tlaiin ahohmanh nih alnak an tuah lo.”  Kut in ṭialmi Baibal kong ṭha tein a hngalmi, a min a thangmi mifim Sir Frederic Kenyon nih hitin a ti: “Baibal kha kut ah i tlaih in mah hi kumzabu tampi chung chankhat hnu chankhat a biapimi a kong tlau loin mi sin a phan khomi Pathian Bia biatak a si tiah ahopaoh nih ralṭha tein an chim khawh.”Pathian miphun nih an tuahmi sualnak ngan kong kha Judah mi le Khrihfa Baibal tlengtu hna nih hmaan tein an rak tlen.* (Nambar 20:12; 2Samuel 11:2-4; Galati 2:11-14) Cu bantukin Judah mi hna nawl an ngaih lo ruangah mawhchiat an sinak kong le minung ruahnak kong a langhtermi Baibal caang hna zong a hmaan ning tein an rak tlen. (Hosea 4:2; Malakhi 2:8,9; Matthai 23:8,9; 1Johan 5:21) Mah kong hna a hmaan ning tein an tlenmi nih Baibal tlengtu hna cu zumh awk a tlakmi le Pathian Bia a sunsakmi an si ti kha a lang.  A hramthawk tein Baibal kha a thiang thlarau thawngin a ṭialtertu Pathian nih Baibal a hmaannak kha a kilven peng lai a si ko lo maw?* (Isaiah 40:8; 1Peter 1:24, 25) Pathian nih hlanlio i minung pawl lawng si loin atu chan i mi zong nih Baibal in ṭhatnak hmu hna seh ti a duh. (1Korin 10:11) “Cathiang nih lungsaunak le lungthin ṭhawnnak a kan pekmi thawngin ruahchannak kha kan ngeih khawh nakhnga Cathiang chung i aa ṭialmi vialte cu kanmah cawnpiaknak caah a si.”—Rom 15:4.  Jesuh le a zultu hna nih Hebru Baibal kut in ṭialmi ca hna kha zumhnak he an cherhchan.—Luka 4:16-21; Lamkaltu 17:1-3.Aa tlak. Baibal cu science cauk a si lo nain science lei kongkau he aa tlaiin a chimmi cu a hmaan. Science fimnak le Baibal aa tlaknak kong, Baibal ṭial a si lioah a nungmi mi tampi zumhnak cu Baibal ah aa telmi science lei kongkau he aa dang ti a langhtermi tahchunhnak hna kha zohhmanh.  Van le vawlei cu hramthawknak an ngei. (Genesis 1:1) Hlanlio tuanbia tampi nih van le vawlei cu sermi an si lo i ningcang loin a rak chuakmi an si tiah an ti. Babilon mi nih rilipi pahnih in a chuakmi pathian hna nih van le vawlei kha an ser tiah an zumh. A dang tuanbia hna nih van le vawlei cu a nganpimi ti (egg) pakhat chungin a chuakmi a si tiah an ti.  Van le vawlei cu khuazing pawl nih si loin kokek phunglam nih a ukmi a si. (Job 38:33; Jeremiah 33:25) Vawlei pumpi i tuanbia tampi nih minung cu khuazing pawl sersiam ningin an um i a caan ah zaangfahnak ngei loin pehtlaihnak hna an tong tiah an ti.  Vawlei cu zeihmanh lo cungah thlai a si. (Job 26:7) Hlanlio mi tampi nih vawlei cu a per i naa asiloah chungkuh ti bantuk saram asiloah mikei nganpi pakhat nih a phorh tiah an zumh.  Rilipi le kaa dangdang in ti cu a khu ah an kai i ruah, dap le rial ti bantukin vawlei ah an tla ṭhan. Cun mah ti hna cu tiva le tidil hna ah an luang. (Job 36:27, 28; Phungchimtu 1:7; Isaiah 55:10; Amos 9:6) Hlanlio Greek mi hna nih vawlei tang i rilipi ti hna cu tiva lei ah an luang tiah an zumh i mah zumhnak kha kumzabu 18 tiang an cohlan.  Tuchan i tlang hna cu hlanlio i rilipi tang ah a rak ummi an si. (Salm 104:6,8) Khuazing hna nih tlang pawl kha atu pungsan ningin an sermi a si tiah an chim tawn.  Thiannak nih ngandamnak kha a huhphenh. Hlanlio Israel mi pek an simi Nawlbia ah mithi ruak tawngh hnuah i kholhnak, chawnh khawhmi zawtnak a ngeimi a dang tein chiahnak le minung ek ningcang tein hlonhnak timi phunglam hna aa tel. (Levitikas 11:28; 13:1-5; Deuteronomi 23:13) Asinain mah lioah Izipt mi nih an hmanmi, hma ah thuhmi sii phunkhat cu minung ek in sermi a si.Baibal ṭha tein hlathlai tikah a um lo ti kha kan hmuh khawh. Mah kong he aa tlaiin mi tampi nih a hmaan loin an ruahmi a kong cheukhat hi ruathmanh:A Hmaan Lomi: Baibal nih van le vawlei cu suimilam 24 a ummi, niruk chungah ser a si tiah a ti.A Hmaanmi: Pathian nih van le vawlei hi zeitik ah dah ser hram a thawk ti kha Baibal nih a chim lo. (Genesis 1:1) Cun Genesis dal 1nak i sernak ni hna cu zei can dah an rauh ti fiang tein langhter lomi caan hna kha an si. A tak ti ahcun van le vawlei ser an si caan kha “ni” tiah a auh.—Genesis 2:4, NW.A Hmaan Lomi: Ceunak in rawl a chuahtermi nika ser a si hlanah thingram pawl ser hmasa an si tiah Baibal nih a ti.—Genesis 1:11, 16.A Hmaanmi: Vancung ah a ummi, arfi phunkhat a simi nika cu thingram pawl hlanah ser hmasa a si ti kha Baibal nih a langhter. (Genesis 1:1) Sernak nikhatnak “ni” asiloah caan chungah ni dat cu vawleicung ah a rak phan. Sernak nithumnak “ni” ah vawlei tuamtu thli thenh a si tikah ceunak in rawl chuahternak caah a zami nika ceunak kha vawlei nih a hmuh. (Genesis 1:3-5, 12, 13) Mah hnu lawngah vawlei in nika kha fiang tein hmuh khawh a si.—Genesis 1:16.A Hmaan Lomi: Nika nih vawlei a hel tiah Baibal nih a ti.A Hmaanmi: Phungchimtu 1:5 nih hitin a ti: “Ni cu a chuah kel in a chuak ṭhiamṭhiam ko, a tlak ningin a tla ṭhiamṭhiam ko; A chuahnak hmun ah khan a hram in i thawk ṭhan awkah a kir ṭhan lengmang ko.” Asinain mah bia cu vawlei in nika a cawlcangh ning kan hmuhnak lawng kha a langhtermi a si. Tuchan hmanhah vawlei nih nika a hel ti kha mi nih an hngalh ko nain “nichuah” le “nitlak” timi biafang kha an hman ṭhiamṭhiam.A Hmaan Lomi: Baibal nih vawlei cu a per tiah a ti.A Hmaanmi: “Vawlei ki li” timi biafang nih vawlei cu ki pali a ngei tiah a ti duhnak a si lo. Mah biafang kan rel tikah vawlei pumpi kha a chim duhmi a si ti kha kan hngalhthiam.—Isaiah 11:12; Luka 13:29.Baibal nih vawlei cu a per tiah a kan cawnpiak lo.* Baibal cu science lei cauk a si lo. Asinain science fimnak he aa kalhnak a um lo. Baibal chimmi cu “zungzal in an hmun.”—Salm 111:8.Baibal nih “vawlei ki li” a ti tikah zei sullam dah a ngeih?Satan nih Jesuh a tukforhnak he aa tlaiin tah zeitin?Baibal ah hmanmi “vawlei ki li” le “vawlei kil kip” timi biafang kha a ca ningin lak khawh a si lo, cutin lak a si ahcun vawlei cu ki li a ummi asiloah a donghnak a ummi bantuk a si lai. (Isaiah 11:12; Job 37:3) Mah bia cu vawlei pumpi dihlak kha langhternak caah hmanmi a si. Nichuah, nitlak, chaklei, thlanglei tiin hmun li caah a hman duhmi a si.—Luka 13:29. “Ki li” asiloah “kil kip” tiah lehmi Hebru biafang cu “a deng” timi biafang cungah i hngat dawh a si. Cauk pakhat nih [The International Standard Bible Encyclopedia] “va pakhat i a thla cu a fale khuhnak ah a hman caah [mah Hebru biafang] aa samh khawhnak dihlak kha a chim duhmi a si” tiah a ti. Job 37:3 le Isaiah 11:12 i hmanmi “biafang nih rilikam, ramri asiloah vawleicung pumpi kha a chim duhmi a si” ti zongin a ti.*Jesuh tukforh awkah “Khuachia nih cun Jesuh cu tlang sang ngaingaimi pakhat ah a kalpi i vawleicung peng le ram vialte le an sunparnak vialte kha a hmuhsak dih.” (Matthai 4:8) Mah Baibal kong nih hmun pakhat in vawlei pumpi hmuh khawh a si timi langhternak nih vawlei a per tiah a kan cawnpiak tiin mi cheukhat nih an ti. Mah Baibal caang i “tlang sang ngaingaimi” timi cu a um taktakmi si loin langhternak si dawh a si. Cutin biachahnak tuah a sinak a ruang kha zoh hna u sih.  Vawleicung pennak vialte hmunkhat ah hmuh khawh a sinak tlang cu hi vawlei ah a um lo.  Satan nih Jesuh kha pennak lawng si loin “an sunparnak” zong a hmuhsak. Cu bantuk thil hna cu lam hlat in hmuh khawh a si lo, cucaah Satan nih langhnak phun pakhatkhat hmangin Jesuh kha a hmuhsakmi si dawh a si. Mah cu projector le screen hmangin vawleicung hmun a phunphun i hmanthlak hna hmuhsak bantuk khi a si kho men.  Mah kong a langhter vemi Luka 4:5 nih Satan nih Jesuh cu “chikkhatte ah khin vawleicung ram vialte kha a hmuhsak dih” tiah a ti. Minung mit in vawleicung ram vialte kha chikkhat ah zoh khawh ti cu a si kho lomi a si. Cucaah Satan nih lam pakhatkhat hmangin Jesuh kha a tukforh tiah ti khawh a si.A langhter. Jesuh nih vawleicung a um lioah “vawlei Khamhtu” a si hngami “Pathian thimmi bawi,” Messiah kong chimchungbia tampi kha a rak tlinter. (Daniel 9:25; 1Johan 4:14) A thih hnu hmanhah Messiah kong he aa tlaimi chimchungbia hna kha a tlinter rih.—Salm 110:1; Lamkaltu 2:34-36.“Messiah” timi cu zei sullam dah a si?Messiah kong chimchungbia hna kha mi pakhat nak tam nih an tlinter kho maw?Messiah cu hmailei ah a lang dingmi a si maw?Baibal ah Messiah kong chimchungbia pa zeizat dah a um?Jesuh thawngin a tling cangmi Messiah kong chimchungbia cheukhatHebru biafang Ma·shiʹach (Messiah) le mah he aa lomi Greek biafang Khri·stos (Khrih) cu “Chiti Thuhmi” ti sullam a ngei. Cucaah “Jesuh Khrih” timi cu “Chiti Thuhmi Jesuh” asiloah “Messiah Jesuh” tinak a si.Baibal chan ah mi pakhat cu a hleikhunmi nawlngeihnak pek a si tikah a lu ah chiti thiang an toihnak thawngin chiti thuh a si. (Levitikas 8:12; 1Samuel 16:13) Jesuh cu Pathian nih Messiah in a sangmi nawlngeihnak a pek. (Lamkaltu 2:36) Asinain Pathian nih Jesuh kha chiti taktak in si loin thiang thlarau in chiti a thuh.—Matthai 3:16.An tlinter kho lo. Siapi neh pakhat nih mi pakhat lawng a aiawh bantukin Baibal chimchungbia hna nih Messiah asiloah Khrih pakhat lawng kha a aiawh. Asinain Baibal nih “nal messiah le nal profet kha an chuak lai i Pathian mithim pawl hlen kha a si kho dingmi thil a si ahcun cu hna hlen khawhnak ding caah cun hmelchunhnak le khuaruahhar nganngan kha an ser hna lai” tiah ralrin a kan pek.—Matthai 24:24.A si lo. Baibal nih Messiah cu Israel Siangpahrang David tefa a si lai tiah a chimchung. (Salm 89:3,4) Asinain Judah pupa hna cazin cu a rak tlau, mah cu AD 70 ah Rom nih Jerusalem an hrawh lioah a rawkmi a si kho men.* Mah caan thawkin anih cu Siangpahrang David tefa a si tiin ahohmanh nih an langhter kho lo. Asinain Jesuh chan ah mah pupa hna cazin cu a um rih caah David tefa a si ti kha a ral pawl hmanh nih an al ngam lo.—Matthai 22:41-46.Messiah kong chimchungbia pa zeizat dah a um ti cu fiang tein kan chim kho lo. Tahchunhnak ah, chimchungbia kong an rel ning cu aa lo lo. Isaiah 53:2-7 ah Messiah kong chimchungbia tampi a um. Mi cheukhat nih mah Baibal dihlak kha chimchungbia pakhat in an rel i cheukhat nih cun chimchungbia pakhat cio kha a dangdang in an rel.ChimchungbiaA UmnakA TlinnakAbraham TefaGenesis 22:17, 18Matthai 1:1Abraham fapa Isak tefaGenesis 17:19Matthai 1:2Israel mi, Judah hrinsorGenesis 49:10Matthai 1:1,3Siangpahrang David hrinsorIsaiah 9:7Matthai 1:1Ngaknu thiang chungin a chuakIsaiah 7:14Matthai 1:18, 22, 23Bethlehem khua ah a chuakMikah 5:2Matthai 2:1, 5,6Immanuel* tiah auh a siIsaiah 7:14Matthai 1:21-23A nautami sining in aa thawkIsaiah 53:2Luka 2:7A chuah hnuah ngakchia pawl cu thah an siJeremiah 31:15Matthai 2:16-18Izipt ah kalpi a siHosea 11:1Matthai 2:13-15Nazareth* khua mi tiah auh a siIsaiah 11:1Matthai 2:23A hmaiah lamkal thlah a siMalakhi 3:1Matthai 11:7-10AD 29*ah Messiah in chiti thuh a siDaniel 9:25Matthai 3:13-17Pathian nih a Fapa in a thanhSalm 2:7Lamkaltu 13:33, 34Pathian inn caah lungthawhnak a ngeiSalm 69:9Johan 2:13-17Thawngṭha thanhtu a siIsaiah 61:1Luka 4:16-21Galili ram ah ceunak nganpi a tlungIsaiah 9:1,2Matthai 4:13-16Moses bantukin khuaruahhar thil a tuahDeuteronomi 18:15Lamkaltu 2:22Moses bantukin Pathian bia a chimDeuteronomi 18:18, 19Johan 12:49Mizaw tampi kha a damter hnaIsaiah 53:4Matthai 8:16, 17Mi nih biapi ah an chiah nakhnga aa zuam loIsaiah 42:2Matthai 12:17, 19Namnehmi hna cungah zaangfahnak a langhterIsaiah 42:3Matthai 12:9-20; Marka 6:34Pathian dinnak kha a langhterIsaiah 42:1,4Matthai 12:17-20A Ṭha Bikmi Ruahnak CheutuIsaiah 9:6,7Johan 6:68Jehovah min a thanhSalm 22:22, NWJohan 17:6Tahchunhnak hmangin a chimSalm 78:2Matthai 13:34, 35HruaituDaniel 9:25Matthai 23:10Mi tampi nih an zum loIsaiah 53:1Johan 12:37, 38Tlukrilhtertu lungIsaiah 8:14, 15Matthai 21:42-44Mi nih an hlawtSalm 118:22, 23Lamkaltu 4:10, 11A ruang um loin an huatSalm 69:4Johan 15:24, 25Jerusalem khua ah laa i cit in teinak he a lutZekhariah 9:9Matthai 21:4-9Ngakchia nih an thangṭhatSalm 8:2Matthai 21:15, 16Jehovah min in a raSalm 118:26Johan 12:12, 13A zumhmi a hawikom pakhat nih a rawiSalm 41:9Johan 13:18Ngun tangka 30 in rawi a si*Zekhariah 11:12, 13Matthai 26:14-16; 27:3-10A hawile nih an zamtak Zekhariah 13:7Matthai 26:31, 56A hmaan loin sual an puhSalm 35:11Matthai 26:59-61Sual a puhtu hna hmaiah dai tein a umIsaiah 53:7Matthai 27:12-14Cil an chakIsaiah 50:6Matthai 26:67; 27:27, 30A lu ah fung in an tukMikah 5:1Marka 15:19Hrihrual in an tukIsaiah 50:6Johan 19:1A hremtu hna kha a lehrulh hna loIsaiah 50:6Johan 18:22, 23Cozah nawlngeitu hna nih rawi awkah khua an khanSalm 2:2Luka 23:10-12A kut le a ke kha thir an khenhSalm 22:16Matthai 27:35; Johan 20:25A puan caah voihfung an zuhSalm 22:18Johan 19:23, 24Misual mi hna he rel chih a siIsaiah 53:12Matthai 27:38Serhsat le volhpamh a siSalm 22:7,8Matthai 27:39-43Misual mi hna caah fahnak a inIsaiah 53:5,61Peter 2:23-25Pathian hlawtmi a loSalm 22:1Marka 15:34Mitsur hang hnitkha he cawhmi kha an pek Salm 69:21Matthai 27:34A thih hlanah a ti a halSalm 22:15Johan 19:28, 29A thlarau kha Pathian sinah a chiahSalm 31:5Luka 23:46A nunnak a pekIsaiah 53:12Marka 15:37Sualnak hloh awkah tlanhnak man a pekIsaiah 53:12Matthai 20:28A ruh khiah a si loSalm 34:20Johan 19:31-33, 36Chunh a siZekhariah 12:10Johan 19:33-35, 37Mirum mi hna sinah vui a siIsaiah 53:9Matthai 27:57-60Thihnak in thawhter a siSalm 16:10Lamkaltu 2:29-31Rawitu zaka ah midang an airolhSalm 109:8Lamkaltu 1:15-20Pathian orhlei kam ah a ṭhuSalm 110:1Lamkaltu 2:34-36Armageddon raldohnak timi cu minung cozah le Pathian karah a ummi hmanung bik raldohnak kha a si. Minung cozah le an sin i a ṭangmi hna nih Pathian uknak an cohlan lonak thawngin atu hmanhin Pathian kha an ralchanh. (Salm 2:2) Armageddon raldohnak nih minung uknak kha a donghter cang lai.—Daniel 2:44.“Armageddon” timi biafang kha Baibal ah Biathlam 16:16 ah voikhat lawng hmuh a si. “Vawleicung siangpahrang vialte” cu “Lianngan Bik Pathian ni lianngan ni ah” pakhat le pakhat i doh dingin hmunkhat ah an i pum. “Cu hmun cu Hebru holh in Armageddon ti a si.”—Biathlam 16:14.Armageddon ah ahote dah aa do lai? Jesuh Khrih nih vancung ralkapbu kha a hruai hna lai i Pathian ral pawl kha a hrawh dih hna lai. (Biathlam 19:11-16, 19-21) Mah ral lakah Pathian nawlngeihnak a ralchanhmi le Pathian zei i a rel lomi an i tel.—Ezekiel 39:7.Armageddon raldohnak cu Nichuah Laifang ah a si lai maw? A si lai lo. Armageddon raldohnak cu hmun pakhat lawngah si loin vawleicung pumpi ah a tlung dingmi a si.—Jeremiah 25:32-34; Ezekiel 39:17-20.A caan ah “Har–Magedon” (Hebrew Har Meghiddohnʹ) tiah lehmi Armageddon timi cu “Megiddo Tlang” ti sullam a ngei. Megiddo khua cu hlanlio Israel ram i khua pakhat a si. Mah khua pawngah teinak le sunghnak a hliahmi raldohnak hna a rak um ti kha tuanbia nih an langhter. Baibal ah hmuhmi raldohnak cheukhat zong cuka ah a rak si. (Biaceihtu 5:19, 20; 2Siangpahrang 9:27; 23:29) Asinain Armageddon raldohnak cu hlanlio Megiddo khua pawngkam ah a si lai lo. Cuka ah a ngan i a rawnmi tlang a um lo. Pathian a domi ral vialte an i pumh ahcun Jezreel Nelrawn tiang hmanhah an i tlum lai lo. Cucaah Armageddon timi cu Pathian uknak kha hmanung bik tiang ralchanh dingin miphun pawl an i pumhmi vawlei thil sining kha a si.Armageddon raldohnak ah zeidah a cang lai? Pathian nih a ṭhawnnak zeitindah a hman lai ti kha kan hngal lo. Asinain hlanah a rak hmanmi hriamnam pawl kha Armageddon zongah a herh ningin a hman khawh. Mah hriamnam hna lakah—rial, lihnin, tilian, mei le kat, ṭek le zawtnak hna an i tel. (Job 38:22, 23; Ezekiel 38:19, 22; Habakkuk 3:10, 11; Zekhariah 14:12) Pathian ral pawl cu anmahle anmah i tuai-ur in an i that lai. Asinain anmah a dotu taktak cu Jehovah Pathian a si kha a donghnak ah an hngalh lai.—Ezekiel 38:21, 23; Zekhariah 14:13.Armageddon raldohnak ruangah vawlei hi a rawk dih lai maw? Hi vawlei cu minung nih zungzal in an umnak ding hmun a si caah a rawk lai lo. (Salm 37:29; 96:10; Phungchimtu 1:4) Armageddon raldohnak ah mi vialte cu an thi dih lai lo. Pathian salle a simi “mibu nganpi” cu a nung in an luat lai.—Biathlam 7:9, 14; Salm 37:34.Asinain Baibal nih “vawlei” timi biafang kha hi vawlei taktak ca i a hman lengah a caan ah Pathian a ralchanhmi misual pawl ca zongah a hman tawn. (1Johan 2:15-17) Cu bantukin Armageddon raldohnak ruangah “hi vawlei donghnak” a phan lai.—Matthai 24:3, KingJames Version.Armageddon raldohnak cu zeitik ah dah a si lai? ‘Harnak nganpi’ i a zik a simi Armageddon raldohnak he aa tlaiin Jesuh nih hitin a chim: “Asinain cu ni le cu caan cu zeitik ah dah a si lai ti kha ahohmanh nih an hngal lo; vancungmi zong nih an hngal lo, Fapa zong nih a hngal hlei lo, Pa lawnglawng nih a hngalh.” (Matthai 24:21, 36) Asinain Armageddon raldohnak cu 1914 in aa thawkmi, mit in hmuh khawh lomi Jesuh ratnak caan chungah a si lai ti kha Baibal nih a langhter.—Matthai 24:37-39.A si lai lo, Vawlei cu zeitikhmanh ah mei in khangh asiloah hrawh a si lai lo i a dang in airolh zong a si lai lo. Pathian nih vawlei hi zungzal hmun dingin a ser tiah Baibal nih a langhter.  “A dingmi cu ram chungah him tein an um lai i ram cu zungzal in anmah ta a si lai.”—Salm 37:29.  “Vawlei cu a umnak hmun ah khan fek tein na bunh i ahohmanh nih an ṭhial kho lo.”—Salm 104:5.  “Vawlei cu a sining ṭhiamṭhiam khan a hmun zungzal ko.”—Phungchimtu 1:4.  “Vawlei kha a ser i a siam, fek te le saupi nguh in a ser, vawlei cu thetse ram, ram pakpalawng ah a ser lo, minung umnak caah a ser.”—Isaiah 45:18.Thli le ti thurhnawmhnak, raldohnak asiloah a dangdang ruangah vawlei rawh dih dingin cun Pathian nih a awnh lai lo. Mah canah ‘vawlei a hrawktu hna kha a hrawh’ hna lai. (Biathlam 11:18) Zeitindah cutin a tuah lai?Vawlei a huppheng kho lomi minung cozah kha zei thil paoh a tuah khomi, a tlingmi vancung Pennak in Pathian nih a airolh lai.
