(Daniel 2:44; Matthai 6:9, 10) Mah Pennak i uktu cu Pathian Fapa, Jesuh Khrih a si lai. (Isaiah 9:6,7) Vawleicung a um lioah Jesuh nih kokek ṭhawnnak a uk khawh kha a rak langhter. (Marka 4:35-41) Pathian Pennak Siangpahrang in Jesuh nih vawlei le kokek ṭhawnnak hna kha a uk lai. Vawlei kha a hramthawk ah a rak ummi, aa dawh tukmi Eden dum bantukin ser ṭhan a si lai.—Matthai 19:28; Luka 23:43.A langhter lo. 2Peter 3:7 ah a chimmi “atu i a ummi van le vawlei hi mei in hrawh awkah a zuah rih hna” timi bia an hngalhthiam ning a palh caah a si. A sullam hngalhthiam awkah a biapimi mah a kong pahnih hi zohhmanh: Baibal nih “van,” “vawlei” le “mei” timi biafang hna kha a dang sullam zongin a hman tawn. Tahchunhnak ah, Salm 33:8 ah hitin a ti: “Vawlei vialte, BAWIPA cu ṭih tuah.” Hika ah “vawlei” timi nih minung kha a aiawh. KuathnihPeter 3:7 i a cungtang bia nih van, vawlei le mei i a sullam kha a langhter. Caang 5 le 6 ah Noah chan i Buanchukcho kong a langhter. Mah lioah vawlei cu ti in hrawh a si ko nain vawlei taktak cu a rak tlau lo. Mah canah a puarhrangmi minung asiloah “vawlei” tu cu hrawh a rak si. (Genesis 6:11, Judson Bible) Vawleicung i mi pawl a uk liomi minung cozah “van” zong hrawh a rak si. Miṭhalo lawng hrawh an si, vawlei cu a rawk lo. Buanchukcho in vawlei hrawhnak in Noah le a chungkhar cu an luat i vawleicung ah khua an rak sa rih.—Genesis 8:15-18.Hrawhnak caah hmanmi ti bantukin 2Peter 3:7 ah langhtermi “mei” zong nih vawlei kha si loin miṭhalo pawl kha a hrawh hna lai. Pathian nih “van thar le vawlei thar, dinnak a umnak hmun” kha a kan kamh. (2Peter 3:13) “Vawlei thar” tiah auhmi minung bu thar kha “van thar” tiah auhmi Pathian Pennak cozah thar nih a uk lai. Pathian Pennak uknak tangah vawlei cu a himmi paradis a hung si lai.—Biathlam 21:1-4.Jesuh a chuah hnuah a sin i a va tlawngmi hna kha a laar ngaimi Christmas phungphai ahcun “mifim pathum” asiloah “siangpahrang pathum” in langhter an si nain Baibal nih cun cutin a langhter lo. (Matthai 2:1) Mah canah Thawngṭha cauk ṭialtu Matthai nih Jesuh sin a tlawngmi hna kong a ṭial tikah Greek biafang ma’goi kha a hman. Mah biafang nih arfi zohthiammi hna le khuachia thiamnak a ngeimi hna kha a sawh duhmi a si.* Baibal lehnak tampi zong nih “arfi zohthiammi” asiloah “khuachia thiamnak a ngeimi”* ti in an leh.“Mifim hna” cu pa zeizat dah an si?“Mifim hna” cu siangpahrang an si maw?“Mifim hna” i an min cu ahodah an si?“Mifim hna” cu Jesuh sinah zeitik ah dah an va tlawn?“Mifim hna” kha Pathian nih Bethlehem “arfi” hnu zulh dingin a fial hna maw?“Mifim hna” cu pa zeizat dah an si?Baibal nih mah kong cu a langhter lo, asinain pa zeizat dah an si timi kong he aa tlaiin ruahnak tampi a um. Encyclopedia Britannica cauk nih hitin a ti: “Nichuahlei phungphai ahcun 12 an si tiah an ti. Nitlaklei phungphai ahcun laksawng pathum a simi ‘sui, frankinsens zihmui le mura zihmui’ (Matthai 2:11) cungah i hngat in mifim pathum an si tiah an ti.”“Mifim hna” cu siangpahrang an si maw?Christmas phungphai ahcun mah mifim hna kha siangpahrang in an langhter hna, asinain Baibal nih cun cutin a langhter lo. Encyclopedia Britannica cauk nih Jesuh a chuah in kum za leng a rauh hnuah mi nih Jesuh chuah ni he aa tlaiin phungphai pawl an chap chih i “mah mifim hna cu siangpahrang an si tiah an hun chim” tiin a langhter.“Mifim hna” i an min cu ahodah an si?Baibal nih arfi zohthiammi hna i an min kha a langhter lo. The International Standard Bible Encyclopedia cauk nih “annih kha tuanbia min (tahchunhnak ah, Gaspar, Melchior le Balthasar) pek dingin an i zuam” tiah a ti.“Mifim hna” cu Jesuh sinah zeitik ah dah an va tlawn?Arfi zohthiammi hna cu Jesuh a chuah in thla tampi hnuah an va tlawnmi a si men lai. Zeicatiah Jesuh thah a duhmi Siangpahrang Herod nih kumhnih le kumhnih tang ngakchiapa pawl thah dingin nawl a rak pek hna. Mah cu arfi zohthiammi hna nih an chimmi bia cungah i hngat in a tuakmi a si.—Matthai 2:16.Arfi zohthiammi hna nih Jesuh kha a chuah zan ah an va tlawnmi a si lo. Baibal nih hitin a ti: “Inn chungah khan an vung lut i ngakchia kha a nu Mari sinah cun an vung hmuh.” (Matthai 2:11) Mah nih Jesuh te chungkhar cu inn pakhat ah an um cang ti kha a langhter, cun Jesuh zong caw rawl einak kuang chungah an thlimmi bawhte a si ti lo.—Luka 2:16.“Mifim hna” kha Pathian nih Bethlehem “arfi” hnu zulh dingin a fial hna maw?Pathian nih Bethlehem arfi kha a chuahter i arfi zohthiammi hna kha Jesuh sinah lam a hruai hna tiah mi cheukhat nih an zumh. Cutin a si khawh lonak a ruang kha zohhmanh hna u sih. Arfi tiah ruahmi a ceumi nih arfi zohthiammi hna kha Jerusalem lei ah kal hmasa dingin lam a hruai hna. Baibal nih hitin a ti: “Arfi zohthiammi hna kha nichuahlei in Jerusalem khua ah khan an ra i, ‘Judah siangpahrang a si lai dingmi ngakchia a chuakmi cu khuazei ah dah a um? A arfi nichuahlei in a chuah kha kan hmuh i amah biak awkah cun atu hi kan ra.’”—Matthai 2:1,2. Arfi zohthiammi hna kha Bethlehem ah kal dingin lamhruainak a pemi hna cu arfi a si lo, SiangpahrangHerod a si. Herod nih amah dotu “Judah siangpahrang” kong a theih tikah biakammi Khrih a chuah lainak hmun kha a hlathlai. (Matthai 2:3-6) Bethlehem ah a chuak lai ti a hngalh tikah arfi zohthiammi hna kha Bethlehem ah kal in ngakchia kha va zoh awkah a fial hna, cun a sinah rak kir ṭhan in a kong chimh ṭhan ding zongin a fial hna.Cucaah arfi zohthiammi hna cu Bethlehem lei ah an kal. Baibal nih hitin a ti: “Siangpahrang nih a ti hna bang cun an kal; cun nichuahlei ah an rak hmuh cangmi arfi kha a lang ṭhan i an hmaiah a kal i ngakchia umnak cungah cun a dir.”—Matthai 2:9. Mah “arfi” ruangah Jesuh cu thah a rak si deng i sualnak a ngei lomi a dang ngakchia tampi zong thah an rak si. Arfi zohthiammi hna cu Bethlehem in an chuah tikah Herod sinah kir ṭhan ti lo dingin Pathian nih ralrin a pek hna.—Matthai 2:12.Herod nih zeitindah a rak lehrulh? Baibal nih hitin a ti: “Herod nih nichuahlei mifim hna nih an ka hlen, ti kha a hngalh tikah a thin a hung ngaingai. Arfi a chuahnak kong nichuahlei mifim hna nih an chimning khan a caan cu a tuak i Bethlehem khua le a pawngkam i a ummi khua hna chung i ngakchiapa kumhnih ri in a tanglei paoh kha thah dih hna awkah nawlbia a pek hna.” (Matthai 2:16) Pathian nih cu bantuk thilṭhalo a chuah nakhnga a tuah lai lo.—Job 34:10.Buanchukcho cu a um taktakmi a si. Pathian nih miṭhalo pawl hrawh awkah a umtermi a si, asinain miṭha pawl le saram pawl him tein an um khawh nakhnga Noah kha lawng sak a fial. (Genesis 6:11-20) “Pathian thaw chuah hnawhmi” Baibal cauk ah a ummi a si caah Buanchukcho cu a um taktakmi a si tiah kan zumh khawh.—2 Timote 3:16.A um taktakmi asiloah tuanbia maw a si?Zeicah Buanchukcho cu a um?Mi nih Buanchukcho a tlung lai ti kha an hngal maw?Noah sakmi lawng cu zeidah a lawh?Noah nih lawng saknak ah zei can dah a rauh?Buanchukcho tuanbiaBaibal nih Noah le Buanchukcho kong kha tuanbia si loin a um taktakmi in a langhter. Baibal ṭialtu hna nih Noah cu a um taktakmi in an cohlan. Tahchunhnak ah, Baibal ṭialtu Ezra le Luka nih tuanbialei kong ṭial awkah ṭha tein hlathlainak an tuah. Israel mi chuahkehnak kong an ṭial tikah Noah aa tel, cucaah Noah cu a rak um taktakmi a si ti a fiang. (1 Chanrelnak 1:4; Luka 3:36 ) Thawngṭha Cauk ṭialtu Matthai le Luka nih Jesuh chimmi Noah le Buanchukcho kong kha an rak ṭial.—Matthai 24:37-39; Luka 17:26, 27.Mah lengah profet Ezekiel le lamkaltu Paul nih Noah kha zumhnak le dinnak kong ah zohchunh awk ṭha in an langhter. (Ezekiel 14:14, 20; Hebru 11:7) Tuanbia chung i mi pakhat kha zohchunh awk ṭhami in mah Baibal ṭialtu hna nih an langhter lai maw? Noah le a dang zumhfekmi nu le pa hna cu a um taktakmi an si caah zohchunh awk ṭha an si.—Hebru 12:1; Jeim 5:17. Baibal nih Buanchukcho kong he aa tlaiin a dikthliar in a langhter. Buanchukcho kong Baibal tuanbia cu tuanbia sawhsawh bantukin “Hlan lioah” timi bia in aa thawk lo. Mah canah Buanchukcho he aa tlaiin a kum, a thla le a ni kha Baibal nih a langhter. (Genesis 7:11; 8:4, 13, 14) Cun Noah sakmi lawng i a sau, a kauh zong a langhter. (Genesis 6:15) Mah kong hna nih Buanchukcho cu tuanbia men si loin a um taktakmi a si ti kha a langhter.Baibal nih Buanchukcho hlanah mi cu ‘an ṭhalo tuk hringhran’ tiah a ti. (Genesis 6:5) Vawleicung ah zaangennak le nupa sualnak in a khah caah “Pathian mithmuh ah miṭhalo an si dih” ti zongin a ti.—Genesis 6:11; Judas 6, 7.Cu bantukin ṭhatlonak a tam tukmi cu a ṭhalomi vancungmi hna nih minung nu hna he an i ṭhitum caah a si tiah Baibal nih a ti. Mah vancungmi nih an hrinmi fale cu Nefalim tiah auh an si, annih nih mah lio caan i a nungmi hna kha harnak le fahnak an pek hna. (Genesis 6:1, 2, 4) Cucaah Pathian nih miṭhalo pawl hrawh awk le miṭha pawl kha nunning thar in nun khawh awkah bia a khiah.—Genesis 6:6, 7, 17.An hngalh. Pathian nih Noah kha a cang dingmi kong a chimh i a chungkhar le saram pawl him tein an um khawh nakhnga lawng sak dingin lamhruainak a pek. (Genesis 6:13, 14; 7:1-4) Noah nih mi pawl kha a ra laimi hrawhnak kong ralrin a pek hna nain zei ah an rel lo. (2 Peter 2:5) Baibal nih hitin a ti: “Tilian a hung tlun taktak i a fenh dih hna hlantiang kha cu, zeihmanh an hngal lo.”—Matthai 24:37-39.Lawng cu a ngan tukmi kuang bantuk a si i a sau pe 437 (133 meter), a kauh pe 73 (22 meter), a san pe 44 (13 meter) a si.* Lawng cu thing ṭha in an sak i a chung he, a leng he kattaza sii an thuh. Dot thum a um i a khaan zong tampi a um. Lawng a kam ah innka a um i a cungah thlalang awng a um. Ti a tlak khawh nakhnga a cung khuh kha a lai in zumter dawh a si.—Genesis 6:14-16.Noah cu lawng saknak ah zei can dah a rauh ti kha Baibal nih a chim lo, asinain kumhrabu tampi rauh dawh a si. Noah cu a fapa upa bik a ngeih lioah kum 500 leng a si i Buanchukcho a tlun lioah kum 600 a si.*—Genesis 5:32; 7:6.Pathian nih Noah kha a fapale pathum an cutzat i nupi an ngeih hnuah lawng sak a fial, mah caan karlak cu kum 50 asiloah 60 hrawng a rau men lai. (Genesis 6:14, 18) Mah cungah i hngat in lawng saknak ah kum 40 asiloah 50 an rau tiah ti khawh a si.A hmang lo. Minung, saram le thingkung hna kha anmahle an ‘phun’ ningin Pathian nih a ser hna tiah Baibal nih fiang tein a langhter.* (Genesis 1:12, 21, 25, 27; Biathlam 4:11) Minung cu a hmasa bik kan nu le kan pa Adam le Eve hrinsor lawngte kan si tiah a ti. (Genesis 3:20; 4:1) Baibal ah Pathian nih thlennawnnak kha hmangin thilnung a phunphun a ser hna timi kong a um lo. Asinain science lei mifim pawl nih thilnung phunkhat cio ah a phun aa ṭhen ṭhanmi a phunphun a um tiah an timi cu Baibal he aa ralkah lo.Pathian nih thlennawnnak kha a hmang maw?Baibal le thlennawnnak cu aa tlak maw?Thingkung le saram pawl an i thlen khawhmi cu thlennawnnak a si maw?Pathian nih thlennawnnak kha hmangin thilnung pawl a ser hna tiah a zummi hna nih ruahnak a phunphun an ngei. Encyclopædia Britannica ningin “thlennawnnak timi cu Pathian nih kokek vawlei a uk tikah a hmanmi lam pakhat a si tiah mi cheukhat nih an zumh.”Mah zumhnak lakah a tanglei i ruahnak hna zong hi aa tel kho men:  Hlanlio kum tampi in thilnung dihlak cu chuahkehnak aa lomi in hrinsormi kan si.  Thilnung phunkhat cu aa thleidang tukmi a dang thilnung phunkhat ah duhsah duhsah tein aa thleng.  Mah thlennak ah a biapi bikmi cu Pathian a si.Thlennawnnak nih Genesis Baibal i sernak kong cu a palh dih tiah a ti bantuk a si. Asinain Jesuh nih Genesis Baibal chung i sernak kong cu a si taktakmi kong in a langhter. (Genesis 1:26, 27; 2:18-24; Matthai 19:4-6) Jesuh cu vawleicung a rat hlanah van ah Pathian he an umṭi i ‘zeizong vialte sernak’ ah a bawmh tiah Baibal nih a ti. (Johan 1:3) Cucaah Pathian nih thlennawnnak kha hmangin thilnung a phunphun a ser hna timi ruahnak cu Baibal he aa tlak lo.Baibal ah phun pakhat in zeitluk tiangin dah phun aa ṭhen khawh timi kong a chim lo. Pathian nih a sermi thingkung le saram pawl cu pawngkam sining he aa tlakin an i thleng kho asiloah an nung kho timi cu Baibal he aa ralkah lo. Mi cheukhat nih cutin an i thlen khawhmi cu thlennawnnak a si tiah an zumh nain thilnung a thar phun khat a chuak timi a um lo.Baibal ah “Sui Nawlbia” timi biafang cu a um lo. Asinain mi tampi nih mah biafang kha Jesuh cawnpiakmi nawlbia caah an hman. A min a thang tukmi Tlang Cung Cawnpiaknak ah Jesuh nih hitin a ti: “Mi nih kan cungah tuah hna seh ti nan duh bantuk khan midang cung zongah va tuah ve u.” (Matthai 7:12; Luka 6:31) Sui Nawlbia kha hiti zongin langhter a si: “Na cungah tuah hna seh ti na duh bangin midang cung zongah va tuah ve.”—Encyclopedia of Philosophy.Sui Nawlbia timi a sullam cu zeidah a si?Sui Nawlbia cu zeicah a ṭhat?Sui Nawlbia cu peknak le hmuhnak kong sawhsawh a si maw?Sui Nawlbia kha zeitindah na zulh khawh?Sui Nawlbia nih midang kha rak kan pehtlai hna seh ti kan duhmi ningin pehtlaih ve hna awkah a kan forh. Tahchunhnak ah, mi tampi nih upatnak, nemnak le dawtnak in midang nih an pehtlaih hna tikah an sunsak tuk. Kannih zong midang cungah cutin kan tuah ve awk a si.—Luka 6:31.Sui Nawlbia kha thil sining tampi ah hman khawh a si. Tahchunhnak ah, mah nih...  Chungkhar a fehter khawh.—Efesa 5:28, 33.  Fale zohkhenhnak ah nulepa kha a bawmh khawh hna.—Efesa 6:4.  Hawikom, innpa le rianṭuanṭi hawi he pehtlaihnak ṭha a kan ngeihter khawh.—Phungthlukbia 3:27, 28; Kolose 3:13.Sui Nawlbia cu Biakam Hlun ah tampi kan hmuhmi phunglam he an i khat. Jesuh nih a chimmi mah nawlbia cu “[Baibal a hramthawk uknga] Nawlbia le Profet bia [profet cauk] hna i a sullam a si.” (Matthai 7:12) Phungdang in cun, Sui Nawlbia cu Biakam Hlun i a hrampi biatak a simi, innpa daw u timi ah khan an i fun dih.—Rom 13:8-10.A si lo. Sui Nawlbia nih peknak kong kha a hleiin a langhter. Jesuh nih Sui Nawlbia kong a chim tikah zaran mi sawhsawh pehtlaih ning lawng kha si loin kan ral pawl pehtlaih ning zong aa tel. (Luka 6:27-31, 35) Cucaah Sui Nawlbia nih mi vialte cungah ṭhatnak tuah awkah a kan forh.1. Midang duhning kha hmuhthiam i zuam. Na pawngkam mi kha ṭha tein zoh hna. Tahchunhnak ah, mi pakhat nih a ritmi eidin thiltom a cawimi kha na hmuh men lai, na innpa siizung a phan ti kha na theih men lai asiloah na rianṭuanṭi hawi a lung a donghmi kha na hmuh men lai. ‘Midang duhning kha hmuhthiam naa zuam’ tikah an caah bawmtu a si hngami bia chim awk asiloah tuah awkah caanṭha na hmuh ko lai.—Filipi 2:4.2. Zawnruahnak ngei. Midang zaka ah i umter chunh. An tonmi thil sining khi hei tong law zeitindah na um lai? (Rom 12:15) Midang intuarnak kha hngalhthiam naa zuam tikah mah nih anmah bawmh awkah ann forh lai.3. A tlarimi si. Mi vialte cu kan i dang ti kha i cinken. Midang nih kan caah tuah hna seh ti an duhmi le nangmah nih ka caah tuah hna seh ti na duhmi cu aa khat men lai lo. Cucaah na tuah khawhmi thil tampi lakah an duh hnga dingmi kha tuah i zuam.—1Korin 10:24.A si lo. Baibal nih tangka cu a ṭhalo tiah a ti lo i ṭhatlonak vialte a chuahtertu a si ti zongin a ti lo. “Tangka ... hi ṭhatlonak phun kip chuahnak hram a si” timi bia cu a tling loin an cherhchanmi a si i mah nih Baibal cungah a hmaan lomi hmuhnak a ngeihter hna. A tak ti ahcun Baibal nih “tangka duhnak hi ṭhatlonak phun kip chuahnak hram a si” tiah a ti.*—1Timote 6:10.Baibal nih tangka kong he aa tlaiin zeidah a chim?Zeicah Baibal nih tangka duhnak he aa tlaiin ralrin a kan pek?Tangka he aa tlaimi Baibal ruahnak cheuhnak in zeitindah ṭhatnak kan hmuh khawh?Tangka kong he aa tlaimi Baibal caang hnaBaibal nih tangkacu fimkhurteinkanhman tikah man a ngei tuk i ‘huhphenhnak’ hmanh a kan pek khawh tiah a ti. (Phungchimtu 7:12, NW) Baibal nih midang cungah siannak a langhtermi hna kha a thangṭhat hna. Mah ah tangka lei bawmhnak zong aa tel.—Phungthlukbia 11:25Baibal nih kan nunnak ah tangkakhaa biapibik ah chiah lo dingin ralrin a kan pek. Hitin a ti: “Tangka hi duh tuk hlah u, nan ngeihmi ah khan nan lung awi ko u.” (Hebru 13:5) Kan cawn khawhmi cu tangka kha aa tlak ningin hman le rum awkah i zuam lo ding kha a si. Mah canah tirawl, thilpuan leumnak inn ti bantuk kan herh taktakmi thil hna in i lungsi awkah kan i zuam ding a si.—1Timote 6:8.Ahak a kaumi nihcunzungzal nunnak an hmu lai lo. (Efesa 5:5) Zeicatiah hakkauhnak cu siasal biaknak asiloah a hmaan lomi biaknakphunkhat a si caaha si.(Kolose 3:5) Cun a hak a kaumi nih an duhmi thil hmuh khawhawkaha ṭhami phunglam hna kha an hlawt tawn. Phungthlukbia 28:20 nih “khulrang in rum aa zuammi cu dantatnak hmu loin a um lai lo” tiah a ti. Mah nih tlerhkhonhnak, hramhram in tangka chuhnak, hlennak, minung firnak le thahnak ti bantuk zaang-ennak hna hmanh a tuahter khawh hna.Tangkaduhnaknih a ṭhalomi ziaza a kan ngeihter lo hmanhah a dang thil ṭhalo tampi a chuahter khawh. Baibal nih “rum a duhmi hna cu tukforhnak chungah khan an tla i ṭih a nungmi le ṭhatlonak a chuahter khotu duhnak nih khan rap foih in a foih hna” tiah a ti.—1Timote 6:9.Tangka ruangah ziazalei phunglam le thlaraulei thil hna kha kan thlahdorh lo ahcun Pathian mithmai ṭha le bawmhnak kan hmuh lengah mahle mah upatnak zong kan ngei lai. Pathian nih a lung lawmhter awkah lungthin tak tein aa zuammi kha hitin bia a kamh hna: “Kaan kaltak bal hna lai lo i kaan hlaw bal fawn hna lai lo.” (Hebru 13:5, 6) Cun “zumh awk tlakmi cu thluachuahnak tampi a hmu lai” ti zongin bia a kan kamh.—Phungthlukbia 28:20.Aan bawmh khawh. Pathian nih a zawmi a salle kha a zohkhenh hna. Zumhfekmi a salle kong he aa tlaiin Baibal nih hitin a ti: “A zawt tikah BAWIPA nih a bawmh lai i a damter ṭhan lai.” (Salm 41:3) Caan saupi a zawmi na si ahcun inkhawh awkah a tanglei i a kong pathum nih aan bawmh khawh: Inkhawhnak ngeih awkah thla cam. “Pathian daihnak, minung hngalhnak a lonhtu” kha na hmuh lai, mah nih na lungretheihnak kha a zorter khawh i lungdaihnak aan pek khawh.—Filipi 4:6, 7. A ṭhatnak in hmuhnak ngei. Baibal nih hitin a ti: “Lungthin lawmh hi sii ṭha a si, sihmanhsehlaw lungthin ngaihchia nih ruh kha a roter.” (Phungthlukbia 17:22) Nuam tein um khawh i zuam, mah nih na ngaihchiatnak kha a zorter deuh lai i na ngandamnak zong a ṭhatter deuh lai. Hmailei naa ruahchannak kha fehter. A ṭhami ruahchannak nih caan saupi na zawt hmanhah i nuamh awkah aan bawmh khawh. (Rom 12:12) Baibal nih hmailei caan kong he aa tlaiin hitin a chimchung: “Kan ram i a ummi cu ka zaw tiah an zai ti lai lo.” (Isaiah 33:24) Chan thar science fimnak nih a damh khawh lomi zawtnak hna kha Pathian nih a hloh cang lai. Tahchunhnak ah, Baibal nih tar an no ṭhan lai timi he aa tlaiin hitin a ti: “Cu pa cu a tlanval lio nak khan a titsa a ṭha deuh lai i a ṭhawn siling te ah khan a kir ṭhan lai.”—Job 33:25.Cinken awk: Jehovah Tehte Hna nih Pathian bawmhnak kha an i bochan ko nain caan saupi zawtnak he aa tlaimi siithlopnak zong an cohlan. (Marka 2:17) Asinain siithlop ning pakhatkhat he aa tlaiin hnatlaknak kan tuahmi cu a um lo; pakhat cio nih mah tein biakhiahnak tuah awk a si ti kha kan hngalh.Baibal ah Jesuh cu “Pathian Fapa” tiah a auh lengmang. (Johan 1:49) “Pathian Fapa” timi bia nih Jesuh i tel in Pathian cu thilnung vialte i nunnak Hrampi asiloah Sertu a si ti kha a langhter. (Salm 36:9; Biathlam 4:11) Minung nih fa kan ngeih bantuk in Pathian zong nih fa a ngeih ve hna tiah Baibal nih a kan cawnpiak lo.Baibal nih vancungmi zong “Pathian fapa hna” tiah a auh hna. (Job 1:6) Cun Baibal nih a hmasa bik mipa Adam zong “Pathian fapa” tiah a auh. (Luka 3:38) Asinain Jesuh cu Pathian nih a ser hmasa bikmi le amah nih direct in a sermi a si caah Baibal nih Pathian Fapa ngeihchun tiah a ti.Jesuh cu vawleicung ah hrin a si hlanah vancung ah a um cang maw?Jesuh cu vawleicung a rat hlanah zeidah a tuah?A um cang. Jesuh cu vawleicung ah minung in hrin a si hlanah vancung ah thlarau pum in a rak um cang. Jesuh theng nih hitin a ti: “Vancung in ka rung ṭum.”—Johan 6:38; 8:23.Zei zong vialte a ser hlanah Pathian nih Jesuh kha a ser. Jesuh kong he aa tlaiin Baibal nih hitin a ti:  “Khrih cu ... sermi thil vialte hna nakin a cungnung deuhmi a si.”—Kolose 1:15.  “Amah cu Pathian nih a sermi vialte hram a si.”—Biathlam 3:14.“Amah a hram cu kan hnuleipi caan, a luan cangmi caan chungah khan a um cangmi a si” timi chimchungbia kha Jesuh nih a tlinter.—Mikah 5:2; Matthai 2:4-6.Vancung ah a sangmi rian a rak ngei. Jesuh nih mah a sangmi rian kong he aa tlaiin a thlacamnak ah hitin a ti: “Ka Pa, vawlei ser hlan i nangmah sin i ka rak ngeihmi sunparnak kha ... ka pe tuah.”—Johan 17:5.Zei zong vialte sernak ah Pathian kha a rak bawmh. Jesuh cu “rian thiam ngaimi” in Pathian he rian an ṭuanṭi. (Phungthlukbia 8:30) Jesuh kong he aa tlaiin Baibal nih hitin a ti: “Pathian nih Khrih thawng cun van le vawlei i a ummi thil vialte kha a ser hna.”—Kolose 1:16.Pathian nih Jesuh hmangin zei zong vialte kha a ser. Van le vawlei i tel in vancungmi vialte zong a ser hna. (Biathlam 5:11) Thil sining cheukhat ah Pathian le Jesuh an rian ṭuan ning cu inn pungsan a suaitu [architect] le inn a satu he aa lo. Inn pungsan a suaitu nih inn pungsan kha a suai i inn satu nih mah ningin a sak.Anih cu Bia a si. Minung in hrin a si hlan i a nunnak kong he aa tlaiin a chim tikah Baibal nih Jesuh kha “Bia” tiah a auh. (Johan 1:1) Cucaah a dang vancungmi pawl sinah thawngthanh awk le lamhruainak pek awkah Pathian nih a Fapa kha a hman ti cu a fiang ko.Jesuh cu minung sinah Pathian Bia a chimtu zong a si. Eden dum i Adam le Evi sinah Pathian nih Bia a simi Jesuh sinin lamhruainak a pekmi hna a si men lai. (Genesis 2:16, 17) Hlanlio Israel mi thetse ram ah lam a hruaitu hna vancungmi zong Jesuh a si men lai. Mah vancungmi nawl kha ngaih awkah Israel mi pawl cu nawl pek an si.—Exodus 23:20-23.*A langhter. Jesuh nih vawleicung a um lioah “vawlei Khamhtu” a si hngami “Pathian thimmi bawi,” Messiah kong chimchungbia tampi kha a rak tlinter. (Daniel 9:25; 1Johan 4:14) A thih hnu hmanhah Messiah kong he aa tlaimi chimchungbia hna kha a tlinter rih.—Salm 110:1; Lamkaltu 2:34-36.“Messiah” timi cu zei sullam dah a si?Messiah kong chimchungbia hna kha mi pakhat nak tam nih an tlinter kho maw?Messiah cu hmailei ah a lang dingmi a si maw?Baibal ah Messiah kong chimchungbia pa zeizat dah a um?Jesuh thawngin a tling cangmi Messiah kong chimchungbia cheukhatHebru biafang Ma·shiʹach (Messiah) le mah he aa lomi Greek biafang Khri·stos (Khrih) cu “Chiti Thuhmi” ti sullam a ngei. Cucaah “Jesuh Khrih” timi cu “Chiti Thuhmi Jesuh” asiloah “Messiah Jesuh” tinak a si.Baibal chan ah mi pakhat cu a hleikhunmi nawlngeihnak pek a si tikah a lu ah chiti thiang an toihnak thawngin chiti thuh a si. (Levitikas 8:12; 1Samuel 16:13) Jesuh cu Pathian nih Messiah in a sangmi nawlngeihnak a pek. (Lamkaltu 2:36) Asinain Pathian nih Jesuh kha chiti taktak in si loin thiang thlarau in chiti a thuh.—Matthai 3:16.An tlinter kho lo. Siapi neh pakhat nih mi pakhat lawng a aiawh bantukin Baibal chimchungbia hna nih Messiah asiloah Khrih pakhat lawng kha a aiawh. Asinain Baibal nih “nal messiah le nal profet kha an chuak lai i Pathian mithim pawl hlen kha a si kho dingmi thil a si ahcun cu hna hlen khawhnak ding caah cun hmelchunhnak le khuaruahhar nganngan kha an ser hna lai” tiah ralrin a kan pek.—Matthai 24:24.A si lo. Baibal nih Messiah cu Israel Siangpahrang David tefa a si lai tiah a chimchung. (Salm 89:3,4) Asinain Judah pupa hna cazin cu a rak tlau, mah cu AD 70 ah Rom nih Jerusalem an hrawh lioah a rawkmi a si kho men.* Mah caan thawkin anih cu Siangpahrang David tefa a si tiin ahohmanh nih an langhter kho lo. Asinain Jesuh chan ah mah pupa hna cazin cu a um rih caah David tefa a si ti kha a ral pawl hmanh nih an al ngam lo.—Matthai 22:41-46.Messiah kong chimchungbia pa zeizat dah a um ti cu fiang tein kan chim kho lo. Tahchunhnak ah, chimchungbia kong an rel ning cu aa lo lo. Isaiah 53:2-7 ah Messiah kong chimchungbia tampi a um. Mi cheukhat nih mah Baibal dihlak kha chimchungbia pakhat in an rel i cheukhat nih cun chimchungbia pakhat cio kha a dangdang in an rel.ChimchungbiaA UmnakA TlinnakAbraham TefaGenesis 22:17, 18Matthai 1:1Abraham fapa Isak tefaGenesis 17:19Matthai 1:2Israel mi, Judah hrinsorGenesis 49:10Matthai 1:1,3Siangpahrang David hrinsorIsaiah 9:7Matthai 1:1Ngaknu thiang chungin a chuakIsaiah 7:14Matthai 1:18, 22, 23Bethlehem khua ah a chuakMikah 5:2Matthai 2:1, 5,6Immanuel* tiah auh a siIsaiah 7:14Matthai 1:21-23A nautami sining in aa thawkIsaiah 53:2Luka 2:7A chuah hnuah ngakchia pawl cu thah an siJeremiah 31:15Matthai 2:16-18Izipt ah kalpi a siHosea 11:1Matthai 2:13-15Nazareth* khua mi tiah auh a siIsaiah 11:1Matthai 2:23A hmaiah lamkal thlah a siMalakhi 3:1Matthai 11:7-10AD 29*ah Messiah in chiti thuh a siDaniel 9:25Matthai 3:13-17Pathian nih a Fapa in a thanhSalm 2:7Lamkaltu 13:33, 34Pathian inn caah lungthawhnak a ngeiSalm 69:9Johan 2:13-17Thawngṭha thanhtu a siIsaiah 61:1Luka 4:16-21Galili ram ah ceunak nganpi a tlungIsaiah 9:1,2Matthai 4:13-16Moses bantukin khuaruahhar thil a tuahDeuteronomi 18:15Lamkaltu 2:22Moses bantukin Pathian bia a chimDeuteronomi 18:18, 19Johan 12:49Mizaw tampi kha a damter hnaIsaiah 53:4Matthai 8:16, 17Mi nih biapi ah an chiah nakhnga aa zuam loIsaiah 42:2Matthai 12:17, 19Namnehmi hna cungah zaangfahnak a langhterIsaiah 42:3Matthai 12:9-20; Marka 6:34Pathian dinnak kha a langhterIsaiah 42:1,4Matthai 12:17-20A Ṭha Bikmi Ruahnak CheutuIsaiah 9:6,7Johan 6:68Jehovah min a thanhSalm 22:22, NWJohan 17:6Tahchunhnak hmangin a chimSalm 78:2Matthai 13:34, 35HruaituDaniel 9:25Matthai 23:10Mi tampi nih an zum loIsaiah 53:1Johan 12:37, 38Tlukrilhtertu lungIsaiah 8:14, 15Matthai 21:42-44Mi nih an hlawtSalm 118:22, 23Lamkaltu 4:10, 11A ruang um loin an huatSalm 69:4Johan 15:24, 25Jerusalem khua ah laa i cit in teinak he a lutZekhariah 9:9Matthai 21:4-9Ngakchia nih an thangṭhatSalm 8:2Matthai 21:15, 16Jehovah min in a raSalm 118:26Johan 12:12, 13A zumhmi a hawikom pakhat nih a rawiSalm 41:9Johan 13:18Ngun tangka 30 in rawi a si*Zekhariah 11:12, 13Matthai 26:14-16; 27:3-10A hawile nih an zamtak Zekhariah 13:7Matthai 26:31, 56A hmaan loin sual an puhSalm 35:11Matthai 26:59-61Sual a puhtu hna hmaiah dai tein a umIsaiah 53:7Matthai 27:12-14Cil an chakIsaiah 50:6Matthai 26:67; 27:27, 30A lu ah fung in an tukMikah 5:1Marka 15:19Hrihrual in an tukIsaiah 50:6Johan 19:1A hremtu hna kha a lehrulh hna loIsaiah 50:6Johan 18:22, 23Cozah nawlngeitu hna nih rawi awkah khua an khanSalm 2:2Luka 23:10-12A kut le a ke kha thir an khenhSalm 22:16Matthai 27:35; Johan 20:25A puan caah voihfung an zuhSalm 22:18Johan 19:23, 24Misual mi hna he rel chih a siIsaiah 53:12Matthai 27:38Serhsat le volhpamh a siSalm 22:7,8Matthai 27:39-43Misual mi hna caah fahnak a inIsaiah 53:5,61Peter 2:23-25Pathian hlawtmi a loSalm 22:1Marka 15:34Mitsur hang hnitkha he cawhmi kha an pek Salm 69:21Matthai 27:34A thih hlanah a ti a halSalm 22:15Johan 19:28, 29A thlarau kha Pathian sinah a chiahSalm 31:5Luka 23:46A nunnak a pekIsaiah 53:12Marka 15:37Sualnak hloh awkah tlanhnak man a pekIsaiah 53:12Matthai 20:28A ruh khiah a si loSalm 34:20Johan 19:31-33, 36Chunh a siZekhariah 12:10Johan 19:33-35, 37Mirum mi hna sinah vui a siIsaiah 53:9Matthai 27:57-60Thihnak in thawhter a siSalm 16:10Lamkaltu 2:29-31Rawitu zaka ah midang an airolhSalm 109:8Lamkaltu 1:15-20Pathian orhlei kam ah a ṭhuSalm 110:1Lamkaltu 2:34-36Mikhael kha biaknak cheukhat nih “A Thiangmi Mikhael” tiah an auh. Mah min cu Jesuh vawleicung a rat hlan le vancung a kir ṭhan hnu i a min a si.* Moses ruak kong he aa tlaiin Mikhael cu Satan he an i al. Profet Daniel sinah Pathian bia a phuangtu vancungmi kha Mikhael nih a rak bawmh. (Daniel 10:13, 21; Judas9) Mikhael timi min sullam cu—“Ahodah Pathian He Aa Lo?” timi a si. Mah min ningin Mikhael cu Pathian uknaklei ah a ṭang i ral pawl kha a doh hna.—Daniel 12:1; Biathlam 12:7.Jesuh cu vancungmi bawi bik Mikhael a si tiah chim khawh a sinak a ruang kha zohhmanh hna u sih. Mikhael cu “vancungmi lak i upa bik” a si. (Judas9) “Vancungmi bawi bik” ti sullam a ngeimi “vancungmi lak i upa bik” timi upatnak min cu Baibal ah voihnih lawng a langhter. A voihnih ningin pakrelnak (singular) ca lawngah a hman. Cucaah mah upatnak min cu vancungmi pakhat lawng nih a ngeihmi a si ti kha a fiang. Baibal caang pakhat nih a tho ṭhanmi Jesuh he aa tlaiin hitin a ti: “Au thawng, vancungmi bawi bik au thawng, ... cu a hung thang lai i Bawipa hrimhrim cu vancung khin a rung ṭum lai.” (1Thesalon 4:16) Jesuh nih “vancungmi bawi bik au thawng” a chuah khawhmi cu amah hrim hi vancungmi bawi bik Mikhael a si caah a si. Mikhael cu vancung ralkapbu hruaitu a si. “Mikhael le a vancungmi hna nih khan limkeng [Satan] cu an doh.” (Biathlam 12:7) Mikhael cu vancung ah nawl a ngei ngaimi a si caah “vancungmi bawi bik” le “a nganmi vancungmi” tiah auh a si. (Daniel 10:13, 21; 12:1) Mah upatnak min hna ruangah Mikhael cu “vancung ralkapbu hruaitu a hung si” tiah New Testament scholar David E. Aune nih a ti.Vancung ralkapbu cungah nawl a ngeimi a dang min pakhat zong kha Baibal nih a langhter. Hitin a ti: “Bawipa Jesuh cu a vancungmi mi ṭhawng hna le meizik he ... a rung ṭum tikah ding tein a tuah lai.” (2Thesalon 1:7,8; Matthai 16:27) Jesuh cu “vancung ah a kai i Pathian orhlei kam ah a um i vancungmi vialte le vancung nawlngeihnak vialte le ṭhawnnak vialte kha a uk dih hna.” (1Peter 3:21, 22) Pathian nih Jesuh he, Mikhael he vancung ralkapbu hruaitu in rian pek cu a si khawh lo caah mah min pahnih cu mi pakhat ngeihmi a si lai tiah kan chim khawh. Mikhael cu a um bal lomi “harnak ṭhalo bik” a tlun caan ah “a hung chuak lai.” (Daniel 12:1) Daniel cauk chungah “a chuak lai” timi biafang kha thil sining a tawngtham dingmi siangpahrang he aa tlaiin a hman tawn. (Daniel 11:2-4, 21) “Pathian Bia” tiah auhmi Jesuh Khrih nih “siangpahrang vialte Siangpahrang” in Pathian ral vialte kha a hrawh dih hna lai i Pathian miphun kha a huhphenh hna lai. (Biathlam 19:11-16) ‘Vawlei hramthawk in nihin ni tiangah a ummi harnak a zeihmanh nakin a fak deuhmi harnak’ caan ah Jesuh nih cutin a tuah lai.—Matthai 24:21, 42.Jesuh Khrih cu mah ni, mah thla ah a chuak tiah langhtermi Baibal ah a um lo. Cherhchanmi cauk cheukhat ah hitin a langhter:  “Khrih a chuah ni taktak cu hngalh a si lo.”—New Catholic Encyclopedia.  “Khrih a chuah ni cu fiang tein hngalh a si lo.”—Encyclopedia of Early Christianity.‘Jesuh cu zeitikah dah a chuah?’ timi biahalnak i a phi cu Baibal ah direct in a um lo nain Jesuh a chuah laite ah a cangmi thil pahnih a um. Mah thil sining kha zoh in mi tampi nih Jesuh cu December 25 ah a chuah lo tiah an ti.Khuasik caan ah a si lo Min thlaknak. Jesuh a chuah hlanah Caesar Augustus nih “ram chung i a ummi vialte nih milu relnak caah nan min nan i thla dih lai” tiah nawl a chuah. Cucaah mikip nih “anmahle an khua cio ah” kal in min an i thlak a hau. An khua cio i an kir ṭhan tikah zarhkhat asiloah mah nak tam an rau kho. (Luka 2:1-3) Ngunkhuai kholhnak le ralkap tlaknak ti bantuk caah bawmtu a si nakhnga cutin nawl a chuahmi a si kho men. Mi pawl nih cu bantuk kongkau ruangah khual tlawn kha an duh lo. Cucaah Augustus nih a ukmi mi pawl kha khuasik caan ah hramhram in khual tlawnter in an thinhun dingin cun a tuah theng lai lo. Tuu. “An tuurun a zohkhenh i ramlak i a riakmi” tuukhal pawl an um. (Luka 2:8) Tuurun pawl cu “Lanhtak Puai [March thla donghlei] a phak hlan zarhkhat” in November thla lai tiang hrawng ramlak ah an um tiah cauk pakhat (Daily Life in the Time of Jesus) nih a ti. Hitin a ti chap: “Tuurun pawl cu khuasik caan ah cungkhuh a ummi thlam tangah an um. Asinain tuukhal pawl cu ramlak ah an um tiah Thawngṭha cauk nih a ti caah khuasik caan ah Christmas puai an tuahmi hi hmaan dawh a si lo.”Khuasik thla thawkJesuh a thih nithla AD 33, ṭhal caan, Nisan 14, Lanhtak Puai in hnulei ah kan rel ṭhan ahcun Jesuh zeitik ah dah a chuah ti kha hngalh khawh a si. (Johan 19:14-16) Kum thum le cheu a raumi phungchim rian a thawk lioah Jesus cu kum 30 hrawng a si. Cucaah Jesuh cu BC 2, khuasik thla thawk ah a chuak.—Luka 3:23.Jesuh Khrih cu December 25 ah a chuak timi langhtertu a um lo nain zeicah mah ni ah Christmas puai an tuah? Encyclopædia Britannica ningin biaknaklei hruaitu hna nih khuasik thla i ni a tawi bik caan ah “siasal a biami Rom mi hna nih tuahmi ‘teinak a hmu pengmi nika pathian chuah ni puai’ he khahter” dingin mah ni kha an thimmi a si. The Encyclopedia Americana ningin “a hmaan lomi biaknak in Khrihfa biaknak ah a rak lutmi hna caah cohlan a fawi deuh nakhnga” cutin an tuahmi a si tiah Baibal lei mifim tampi nih an zumh.Jesuh a chuah hnuah a sin i a va tlawngmi hna kha a laar ngaimi Christmas phungphai ahcun “mifim pathum” asiloah “siangpahrang pathum” in langhter an si nain Baibal nih cun cutin a langhter lo. (Matthai 2:1) Mah canah Thawngṭha cauk ṭialtu Matthai nih Jesuh sin a tlawngmi hna kong a ṭial tikah Greek biafang ma’goi kha a hman. Mah biafang nih arfi zohthiammi hna le khuachia thiamnak a ngeimi hna kha a sawh duhmi a si.* Baibal lehnak tampi zong nih “arfi zohthiammi” asiloah “khuachia thiamnak a ngeimi”* ti in an leh.“Mifim hna” cu pa zeizat dah an si?“Mifim hna” cu siangpahrang an si maw?“Mifim hna” i an min cu ahodah an si?“Mifim hna” cu Jesuh sinah zeitik ah dah an va tlawn?“Mifim hna” kha Pathian nih Bethlehem “arfi” hnu zulh dingin a fial hna maw?“Mifim hna” cu pa zeizat dah an si?Baibal nih mah kong cu a langhter lo, asinain pa zeizat dah an si timi kong he aa tlaiin ruahnak tampi a um. Encyclopedia Britannica cauk nih hitin a ti: “Nichuahlei phungphai ahcun 12 an si tiah an ti. Nitlaklei phungphai ahcun laksawng pathum a simi ‘sui, frankinsens zihmui le mura zihmui’ (Matthai 2:11) cungah i hngat in mifim pathum an si tiah an ti.”“Mifim hna” cu siangpahrang an si maw?Christmas phungphai ahcun mah mifim hna kha siangpahrang in an langhter hna, asinain Baibal nih cun cutin a langhter lo. Encyclopedia Britannica cauk nih Jesuh a chuah in kum za leng a rauh hnuah mi nih Jesuh chuah ni he aa tlaiin phungphai pawl an chap chih i “mah mifim hna cu siangpahrang an si tiah an hun chim” tiin a langhter.“Mifim hna” i an min cu ahodah an si?Baibal nih arfi zohthiammi hna i an min kha a langhter lo. The International Standard Bible Encyclopedia cauk nih “annih kha tuanbia min (tahchunhnak ah, Gaspar, Melchior le Balthasar) pek dingin an i zuam” tiah a ti.“Mifim hna” cu Jesuh sinah zeitik ah dah an va tlawn?Arfi zohthiammi hna cu Jesuh a chuah in thla tampi hnuah an va tlawnmi a si men lai. Zeicatiah Jesuh thah a duhmi Siangpahrang Herod nih kumhnih le kumhnih tang ngakchiapa pawl thah dingin nawl a rak pek hna. Mah cu arfi zohthiammi hna nih an chimmi bia cungah i hngat in a tuakmi a si.—Matthai 2:16.Arfi zohthiammi hna nih Jesuh kha a chuah zan ah an va tlawnmi a si lo. Baibal nih hitin a ti: “Inn chungah khan an vung lut i ngakchia kha a nu Mari sinah cun an vung hmuh.” (Matthai 2:11) Mah nih Jesuh te chungkhar cu inn pakhat ah an um cang ti kha a langhter, cun Jesuh zong caw rawl einak kuang chungah an thlimmi bawhte a si ti lo.—Luka 2:16.“Mifim hna” kha Pathian nih Bethlehem “arfi” hnu zulh dingin a fial hna maw?Pathian nih Bethlehem arfi kha a chuahter i arfi zohthiammi hna kha Jesuh sinah lam a hruai hna tiah mi cheukhat nih an zumh. Cutin a si khawh lonak a ruang kha zohhmanh hna u sih. Arfi tiah ruahmi a ceumi nih arfi zohthiammi hna kha Jerusalem lei ah kal hmasa dingin lam a hruai hna. Baibal nih hitin a ti: “Arfi zohthiammi hna kha nichuahlei in Jerusalem khua ah khan an ra i, ‘Judah siangpahrang a si lai dingmi ngakchia a chuakmi cu khuazei ah dah a um? A arfi nichuahlei in a chuah kha kan hmuh i amah biak awkah cun atu hi kan ra.’”—Matthai 2:1,2. Arfi zohthiammi hna kha Bethlehem ah kal dingin lamhruainak a pemi hna cu arfi a si lo, SiangpahrangHerod a si. Herod nih amah dotu “Judah siangpahrang” kong a theih tikah biakammi Khrih a chuah lainak hmun kha a hlathlai. (Matthai 2:3-6) Bethlehem ah a chuak lai ti a hngalh tikah arfi zohthiammi hna kha Bethlehem ah kal in ngakchia kha va zoh awkah a fial hna, cun a sinah rak kir ṭhan in a kong chimh ṭhan ding zongin a fial hna.Cucaah arfi zohthiammi hna cu Bethlehem lei ah an kal. Baibal nih hitin a ti: “Siangpahrang nih a ti hna bang cun an kal; cun nichuahlei ah an rak hmuh cangmi arfi kha a lang ṭhan i an hmaiah a kal i ngakchia umnak cungah cun a dir.”—Matthai 2:9. Mah “arfi” ruangah Jesuh cu thah a rak si deng i sualnak a ngei lomi a dang ngakchia tampi zong thah an rak si. Arfi zohthiammi hna cu Bethlehem in an chuah tikah Herod sinah kir ṭhan ti lo dingin Pathian nih ralrin a pek hna.—Matthai 2:12.Herod nih zeitindah a rak lehrulh? Baibal nih hitin a ti: “Herod nih nichuahlei mifim hna nih an ka hlen, ti kha a hngalh tikah a thin a hung ngaingai. Arfi a chuahnak kong nichuahlei mifim hna nih an chimning khan a caan cu a tuak i Bethlehem khua le a pawngkam i a ummi khua hna chung i ngakchiapa kumhnih ri in a tanglei paoh kha thah dih hna awkah nawlbia a pek hna.” (Matthai 2:16) Pathian nih cu bantuk thilṭhalo a chuah nakhnga a tuah lai lo.—Job 34:10.Baibal nih Jesuh muisam kong kha a langhter lo caah ahohmanh nih Jesuh muisam taktak kha an hngal lo. Mah nih Jesuh muisam cu a biapi lo ti kha a langhter. Asinain Baibal caang cheukhat zohnak thawngin Jesuh muisam kha mitthlam ah suai khawh a si. A muisam: Jesuh cu Judah miphun a si caah a chuahkehnak miphun mui a keng lai ti cu a fiang ko. (Hebru 7:14) Midang he aa thleidangmi muisam ngeih dawh a si lo. Voikhat cu ahohmanh hngalh loin Galili in Jerusalam khua ah a thli tein a rak kal. (Johan 7:10, 11) A zultu lak zongah aa thleidang hlei lo. Cucaah hriamnam aa kenmi mibu nih amah tlaih dingin an rat tikah Judas Iskariot nih hngalhternak a tuahpiak hna.—Matthai 26:47-49. A sam: Baibal nih “sam sau cu pa caah cun ningzak a si” tiah a ti caah Jesuh cu a sam a sau theng men lai lo.—1Korin 11:14. A khahmul: Jesuh cu khahmul a ngei. “Nan khahmul zong a par nan riam lai lo” timi pa pawl thlauh an simi Judah phungphai kha a rak zulh. (Levitikas 19:27; Galati 4:4) Cun Jesuh nih a ton dingmi harnak kong chimchungbia zongah Jesuh kha khamul a ngeimi in a langhter.—Isaiah 50:6. A pumrua: Langhternak vialte nih Jesuh kha a ṭhawngmi in a langhter. Phungchim rian a ṭuan lioah meng tampi a ke in a rak kal. (Matthai 9:35) Judah mi hna biakinn kha voihnih a rak thenh, tangka thlengtu pawl an cabuai kha a rak lehpiak hna i an saṭil pawl kha hrihrual in a rak ṭhawlpiak dih hna. (Luka 19:45, 46; Johan 2:14, 15) McClintock le Strong Cyclopedia nih hitin a ti: “Thawngṭha cauk vialte nih [Jesuh cu] a ngan a dam i a ṭhawngmi a si kha an langhter.”—VolumeIV, cahmai884. A mithmai: Jesuh cu dawtnak le zaangfahnak a ngeimi a si i mah kha a mithmai ah a lang lai ti cu a fiang ko. (Matthai 11:28, 29) Mikip nih hnemhnak le bawmhnak hmuh awkah a sinah an rat hnawh. (Luka 5:12, 13; 7:37, 38) Ngakchia hmanh nih a sinah um kha an duh.—Matthai 19:13-15; Marka 9:35-37.A hmaan lomi ruahnak: Mi cheukhat nih Jesuh cu Africa mi a si lai tiah an ruah, zeicatiah Biathlam cauk nih a sam kha tuuhmul he a tahchunh i a ke kha “tleu tein an hnormi dar” he a tahchunh caah a si.—Biathlam 1:14, 15.A hmaanmi: Biathlam cauk cu “hngalhtertu” in langhtermi a si. (Biathlam 1:1) Jesuh a sam le a ke langhtermi cu vawleicung a um lio i a muisam kha a langhtermi si loin a thawh ṭhan hnu i a sining langhter awkah tahchunhnak in a hmanmi a si. Biathlam 1:14 ah Jesuh “a sam cu tuuhmul bantuk a si i hawhra bantukin a ngo” tiah a ti tikah a rong taktak kha a chimmi si loin tahchunhnak in a chimmi a si. A raangmi sam nih Jesuh cu kum upa pakhat i fimnak a ngei ti kha tahchunhnak in a langhtermi a si.—Biathlam 3:14.Jesuh a ke cu “somei chungah an tit i tleu tein an hnormi dar bantuk” a si. (Biathlam 1:15) Cun a hmai cu “chunlai ni ceu bantukin a ceu.” (Biathlam 1:16) Cu bantuk langhternak hna he aa khatmi minung ahohmanh an um lo caah mah langhnak cu tahchunhnak a si i a tho ṭhanmi Jesuh cu “a naih in naih khawh lomi ceunak chung i a ummi” a si ti kha a langhter.—1Timote 6:16.A hmaan lomi ruahnak: Jesuh a tha a dermi a si.A hmaanmi: Jesuh a umtu ning cu a pasal tuk. Tahchunhnak ah, hriamnam aa putmi mibu nih amah tlaih awk an rat tikah ralṭha tein aa hngalhter hna. (Johan 18:4-8) Lehtama pakhat in hriamnam pawl ṭha tein a hman khawh caah a thazaang a ṭhawngmi a si ko lai.—Marka 6:3.Zeicah Jesuh nih a vailam tung putnak caah bawmh a herh? Amah he an thlaiṭimi midang pawl thah an si hlanah zeicah a thih? (Luka 23:26; Johan 19:31-33) Jesuh cu thah a si hlan tein pumsalei ah a thazaang a rak der cang. Zan khuadei lungthinlei fahnak a tuar. (Luka 22:42-44) Judah mi nih zan khuadei an hrem i a thaizing zingka ah Rom mi nih tung ah an thlai. (Matthai 26:67, 68; Johan 19:1-3) Mah a kong hna ruangah a thih colhmi a si lai.A hmaan lomi ruahnak: Jesuh cu aa nuam bal lomi, a ngaih a chia pengmi a si.A hmaanmi: Baibal nih “aa nuammi Pathian” in a langhtermi vancung a Pa Jehovah sining hna kha Jesuh nih tling tein a langhter. (1Timote 1:11, NW; Johan 14:9) A tak ti ahcun Jesuh nih midang kha i nuamh khawh ning a cawnpiak hna. (Matthai 5:3-9; Luka 11:28) Mah nih Jesuh mithmai ah nuamhnak a lang lai ti kha a langhter.Mi tampi nih vailamtah cu Khrihfa hmelchunhnak a si tiah an ruah. Asinain Jesuh an thah lioah an hmanmi thilri kong Baibal ah a langhter lo. Cucaah mah thilri cu zei bantuk dah a si ti kha ahohmanh nih fiang tein an hngal kho lo. Asinain Jesuh cu vailamtah cungah si loin a dingmi thingtung cungah a thi ti a langhtertu thil cu Baibal ah a um.Baibal nih Jesuh an thah lioah hmanmi thilri kong a langhter tikah tam deuh cu Greek biafang stau·rosʹ kha a hman. (Matthai 27:40; Johan 19:17) Mah biafang kha “vailamtah” tiah an leh tawn nain a hrampi sullam taktak cu “a dingmi tung” tinak a si tiah Baibal lei mifim tampi nih an cohlan.* Stau·rosʹ timi biafang cu “thing pahnih kalh in aa pehmi phun a si timi sullam a ngei lo” tiah cauk pakhat nih a ti.—A Critical Lexicon and Concordance to the English and Greek New Testament.Baibal ah stau·rosʹ he a sulllam aa khatmi xyʹlon timi Greek biafang zong a hman. (Lamkaltu 5:30; 1Peter 2:24) Mah biafang cu “thing,” “fung,” “tung,” asiloah “thingkung” timi sullam a ngei.* The Companion Bible nih hitin a ti: “Greek Baibal [Biakam Thar] ah thing pahnih phun in a langhtermi zeihmanh a um lo.”Pathian nih biaknak ah vailamtah hman kha a cohlang maw?Misual pawl thahnak ah an hmanmi tung kha Latin biafang in crux simplex tiah an auhJesuh an thah lioah hmanmi thilri pungsang cu zei bantuk a si hmanhah a tanglei kong hna le Baibal caang hna nih biaknak ah vailamtah hman awk a si lo ti kha a langhter. Vailamtah i telin hmanthlak, siasal le hmelchunhnak hna hmangin biak kha Pathian nih a duh lo. Pathian nih Israel mi kha an biaknak ah ‘zei bantuk mui a kengmi’ hmanh hman lo dingin nawl a pek hna. Cu bantukin Khrihfa pawl zong “siasal kha bia hna hlah u” tiah a ti hna.—⁠Deuteronomi 4:15-19; 1Korin 10:14. Kumzabu pakhatnak i Khrihfa hna nih biaknak ah vailamtah an hmang lo.* Lamkaltu pawl  cawnpiaknak le an nunning kha Khrihfa dihlak nih an i zohchunh awk a si.—⁠2Thesalon 2:15. Biaknak ah vailamtah hmannak cu a hmaan lomi biaknak in aa thawkmi a si.* Jesuh a thih in kum za leng a rauh hnuah church pawl cu Jesuh cawnpiaknak in lam an pial i Khrihfabu ah a lut tharmi pawl kha vailamtah i telin “a hmaan lomi biaknak i hmelchunhnak hna kha hmannak nawl an awnh hna.” (The Expanded Vine’s Expository Dictionary of New Testament Words) Asinain mi pawl an biaknak aa thlen nakhnga caah a hmaan lomi biaknak hmelchunhnak pawl hman cu Baibal nih a cohlang lo.—⁠2Korin 6:17.Jesuh nih a nunnak kha raithawinak caah a pek i zumhfekmi minung kha a khamh hna. (Matthai 20:28) Cucaah Baibal nih Jesuh kha “vawlei Khamhtu” tiah a auh. (1 Johan 4:14) Cun hiti zongin a ti: “Amah thawng lawnglawng in khamhnak hi hmuh khawh a si.  Zeicahtiah vawleicung dihlak ah hin a kan khamh khotu ding min dang zeihmanh a um lo.”—Lamkaltu 4:12.Jesuh nih amah a zummi vialte caah ‘thihnak a in.’ (Hebru 2:9; Johan 3:16) Mah hnuah “Pathian nih mithi hna sinin a thawhter” i van ah thlarau pum in a kir ṭhan. (Lamkaltu 3:15) Cucaah Jesuh nih “amah thawngin Pathian a fuhmi hna paoh cu a khamh khawh zungzal ko hna; zeicahtiah zungzal in a nun caah Pathian kha a nawlpiak khawh zungzal hna.”—Hebru 7:25.Kan caah Jesuh nih nawlpiak cu zeicah a herh?Kan dihlak in misual kan si. (Rom 3:23) Sualnak cu Pathian le kan karah dawnkhantu a si i mah nih thihnak a chuahter. (Rom 6:23) Asinain Jesuh cu tlanhnak man a zummi hna caah Pathian ‘sinah bia a chimpiak hna.’ (1Johan 2:1) An thlacamnak ngaihpiak awk, Jesuh raithawinak cungah i hngat in an sualnak ngaihthiam awkah Pathian sinah a nawlpiak hna. (Matthai 1:21; Rom 8:34) Mah cu amah a duhning a si caah Jesuh nawlnak kha a ngaihpiak. Pathian nih Jesuh kha “vawlei Khamhtu” si awkah a rung thlah.—Johan 3:17.Jesuh zumhnak men in khamhnak hmuh a si lai maw?A si lo. Khamhnak kan hmuh nakhnga Jesuh zumhnak lawng in a za lo. (Lamkaltu 16:30, 31) Baibal nih hitin a ti: “Pum cu thlarau loin a thih bantukin zumhnak zong cu tuahnak loin a thi ve.” (Jeim 2:26) Khamhnak hmuh awkah mah hi kan tuah a hau:  Jesuh le a Pa Jehovah kong kan cawn a hau.—Johan 17:3.  Anmah kan zumh hnanak fehter a hau.—Johan 12:44; 14:1.  An nawlbia zulhnak thawngin kan zumhnak langhter a hau. (Luka 6:46; 1Johan 2:17) Jesuh nih “Bawipa, Bawipa,” tiah a ka timi paohin khamh an si lai lo, sihmanhsehlaw “vancung i a ummi ka Pa nih tuah hna seh ti a duhmi a tuahmi lawnglawng” khamh an si lai tiah a ti.—Matthai 7:21.  Harnak caan hmanhah kan zumhnak langhter peng a hau. Jesuh nih fiang tein hitin a ti: “A dongh tiangin a fekmi cu khamh an si lai.”—Matthai 24:13.Jesuh tlanhnak man cu minung kha sualnak le thihnak in Pathian khamhnak lam a si. Baibal nih Jesuh thletmi thisen kha tlanhnak man in a langhter. (Efesa 1:7; 1Peter 1:18, 19) Cucaah Jesuh nih ‘mi tampi tlanhnak ca ka nunnak pek awkah’ ka ra tiah a ti.—Matthai 20:28.Zeicah ‘mi tampi tlanhnak’ cu a herh?Hmasa bik mipa Adam cu mitling in ser a si i sualnak a ngei lo. Zungzal nun ding ruahchannak a ngei nain Pathian nawl a ngaih lo caah mah kha a rak sung. (Genesis 3:17-19) Fa a ngeih tikah sualnak ro a pek hna. (Rom 5:12) Cucaah Adam nih amah le a fale kha sualnak le thihnak sal ah a ‘zuar’ hna tiah Baibal nih a ti. (Rom 7:14) A tefa hna cu a tlingmi an si ti lo, cucaah Adam sunghmi thil kha ahohmanh nih an caw ṭhan kho ti lo.—Salm 49:7,8.Ruahchannak a ngei lomi Adam tefa hna kha Pathian nih a zaangfah hna. (Johan 3:16) Asinain a dingmi Pathian phunglam nih a fekmi a hrampi kong um loin an sualnak kha a ngaithiam hna lo. (Salm 89:14; Rom 3:23-26) Pathian nih minung kha a kan dawt tuk caah kan sualnak ngaihthiam lawng si loin hlohpiak awkah phung ningin a kan timhpiak. (Rom 5:6-8) Mah phung ningin sermi cu tlanhnak man kha a si.Tlanhnak man timi cu zeidah a si?Baibal ningin “tlanhnak man” timi biafang ah a kong pathum aa tel:               Pekmi a man kha a si.—Nambar 3:46, 47. Luatnak asiloah tlanhnak kha a si.—Exodus 21:30. A man aa khatmi asiloah a khuhmi kha a si.*Mah a kong pathum cu Jesuh tlanhnak man he zeitindah aa pehtlaih ti kha zohhmanh u sih. A man. Baibal nih Khrihfa hna cu “a man in cawkmi” an si tiah a ti. (1Korin 6:20; 7:23) Mah man cu Jesuh thi kha a si. Jesuh nih ‘hrin kip le chung kip le holh kip le phun kip chungin, minung cu Pathian [caah a thi in a cawk hna, NW] sinah a phakpi hna.’—Biathlam 5:8,9. Luatnak. Jesuh tlanhnak man thawngin sualnak in ‘luatnak’ kan hmu.—1Korin 1:30; Kolose 1:14; Hebru 9:15. A man aa khatmi. Jesuh tlanhnak man cu Adam nih a sunghmi, a tlingmi miung nunnak he aa khat. (1Korin 15:21, 22, 45, 46) Baibal nih hitin a ti: “Mipa [Adam] pakhat nawlngaih lo ruangah mi tampi kha misual i ser an si bantukin mipa [Jesuh] pakhat nawlngaih ruangah mi tampi cu miding ah ser an si lai.” (Rom 5:19) Mah nih mi pakhat thihnak nih mi tampi caah tlanhnak man zeitindah a pek khawh ti kha a kan hngalhter. A tak ti ahcun, Jesuh tlanhnak cu mah in ṭhatnak hmuh a duhmi “mi vialte caah aa khatmi tlanhnak” a si.—1Timote 2:5,6.Pathian Pennak timi cu Jehovah Pathian nih a dirhmi cozah taktak kha a si. “Pathian pennak” kha “vancung pennak” ti zongin auh a si, zeicatiah vancung in a uk lai caah a si. (Marka 1:14, 15; Matthai 4:17) Pathian Pennak cu lam a phunphun in minung cozah he aa lo, asinain minung cozah nakin a let tampi in a ṭha deuh. Uktu hna. Pathian nih Jesuh Khrih kha a Pennak ah Siangpahrang in rian a pek i minung uktu hna nakin a sang deuhmi nawlngeihnak a pek. (Matthai 28:18) Jesuh nih a nawlngeihnak kha a ṭhatnaklei in a hman. Zumhawk a tlakmi le zaangfahnak a ngeimi Hruaitu a si kha a rak langhter. (Matthai 4:23; Marka 1:40, 41; 6:31-34; Luka 7:11-17) Pathian lamhruainak tangah Jesuh nih vancung ah amah he ‘vawlei a ukṭi’ dingmi hna kha miphun zakip chungin a thim hna.—Biathlam 5:9, 10. Uknak Caan. Aa thleng lengmangmi minung cozah he i lo loin, Pathian Pennak cu “zeitikhmanh ah a rawk lai lo.”—Daniel 2:44. Rammi. Zei bantuk miphun an si ah, khoika a ummi an si ah Pathian duhnak a tuahmi poah cu Pathian Pennak rammi an si kho.—Lamkaltu 10:34, 35. Upadi. Pathian Pennak i upadi (asiloah nawlbia) nih ṭhatlonak tuah kha thlauh lawng si loin rammi pawl i an ziaza zong a ṭhatter chin. Tahchunhnak ah, Baibal nih hitin a ti: “‘Bawipa na Pathian cu na lungthin dihlak le na ruahnak dihlak le na nunnak dihlak in na dawt lai,’ ti hi a ngan bik le a biapi bik nawlbia cu a si. A hun changtu biapi bik nawlbia cu, cu bantuk ṭhiamṭhiam cu a si i, ‘Na innpa cu nangmah naa dawt bantukin na dawt lai,’ ti hi a si.” (Matthai 22:37-39) Pathian le innpa dawtnak nih midang ca ṭhatnak tuah awkah Pennak rammi hna kha a forh hna. Fimcawnnak. Pathian Pennak nih rammi hna caah a sangmi ziazalei phunglam a chiah i mah phunglam ningin nun awkah a cawnpiak hna.—Isaiah 48:17, 18. Rian. Pathian Pennak cu rammi pawl kha fahnak a pe i uktu pawl a rumtermi a si lo. Mah canah Pathian a dawmi hna cu vawleicung paradis ah zungzal in an nung lai timi biakam i telin Pathian duhnak kha a tlinter lai.—Isaiah 35:1, 5, 6; Matthai 6:10; Biathlam 21:1-4.A si lo, Pathian Pennak cu Khrihfa hna i lungthin chungah a ummi men a si lo.* Baibal nih “Vancung Pennak” tiah a auhnak thawngin a umnak hmun kha fiang tein a langhter. (Matthai 4:17) Pathian Pennak cu vancung in a uk dingmi cozah taktak a si tiah Baibal nih a langhtermi kha zohhmanh.  Pathian Pennak ah uktu, ukmi, upadi le nawlngeihnak hna a um. Van le vawlei ah Pathian duhnak tlinter dingin mah nawlngeihnak kha hman a si lai.—Matthai 6:10; Biathlam 5:10.  Pathian cozah asiloah Pennak nih vawleicung i “miphun zakip le holh phun zakip” kha a uk hna lai. (Daniel 7:13, 14) Uknak nawl a ngeimi hna cu rammi nih si loin Pathian nih a thimmi hna an si.—Salm 2:4-6; Isaiah 9:7.  Jesuh nih zumhfekmi lamkaltu hna kha Vancung Pennak ah keimah he “bawiṭhutdan cungah nan ṭhu lai” tiah a ti hna.—Luka 22:28, 30.  Pathian Pennak nih ral a ngei i mah a ral vialte kha a hrawh dih hna lai.—Salm 2:1, 2, 8, 9; 110:1, 2; 1 Korin 15:25, 26.Baibal nih Vancung Pennak cu lungthin chungah a ummi a si i mah nih mi pakhat i lungthin kha a uk tiah a kan cawnpiak lo. Asinain “Vancung Pennak kong” asiloah “Pennak kong thawngṭha” cu minung lungthin cungah huham a ngei kho i a ngeih awk zong a si tiah Baibal nih a langhter.—Matthai 13:19; 24:14.“Pathian Pennak cu nan chungah pei a um cu” timi sullam cu zeidah a si?Baibal lehnak cheukhat i Luka 17:21 bia ruangah Pennak a umnak hmun he aa tlaiin mi cheukhat cu an lung aa tuai. Tahchunhnak ah, “Pathian Pennak cu nan chungah a um” tiah Judson Lehmi Baibal nih a ti. Mah Baibal caang kha a hmaan ning tein hngalhthiam awkah a hnuhmai bia zoh a hau.Pathian Pennak cu Jesuh a ralchanh i thah a timtu hna lungthin chungah a ummi a si loJesuh nih mah bia hi amah a ralchanh i thah a duhmi, biaknaklei hruaitu Farasi mi hna sinah a chimmi a si. (Matthai 12:14; Luka 17:20) Cucaah a lung a khongmi Farasi mi hna lungthin chungah Pathian Pennak um ding cu a si kho hnga maw? Jesuh nih “nan chung cu lih le sualnak in a khat” tiah a ti hna.—Matthai 23:27, 28.A dang Baibal lehnak hna nih Luka 17:21 i Jesuh chimmi bia kha fiang tein hitin an leh: “Pathian Pennak cu nan sinah a um” tiah a ti. (Contemporary English Version) “Pathian Pennak cu nan lakah a um.” (Vawlei Thar Lehnak Baibal) Vancung Pennak cu Farasi hna “nan sinah a um” asiloah “nan lakah a um” tiah a ti tikah Pathian Pennak ah siangpahrang a ṭuan dingmi Jesuh cu an hmaika ah a dirmi kha a chimduhmi a si.—Luka 1:32, 33.Pathian nih zumhfekmi Khrihfa hna lakin mi cheukhat kha milu rikhiah in a thim hna, annih cu an thih hnuah van ah an tho ṭhan lai. (1Peter 1:3,4) Thim a simi hna nih zumhfek tein um peng le an tuahsernak kip ah thiang tein um peng a hau. Cutin a si lo ahcun vancung an ro kha hmuh awkah sining an tlinh kho lai lo.—Efesa 5:5; Filipi 3:12-14.Vancung ah zeidah an tuah lai?Jesuh he kum 1,000 chung siangpahrang le tlangbawi rian an ṭuan lai. (Biathlam 5:9, 10; 20:6) Annih nih “vawlei thar,” asiloah vawlei lei a uk dingmi “van thar,” asiloah vancung cozah kha an dirh lai. Mah lengah Pathian i a hramthawk aa tinhnak ningin mi vialte kha dinnak hmuh ṭhan awkah an bawmh hna lai.—Isaiah 65:17; 2Peter 3:13.Vancung ah a tho ṭhan dingmi cu pa zeizat dah an si?Baibal nih vancung ah a tho ṭhan dingmi cu 144,000 an si tiah a ti. (Biathlam 7:4) Biathlam 14:1-3 ah ṭialmi langhnak ah lamkaltu Johan nih “Zion Tlang i Tuufa a dir komi kha ka hmuh; a sinah cun mi 144,000 an um” tiah a ti. Langhnak chung i “Tuufa” timi cu a tho ṭhanmi Jesuh kha a si. (Johan 1:29; 1Peter 1:19) “Zion Tlang” timi cu Jesuh he vancung ah uktu a ṭuanṭi dingmi 144,000 le Jesuh i a dirhmun kha a si.—Salm 2:6; Hebru 12:22.Pathian Pennak ah Khrih he ukṭi dingin ‘a kawh hna i a thimmi hna’ cu “tuurun hmete” kha an si. (Biathlam 17:14; Luka 12:32) Cucaah Jesuh i a tuu dihlak he tahchunh ahcun annih cu mi tlawmte an si lai ti a fiang.—Johan 10:16.Vancung a kai dingmi hna he aa tlaiin a hmaan lomi ruahnakA hmaan lomi ruahnak: Miṭha vialte vancung an kai dih lai.A hmaanmi: Miṭha tam deuh cu vawleicung ah zungzal in an nung lai tiah Pathian nih bia aa kam.—Salm 37:11, 29, 34.  Jesuh nih “ahohmanh vancung i a kaimi an um bal lo” tiah a ti. (Johan 3:13) Cucaah Jesuh hlanah a thimi Abraham, Moses, Job le David ti bantuk miṭha pawl cu van ah an kai lo ti kha a langhter. (Lamkaltu 2:29, 34) Mah canah vawleicung nunnak ah thawhṭhan dingin ruahchannak an ngei.—Job 14:13-15.  Vancung thawhṭhannak kha “mithi thawhter an si a pakhatnak” tiah auh a si. (Biathlam 20:6) Mah nih a dang thawhṭhannak a um rih ti kha a langhter. Mah cu vawleicung thawhṭhannak a si.  Baibal nih Pathian Pennak uknak tangah cun “thihnak a um ti lai lo” tiah a kan cawnpiak. (Biathlam 21:3,4) Vancung ah cun thihnak a um bal lo caah mah biakam cu vawlei he aa pehtlaimi a si.A hmaan lomi ruahnak: Mikip nih van ah maw kan um lai, vawlei ah dah ti kha an i thim kho.A hmaanmi: ‘Cunglei nunnak i kawhnak,’ phundang cun vancung nunnak cu zei bantuk zumhfekmi Khrihfa hna nih dah an hmuh lai ti kha Pathian lawng nih bia a khiah khawh. (Filipi 3:14) Cucaah thim an simi cu anmah duhnak le hmuitinh ruangah a si lo.—Matthai 20:20-23.A hmaan lomi ruahnak: Vawleicung i zungzal nunnak ruahchannak cu vancung kai awkah aa tlak lomi, a nauta deuhmi pawl pekmi laksawng a si.A hmaanmi: Pathian nih vawleicung ah zungzal nunnak a hmu dingmi hna kha “ka mi” le ‘thluachuah ka pekmi’ tiah a auh hna. (Isaiah 65:21-23) Annih nih vawleicung paradis ah a tlingmi minung in zungzal nun ding timi minung ca i a hramthawk Pathian tinhnak kha tlinternak caanṭha an hmu lai.—Genesis 1:28; Salm 115:16; Isaiah 45:18.A hmaan lomi ruahnak: Biathlam chung i 144,000 cu langhternak nambar men a si, a ca ningin lak khawh a si lo.A hmaanmi: Biathlam cauk ah nambar hna kha langhternak in a hman ko nain nambar cheukhat tu cu a biafang ningin a hman. Tahchunhnak ah, “Tuufa lamkaltu pahleihnih hna min” tiah a langhter. (Biathlam 21:14) Cu bantukin 144,000 zong a ca ningin lak khawh a si tiah biachahnak tuah awkah a ruang ṭha hna a um.Biathlam 7:4 ah “hmelchunhnak an khenhmi [asiloah, vancung nunnak hmu dingin thimmi] hna cu 144,000 an si” tiah a langhter. Mah Baibal caang a cungtang bia ah a pahnihnak phu cu “mibu nganpi, ahohmanh nih a rel in an rel cawk lomi” tiah i thleidang ngaiin a langhter. Mah “mibu nganpi” zong Pathian sinin khamhnak a hmumi an si. (Biathlam 7:9, 10) 144,000 cu langhternak nambar a si i a ca ningin lak khawh lomi a si ahcun mah phu pahnih he aa tlaiin i thleidang ngaiin a langhtermi cu sullam a ngei lai lo.*Mah lengah 144,000 cu ‘minung hna lakin tlanhmi, pekchanh hmasa bikmi’ an si tiah a ti. (Biathlam 14:4) “Pekchanh hmasa bikmi” timi biafang nih mi tlawmpal lawng a simi aiawhtu pawl kha a chim duhmi a si. A rel in rel cawk lomi vawleicung rammi pawl kha vancung in Khrih he a ukṭi dingmi hna he aa tlaiin cutin a langhtermi cu aa tlak tukmi a si.—Biathlam 5:10.Mikhael kha biaknak cheukhat nih “A Thiangmi Mikhael” tiah an auh. Mah min cu Jesuh vawleicung a rat hlan le vancung a kir ṭhan hnu i a min a si.* Moses ruak kong he aa tlaiin Mikhael cu Satan he an i al. Profet Daniel sinah Pathian bia a phuangtu vancungmi kha Mikhael nih a rak bawmh. (Daniel 10:13, 21; Judas9) Mikhael timi min sullam cu—“Ahodah Pathian He Aa Lo?” timi a si. Mah min ningin Mikhael cu Pathian uknaklei ah a ṭang i ral pawl kha a doh hna.—Daniel 12:1; Biathlam 12:7.Jesuh cu vancungmi bawi bik Mikhael a si tiah chim khawh a sinak a ruang kha zohhmanh hna u sih. Mikhael cu “vancungmi lak i upa bik” a si. (Judas9) “Vancungmi bawi bik” ti sullam a ngeimi “vancungmi lak i upa bik” timi upatnak min cu Baibal ah voihnih lawng a langhter. A voihnih ningin pakrelnak (singular) ca lawngah a hman. Cucaah mah upatnak min cu vancungmi pakhat lawng nih a ngeihmi a si ti kha a fiang. Baibal caang pakhat nih a tho ṭhanmi Jesuh he aa tlaiin hitin a ti: “Au thawng, vancungmi bawi bik au thawng, ... cu a hung thang lai i Bawipa hrimhrim cu vancung khin a rung ṭum lai.” (1Thesalon 4:16) Jesuh nih “vancungmi bawi bik au thawng” a chuah khawhmi cu amah hrim hi vancungmi bawi bik Mikhael a si caah a si. Mikhael cu vancung ralkapbu hruaitu a si. “Mikhael le a vancungmi hna nih khan limkeng [Satan] cu an doh.” (Biathlam 12:7) Mikhael cu vancung ah nawl a ngei ngaimi a si caah “vancungmi bawi bik” le “a nganmi vancungmi” tiah auh a si. (Daniel 10:13, 21; 12:1) Mah upatnak min hna ruangah Mikhael cu “vancung ralkapbu hruaitu a hung si” tiah New Testament scholar David E. Aune nih a ti.Vancung ralkapbu cungah nawl a ngeimi a dang min pakhat zong kha Baibal nih a langhter. Hitin a ti: “Bawipa Jesuh cu a vancungmi mi ṭhawng hna le meizik he ... a rung ṭum tikah ding tein a tuah lai.” (2Thesalon 1:7,8; Matthai 16:27) Jesuh cu “vancung ah a kai i Pathian orhlei kam ah a um i vancungmi vialte le vancung nawlngeihnak vialte le ṭhawnnak vialte kha a uk dih hna.” (1Peter 3:21, 22) Pathian nih Jesuh he, Mikhael he vancung ralkapbu hruaitu in rian pek cu a si khawh lo caah mah min pahnih cu mi pakhat ngeihmi a si lai tiah kan chim khawh. Mikhael cu a um bal lomi “harnak ṭhalo bik” a tlun caan ah “a hung chuak lai.” (Daniel 12:1) Daniel cauk chungah “a chuak lai” timi biafang kha thil sining a tawngtham dingmi siangpahrang he aa tlaiin a hman tawn. (Daniel 11:2-4, 21) “Pathian Bia” tiah auhmi Jesuh Khrih nih “siangpahrang vialte Siangpahrang” in Pathian ral vialte kha a hrawh dih hna lai i Pathian miphun kha a huhphenh hna lai. (Biathlam 19:11-16) ‘Vawlei hramthawk in nihin ni tiangah a ummi harnak a zeihmanh nakin a fak deuhmi harnak’ caan ah Jesuh nih cutin a tuah lai.—Matthai 24:21, 42.Khuachia cu a um taktakmi a si. Anih cu a hung ṭhalo i Pathian a ralchanhmi vancungmi a si lengah “hi vawlei uktupa” zong a si. (Johan14:30; Efesa 6:11, 12) Baibal nih a tanglei i min le langhternak hna in Khuachia i a sining kha a phuan:  “Ralchanhtu” ti sullam a ngeimi Satan.—Job 1:6.  “Thangchiattu” ti sullam a ngeimi Khuachia.—Biathlam 12:9.  Baibal nih ‘hlengtu’ in a langhtermi Rul.—2 Korin 11:3.  Tukforhtu.—Matthai 4:3, NW.  Mi lihchim.—Johan 8:44.A ṭhalomi lungput kha a si loMi cheukhat nih Satan Khuachia cu a um taktakmi si loin kan lungthin chungah a ummi a ṭhalomi lungput kha a si tiah an ruah. Asinain Baibal nih Pathian le Satan bia an i ruahnak kong a langhter. Pathian cu a ṭhalomi lungput i telin sualnak zeihmanh a ngei lomi a si. (Deuteronomi 32:4; Job 2:1-6) Satan nih sualnak a ngei lomi Jesuh zong kha a rak tukforh. (Matthai4:8-10; 1 Johan 3:5) Pathian le Jesuh cu an chungah a ummi a ṭhalomi lungput he bia an i ruah ti cu a si kho lomi a si. Cucaah Khuachia cu a um taktakmi a si i a ṭhalomi lungput kha a si lo.Mi tampi nih Khuachia a um taktak ti an zumh lomi cu kan khuaruah a har awk a si maw? A si lo, a ruang cu Satan nih aa tinhnak a tlin khawh nakhnga hlenthawinak kha a hman tiah Baibal nih a ti caah a si. (2Thesalon 2:9, 10) Satan i a hlawh a tling bikmi hlennak pakhat cu a um taktakmi a si kha mi nih an hngalh nakhnga lo an mit a cawttermi hna kha a si.—2Korin 4:4.A hmaan lomi ruahnak: Lucifer cu Khuachia i a min dang a si.A hmaanmi: Baibal cheukhat ah “Lucifer” tiah lehmi Hebru biafang cu “Deirel arfi ceu” ti sullam a ngei. (Isaiah 14:12) Baibal caang a cungtang bia ningin mah biafang nih Babilon siangpahrang hna kha a langhter. An i porhlawt tuk caah Pathian nih a rak hrawh hna. (Isaiah 14:4, 13-20) Babilon siangpahrang hna an tlak hnuah anmah hnehsawhnak in “Deirel arfi ceu” timi biafang cu hman a si. A hmaan lomi ruahnak: Pathian nih Satan hmangin minung an ṭhat le ṭhat lo kha a hnesak hna, mah cungah i hngat in bia a ceih hna.A hmaanmi: Khuachia cu Pathian rianṭuantu si loin Pathian ral a si. Satan Khuachia nih Pathian rian a ṭuanmi hna hmanh kha a ralchanh hna i sual a puh hna.—1Peter 5:8; Biathlam 12:10.Mi nih nunnak sullam kha hngalh an duh caah Minung hi zeitindah kan hun chuah? Nun hnawh chanmi kan ngei maw? tiah biahalnak an tuah. Baibal nih nunnak i aa tinhnak cu Pathian he i hawikomhnak ser ding kha a si tiah a langhter. Baibal nih a langhtermi a hrampi biatak cheukhat hi ruathmanh.  Pathian cu a kan Sertu a si. Baibal nih hitin a ti: “A kan sertu cu amah [Pathian] a si i kannih cu amah ta kan si.”—Salm 100:3; Biathlam 4:11.  Pathian nih kanmah i telin a sermi thil vialte caah tinhnak pakhat a ngei.—Isaiah 45:18.  Pathian nih “thlarau ah michambau” kan si timi hngalhnak he a kan ser. Mah ah nunnak a sullam hngalh duhnak lungthin aa tel. (Matthai 5:3) Mah kan duhnak kha tlinter a duh.—Salm 145:16.  Pathian he hawikom kan sernak thawngin thlaraulei kan chambaunak kha kan tlinter khawh. Pathian he hawikom ser timi cu mi cheukhat caah cun a si kho lomi a lo, asinain Baibal nih hitin a kan forh: “Pathian cu naih u law aan naih ve hna lai.”—Jeim 4:8; 2:23.  Pathian hawi si khawh awkah kan ca i aa tinhnak he aa tlakin kan nun a hau. Phungchimtu 12:13 ah mah aa tinhnak he aa tlaiin hitin a ti: “Pathian cu ṭih law a nawlbia kha zul hna, zeicahtiah minung cu hi nawlbia hna tuah awk caah hin pei rak ser a si cu.”  Hmailei ah Pathian nih sifah harnak vialte a donghter i amah a biami a hawikom pawl zungzal nunnak a pek hna tikah minung ca i a hramthawk Pathian tinhnak a tlinmi kha kan hmuh lai.—Salm 37:10, 11.Baibal nih hitin bia a kan kamh: “Pathian duhnak a tuahmi cu zungzal in an nung.” (1Johan 2:17) Pathian nih zeidah tuah seh ti aan duh?  Pathian le a Fapa Jesuh kong kha cawng. Pathian sin thla a cam lioah Jesuh nih hitin a ti: “Pathian taktak a simi nangmah hngalh le nangmah nih na thlahmi Jesuh Khrih hngalh hi zungzal nunnak cu a si.” (Johan 17:3) Pathian le Jesuh kha zeitindah kan “hngalh” khawh hna? Baibal hlathlainak thawngin le Baibal lamhruainak ningin kan nunnak thawngin kan hngalh khawh hna.* Baibal ah nunnak a kan Petu, Sertu, Jehovah Pathian i a ruahnak hna aa tel. (Lamkaltu 17:24, 25) Cun Baibal ah “zungzal nunnak bia” a kan cawnpiaktu Pathian Fapa, Jesuh kong zong aa tel.—Johan 6:67-69.  Jesuh tlanhnak man raithawinak kha zum. Jesuh vawleicung a ratnak cu ‘mi tampi an rian ṭuanpiak awk le annih tlanhnak caah a nunnak pek awkah’ a si. (Matthai 20:28) Jesuh tlanhnak man raithawinak nih vawlei Paradis ah zungzal nun dingin lam a kan hunpiak.* (Salm 37:29) Jesuh nih hitin a ti: “Pathian nih vawlei hi a dawt hringhran caah a Fapa ngeihchunte kha a pek, cucaah amah a zummi paoh cu an thi lai lo, zungzal nunnak an ngei lai.” (Johan 3:16) Asinain Jesuh zumhnak men lawngin a za lo ti kha philhhlah. ‘Amah kha zumh taktak’ a hau. Cun a cawnpiaknak ningin le a Pa duhnak ning zongin nun a hau.—Matthai 7:21; Jeim 2:17.  Pathian he a ṭhami hawikomhnak ngeih i zuam. Pathian nih ka naih hna sehlaw ka hawikom si hna seh ti a kan duh. (Jeim 2:23; 4:8) Pathian cu zungzal in a nungmi a si. Zeitikhmanh ah a thi bal lo i a hawile zong zungzal in nung hna seh ti a duh. Pathian nih amah a kawlmi vialte hna caah a duhnak kha Baibal ah hitin a langhter: “Zungzal in thluachuah in um ko hna seh.”—Salm 22:26.A Hmaan Lomi Ruahnak: Minung zuamnak thawngin zungzal nunnak hmuh khawh a si.A Hmaanmi: Sii lei ṭhanchonak cheukhat nih minung nunnak cu a sauter khawh deuh ko nain zungzal nunnak hmuh dingin cun an tuah kho lo. Pathian cu “nunnak vialte hram” a si caah amah lawng nih zungzal nunnak a kan pek khawh. (Salm 36:9) Pathian nih ‘thihnak cu zungzal ca in ka hrawh lai’ i zumhfek tein a ummi dihlak kha zungzal nunnak ka pek hna lai tiah bia aa kam.—Isaiah 25:8; 1Johan 2:25.A Hmaan Lomi Ruahnak: Miphun cheukhat lawng zungzal in an nung lai.A Hmaanmi: Pathian cu thleidannak a ngei lo. Mah canah, “mi zei miphun chungmi hmanh a si ah, amah a ṭihmi paoh le dinnak a tuahmi paoh cu a cohlan ko hna.” (Lamkaltu 10:34, 35) Zei bantuk miphun le hnulei nunphung a ngeimi an si hmanhah Pathian nawl a ngaimi vialte cu zungzal nunnak an hmu lai.A Hmaan Lomi Ruahnak: Zungzal nunnak cu mi a simh lai.A Hmaanmi: Zungzal nunnak cu a kan dawtu le i nuam hna seh ti a kan duhtu Pathian sinin a rami a si. (Jeim 1:17; 1Johan 4:8) Pathian nih kan i nuamh nakhnga sullam a ngeimi rian kan herh ti kha a hngalh. (Phungchimtu 3:12) Vawleicung ah zungzal in a nung dingmi hna nih anmah le an dawtmi hna caah ṭhatnak a chuahter hngami, lungsinak a pemi le sullam a ngeimi rian an ngei lai tiah Pathian nih bia aa kam.—Isaiah 65:22, 23.Mah lengah zungzal nunnak a hmumi hna nih Sertu kong le a sermi khuaruahhar thil kong hna kha a thar in an cawn peng rih lai. Minung cu zungzal nun duhnak le Pathian kong hngalh duhnak lungthin he ser kan si. Asinain “Pathian nih a tuahmi kha tling tein hngalh khawhnak kha cu a kan pe lo.” (Phungchimtu 3:10, 11) Cucaah zungzal nunnak a hmumi hna nih hngalh duh awk a simi thil cawn ding le tuah ding an ngei peng lai.Hebru biafang neʹphesh le Greek biafang psy·kheʹ kha Baibal cheukhat ah “thlarau” tiah an leh. Hebru biafang ningin “thaw a ngeimi thilnung” tiah sullam a ngei i Greek biafang ningin “nunnak a ngeimi” tiah sullam a ngei.* Cucaah mah Hebru biafang le Greek biafang nih pum chungah a ummi, thih hnuah a nung rihmi kha a chim duhmi a si lo. A nungmi kha a chim duhmi a si. Cucaah Baibal lehnak tampi nih neʹphesh le psy·kheʹ kha a konglam cungah i hngat in “nunnak,” “minung,” “thilnung” le “keimah” ti bantukin a phunphun in an leh. Baibal nih neʹphesh le psy·kheʹ kha zei bantuk sullam in dah a hman ti kha zohhmanh u sih:Adam cu thlarau pek a si lo—a nungmi mi pakhat a hung si  Jehovah Pathian nih hmasa bik mipa Adam kha a ser tikah “mipa cu a hung nung” tiah Baibal nih a ti. (Genesis 2:7) Cucaah Adam cu thlarau pek a si lo, mah canah nunnak a ngeimi minung a hung si.  Baibal nih thlarau kha rian a ṭuan khomi, thil a khong khomi, a ei khomi, nawlbia a zul khomi le ruak a tawng khomi in a langhter. (Levitikas 5:2; 7:20; 23:30; Deuteronomi 12:20; Rom 13:1, King James Version) Mah tuahsernak hna cu a nungmi minung lawng nih an tuah khawh.Thlarau cu a thi kho lomi a si maw?A si lo, thlarau cu a thi kho. Baibal caang tampi nih thlarau kha a thi khomi in an langhter. Tahchunhnak cheukhat hi zohhmanh u:  “A sualmi thlarau cu a thi lai.”—Ezekiel 18:4, 20, Judson Bible.  Hlanlio Israel chan ah sualnak ngan a tuahmi hna caah dantatnak cu “an thlarau [nunnak] thlei a si.” (Exodus 12:15, 19; Levitikas 7:20, 21, 27; 19:8, King James Version) Mah pa cu “thah a si hrimhrim lai.”—Exodus 31:14.  Baibal caang cheukhat ah miruak caah “a thimi thlarau” timi biafang a hman. (Levitikas 21:11; Nambar 6:6, NW a tanglei fianternak) A hramthawk Hebru holh ah neʹphesh asiloah “thlarau” tiah a hmannak mah Baibal caang hna kha Baibal lehnak tampi nih “miruak” asiloah “mithi” tiah an leh.“Thlarau” cu “nunnak” ti sullam a ngeiBaibal nih “thlarau” kha mah he a sullam aa khatmi “nunnak” ti zongin a hman. Tahchunhnak ah, Job 33:22 ah Hebru biafang “thlarau” (neʹphesh) caah mah he aa lomi “nunnak” kha a hman. Cu bantukin mi pakhat i thlarau asiloah nunnak cu ṭih a nung asiloah a sung kho tiah Baibal nih a langhter.—Exodus 4:19; Biaceihtu 9:17; Filipi 2:30.“Thlarau” cu nunnak timi sullam a ngei ti kha kan hngalhthiam ahcun ‘a thaw a cah pah khin’ tiah aa ṭialmi Baibal caang kha hngalhthiam awkah a kan bawmh lai. (Genesis 35:18) Mah cu langhternak bia a si i mi pakhat nunnak a dongh lai kha a langhtermi a si. Cucaah Baibal lehnak cheukhat nih Genesis 35:18 ah aa telmi mah biafang kha “hmanung bik a thaw” tiah an leh.—Good News Translation; New Jerusalem Bible.A thi kho lomi thlarau zumhnak cu khoika in dah a rat?Khrihfaram hna nih an pommi a thi kho lomi thlarau zumhnak cu Baibal in si loin hlanlio Greek mi hna ruahnak in a rami a si. Encyclopædia Britannica nih hitin a ti: “Thlarau kong he aa tlaiin Baibal langhternak cu thaw dawpnak le chuahnak he aa pehtlai. Hmuh khawh, tawngh khawh a si lomi thlarau le hmuh khawh, tawngh khawh a simi pum tiah aa dang tein a langhter. Pum le thlarau aa khat lo timi Khrihfa zumhnak cu hlanlio Greek mi hna sinin aa thawkmi a si.”Pathian nih a cawnpiaknak ah a thi kho lomi thlarau ti bantuk minung ruahnak hna he fonh a simi kha a ngaithiam lai lo. Baibal nih hitin ralrin a kan pek: “Minung nih pakhat le pakhat an i cawnpiak chin lengmangmi chungin a chuakmi minung fimnak, santlaihnak zeihmanh a ngei lomi fimnak, hlennak menmen a simi cu hmangin, ahohmanh nih sal ah in ser hna hlah seh.”—Kolose 2:8.Pathian nih zumhfekmi Khrihfa hna lakin mi cheukhat kha milu rikhiah in a thim hna, annih cu an thih hnuah van ah an tho ṭhan lai. (1Peter 1:3,4) Thim a simi hna nih zumhfek tein um peng le an tuahsernak kip ah thiang tein um peng a hau. Cutin a si lo ahcun vancung an ro kha hmuh awkah sining an tlinh kho lai lo.—Efesa 5:5; Filipi 3:12-14.Vancung ah zeidah an tuah lai?Jesuh he kum 1,000 chung siangpahrang le tlangbawi rian an ṭuan lai. (Biathlam 5:9, 10; 20:6) Annih nih “vawlei thar,” asiloah vawlei lei a uk dingmi “van thar,” asiloah vancung cozah kha an dirh lai. Mah lengah Pathian i a hramthawk aa tinhnak ningin mi vialte kha dinnak hmuh ṭhan awkah an bawmh hna lai.—Isaiah 65:17; 2Peter 3:13.Vancung ah a tho ṭhan dingmi cu pa zeizat dah an si?Baibal nih vancung ah a tho ṭhan dingmi cu 144,000 an si tiah a ti. (Biathlam 7:4) Biathlam 14:1-3 ah ṭialmi langhnak ah lamkaltu Johan nih “Zion Tlang i Tuufa a dir komi kha ka hmuh; a sinah cun mi 144,000 an um” tiah a ti. Langhnak chung i “Tuufa” timi cu a tho ṭhanmi Jesuh kha a si. (Johan 1:29; 1Peter 1:19) “Zion Tlang” timi cu Jesuh he vancung ah uktu a ṭuanṭi dingmi 144,000 le Jesuh i a dirhmun kha a si.—Salm 2:6; Hebru 12:22.Pathian Pennak ah Khrih he ukṭi dingin ‘a kawh hna i a thimmi hna’ cu “tuurun hmete” kha an si. (Biathlam 17:14; Luka 12:32) Cucaah Jesuh i a tuu dihlak he tahchunh ahcun annih cu mi tlawmte an si lai ti a fiang.—Johan 10:16.Vancung a kai dingmi hna he aa tlaiin a hmaan lomi ruahnakA hmaan lomi ruahnak: Miṭha vialte vancung an kai dih lai.A hmaanmi: Miṭha tam deuh cu vawleicung ah zungzal in an nung lai tiah Pathian nih bia aa kam.—Salm 37:11, 29, 34.  Jesuh nih “ahohmanh vancung i a kaimi an um bal lo” tiah a ti. (Johan 3:13) Cucaah Jesuh hlanah a thimi Abraham, Moses, Job le David ti bantuk miṭha pawl cu van ah an kai lo ti kha a langhter. (Lamkaltu 2:29, 34) Mah canah vawleicung nunnak ah thawhṭhan dingin ruahchannak an ngei.—Job 14:13-15.  Vancung thawhṭhannak kha “mithi thawhter an si a pakhatnak” tiah auh a si. (Biathlam 20:6) Mah nih a dang thawhṭhannak a um rih ti kha a langhter. Mah cu vawleicung thawhṭhannak a si.  Baibal nih Pathian Pennak uknak tangah cun “thihnak a um ti lai lo” tiah a kan cawnpiak. (Biathlam 21:3,4) Vancung ah cun thihnak a um bal lo caah mah biakam cu vawlei he aa pehtlaimi a si.A hmaan lomi ruahnak: Mikip nih van ah maw kan um lai, vawlei ah dah ti kha an i thim kho.A hmaanmi: ‘Cunglei nunnak i kawhnak,’ phundang cun vancung nunnak cu zei bantuk zumhfekmi Khrihfa hna nih dah an hmuh lai ti kha Pathian lawng nih bia a khiah khawh. (Filipi 3:14) Cucaah thim an simi cu anmah duhnak le hmuitinh ruangah a si lo.—Matthai 20:20-23.A hmaan lomi ruahnak: Vawleicung i zungzal nunnak ruahchannak cu vancung kai awkah aa tlak lomi, a nauta deuhmi pawl pekmi laksawng a si.A hmaanmi: Pathian nih vawleicung ah zungzal nunnak a hmu dingmi hna kha “ka mi” le ‘thluachuah ka pekmi’ tiah a auh hna. (Isaiah 65:21-23) Annih nih vawleicung paradis ah a tlingmi minung in zungzal nun ding timi minung ca i a hramthawk Pathian tinhnak kha tlinternak caanṭha an hmu lai.—Genesis 1:28; Salm 115:16; Isaiah 45:18.A hmaan lomi ruahnak: Biathlam chung i 144,000 cu langhternak nambar men a si, a ca ningin lak khawh a si lo.A hmaanmi: Biathlam cauk ah nambar hna kha langhternak in a hman ko nain nambar cheukhat tu cu a biafang ningin a hman. Tahchunhnak ah, “Tuufa lamkaltu pahleihnih hna min” tiah a langhter. (Biathlam 21:14) Cu bantukin 144,000 zong a ca ningin lak khawh a si tiah biachahnak tuah awkah a ruang ṭha hna a um.Biathlam 7:4 ah “hmelchunhnak an khenhmi [asiloah, vancung nunnak hmu dingin thimmi] hna cu 144,000 an si” tiah a langhter. Mah Baibal caang a cungtang bia ah a pahnihnak phu cu “mibu nganpi, ahohmanh nih a rel in an rel cawk lomi” tiah i thleidang ngaiin a langhter. Mah “mibu nganpi” zong Pathian sinin khamhnak a hmumi an si. (Biathlam 7:9, 10) 144,000 cu langhternak nambar a si i a ca ningin lak khawh lomi a si ahcun mah phu pahnih he aa tlaiin i thleidang ngaiin a langhtermi cu sullam a ngei lai lo.*Mah lengah 144,000 cu ‘minung hna lakin tlanhmi, pekchanh hmasa bikmi’ an si tiah a ti. (Biathlam 14:4) “Pekchanh hmasa bikmi” timi biafang nih mi tlawmpal lawng a simi aiawhtu pawl kha a chim duhmi a si. A rel in rel cawk lomi vawleicung rammi pawl kha vancung in Khrih he a ukṭi dingmi hna he aa tlaiin cutin a langhtermi cu aa tlak tukmi a si.—Biathlam 5:10.Baibal ah Greek biafang a·naʹsta·sis kha “thawhṭhannak” tiah a leh. Mah cu “thawhṭhan” asiloah “dir ṭhan” timi sullam a ngei. A tho ṭhanmi pakhat cu thihnak in a hung tho lai i a thih hlan bantuk khan a si ṭhan lai.—1 Korin 15:12, 13.Biakam Hlun tiah auhmi Hebru Baibal ah “thawhṭhannak” timi biafang a um lo nain mah kong he aa tlaiin a chimmi cu a um. Tahchunhnak ah, Job nih hitin a ti: “Mi cu a thih ahcun a nung ṭhan kho lai maw? Cucaah ka rian cu zeitluk in a sau hmanhah ka lung a dong lai lo i Ka luatnak ding cu ka rak hngah ṭheuṭheu ko lai.”—Job 14:13-15; Isaiah 26:19; Daniel 12:2, 13.Mithi cu khoika ah dah an thawhṭhan lai? Mi cheukhat cu Khrih he siangpahrang ṭuanṭi dingin van ah an tho ṭhan lai. (2Korin 5:1; Biathlam 5:9, 10) Baibal nih mah kha “mithi thawhter an si a pakhatnak” tiah a auh caah a dang thawhṭhannak a um rih ti kha kan hngalh khawh. (Biathlam 20:6) Mah thawhṭhannak cu vawleicung ah a si lai. Mi tlawmte lawng van ah thawhter an si lai i tam deuh cu vawlei ah thawhter an si lai.—Salm 37:29.Zeitindah thawhter an si lai? Pathian nih Jesuh kha mithi thawhter khawhnak ṭhawnnak a pek. (Johan 11:25) Jesuh nih “thlan chung i a ummi mithi vialte” kha a nunter ṭhan hna tikah pakhat cio i an sining le cinkennak thluak kha a pek ṭhan hna lai. (Johan 5:28, 29) Van ah thawhter a simi hna cu mit in hmuh khawh lomi thlarau pum in an tho lai. Vawleicung ah thawhter a simi hna cu a ngan a dam i a tlingmi pum in an tho lai.—Isaiah 33:24; 35:5,6; 1Korin 15:42-44, 50.Ahote dah a tho ṭhan lai? Baibal nih “miṭha he, miṭhalo he thihnak in kan tho ṭhan dih lai” tiah a ti. (Lamkaltu 24:15) Miṭha timi ah Noah, Sarah le Abraham ti bantuk zumhfekmi hna an i tel. (Genesis 6:9; Hebru 11:11; Jeim 2:21) Miṭhalo timi ah Pathian phunglam cawn awk le zulh awkah caanṭha hmu loin a thimi hna an i tel.Asinain sualnak a tuah i a nunning aa thleng lomi hna cu an tho ṭhan ti lai lo. Cu bantuk mi hna cu an thih tikah zungzal in hrawh an si i thawhṭhannak ruahchannak an ngei lo.—Matthai 23:33; Hebru 10:26, 27.Zeitik ah dah thawhter an si lai? Van ah a tho ṭhan dingmi hna cu 1914 in aa thawkmi, Khrih a rat caan chungah an tho lai tiah Baibal nih a chimchung. (1Korin 15:21-23) Vawleicung ah a tho ṭhan dingmi hna cu Jesuh Khrih Kum Thongkhat Uknak chungah an tho ṭhan lai. Mah tikah vawlei pumpi cu aa dawh tukmi Paradis ah a cang ṭhan lai.—Luka 23:43; Biathlam 20:6, 12, 13.Zeicah thawhṭhannak cu zumh awk a tlak? Baibal nih mit in hmuhmi a thoṭhanmi minung pakua kong kha a dikthiar in a chim. (1Siangpahrang 17:17-24; 2Siangpahrang 4:32-37; 13:20, 21; Luka 7:11-17; 8:40-56; Johan 11:38-44; Lamkaltu 9:36-42; Lamkaltu 20:7-12; 1Korin 15:3-6) Jesuh nih Lazaruh a thawhtermi cu a hleiin cinken awk tlak a si. A thihnak in nili hnuah mibu hmaiah Jesuh nih khuaruahhar lam in a thawhter. (Johan 11:39, 42) Jesuh a ralchanhtu hna hmanh nih mah kha an al kho lo. Cucaah Jesuh le Lazaruh kha thah ding hmanhin khua an khan.—Johan 11:47, 53; 12:9-11.Pathian nih mithi a thawhter khawh hna i thawhter zong a duh hna ti kha Baibal nih a langhter. Pathian nih ri a ngei lomi cinkennak a thluak chungah thawhter a duhmi hna i an konglam a dikthliar kha aa cinken. Annih kha a ṭhawnnak hmangin a thawhter ṭhan hna lai. (Job 37:23; Matthai 10:30; Luka 20:37, 38) Pathian nih mithi kha a thawhter khawh hna i thawhter zong a duh hna. Hmailei thawhṭhannak kong Baibal nih a chim tikah Pathian kong he aa tlaiin hitin a ti: “Na kut tuahmi thil cu hmuh na ka duh lai.”—Job 14:15.Thawhṭhannak he aa tlaiin a hmaan lomi ruahnak hnaA hmaan lomi ruahnak: Thawhṭhannak timi cu pum le thlarau aa fonh ṭhanmi kha a si.A hmaanmi: Baibal ningin mi pakhat cu a thih tikah a um ti lo, a thi kho lomi thlarau zong a um lo. (Phungchimtu 9:5, 10) Cucaah mi pakhat a thawhṭhan tikah pum le thlarau fonh ṭhanmi kha a si lo. Pathian nih a thar in a ser ṭhanmi a si. A hmaan lomi ruahnak: Mi cheukhat cu an thawhle cangka in hrawh ṭhan colh an si lai.A hmaanmi:  Baibal nih “ṭhatlonak a tuahmi kha an tho ve lai i sualphawt an si lai” tiah a ti. (Johan 5:29) Asinain mah biaceihnak cu an thih hlan i an rak tuahmi cungah si loin an thawhṭhan hnu i an tuahmi thil cungah aa hngat lai. Jesuh nih hitin a ti: “Biatak kaan chimh hna, mithi nih Pathian Fapa aw an theih i a thimi paoh an nun lainak caan kha a ra lio i a phan cang.” (Johan 5:25) An thawhṭhan hnuah an cawnmi kong ‘a theimi’ asiloah a zulmi hna cu “nunnak cauk” chungah an min khumh a si lai.—Biathlam 20:12, 13.A hmaan lomi ruahnak: An thawhṭhan tikah a hmasa an pum thengte in an tho ṭhan lai.A hmaanmi: Mi pakhat a thih tikah a pum cu duhsah tein a rawk i a tlau.—Phungchimtu 3:19, 20.Tuchan ah a cangmi leiser ral hi Pathian nih a chuahtermi a si lo, asinain leiser ral a tongmi hna cungah zaangfahnak a ngei. Pathian Pennak nih a hrawh dingmi thil hna lakah leiser ral cu pakhat a si ve. Atu zongah Pathian nih leiser ral ruangah harnak a tongmi hna kha hnemhnak a pek hna.—2Korin 1:3.Leiser ral cu Pathian dantatnak a si lo tiah zeicah kan ti khawh?Leiser ral cu donghnak caan i hmelchunhnak pakhat a si maw?Leiser ral a tongmi hna kha Pathian nih zeitindah a bawmh hna?Leiser ral caah i timhchung dingin Baibal nih a kan bawm kho maw?Leiser ral a tongmi pawl hnemhnak a pemi Baibal caang hnaLeiser ral le Baibal ah langhtermi Pathian hmanmi ṭhawnnak cu aa dang. Leiser ral nih cun zeithil poah kha a hrawh dih hna. Asinain Pathian nih a ṭhawnnak hmangin dan a tat hna tikah miṭhalo pawl lawng a hrawh hna. Tahchunhnak ah, Pathian nih hlanlio Sodom le Gomorrah khua a hrawh lioah miṭha a simi Lot le a fanule pahnih kha a rak khamh hna.
