(Genesis 19:29, 30) Pathian nih pakhat cio i an lungthin kha a hngalh i miṭhalo tiah a hmuhmi hna lawng kha a hrawh hna.—Genesis 18:23-32; 1Samuel 16:7. Leiser ral cu ralrinnak pek hmasa loin a chuak tawn. Asinain Pathian nih cun miṭhalo pawl kha a hrawh hna hlanah ralrinnak a pek hmasa hna. Mah ralrin peknak a zulmi hna cu luatnak caanṭha an hmu.—Genesis 7:1-5; Matthai 24:38, 39. Minung ruangah leiser ral a chuak tawn. Zeitin in dah? Pawngkam thil hna an hrawhnak thawngin le lihnin, tilian le khuacaan a chiatnak hmun hna ah inn an saknak thawngin a si. (Biathlam 11:18) Cu bantuk minung tuahsernak hna ruangah Pathian kha mawhchiat awk a si lo.—Phungthlukbia 19:3.A si. Baibal nih “chan donghnak” asiloah “ni hmanung bik” caan chungah leiser ral a um lai tiah a chim chung. (Matthai 24:3; 2Timote 3:1) Tahchunhnak ah, atu kan chan he aa tlaiin Jesuh nih hitin a ti: “A kenkip ah mangṭam le lihnin a tlung lai.” (Matthai 24:7) A rauhhlan ah Pathian nih leiser ral i telin sifah harnak vialte kha a hrawh dih cang lai.—Biathlam 21:3,4.Pathian nih Baibal hmangin a hnemh hna. Pathian nih a kan dawt caah harnak kan ton tikah a ngaih a chia tiah Baibal nih a ti. (Isaiah 63:9; 1Peter 5:6,7) Cun hmailei ah leiser ral a um ti lai lo ti zongin bia a kan kamh.—“Leiser ral a tongmi pawl hnemhnak a pemi Baibal caang hna” timi ah zoh. Pathian nih harnak a tongmi hna kha amah a biami hna hmangin a bawmh hna.  Pathian nih Jesuh aa zohchunhmi vawleicung i amah a biatu hna kha a hman hna. Jesuh nih “lung a kuaimi” le “a ngaih a chiami” kha a hnemh hna lai tiah Baibal nih a chimchung. (Isaiah 61:1,2) Pathian a biami hna zong nih cutin an tuah ve.—Johan 13:15.Pathian nih harnak a tongmi pawl an herhmi thilri bawmh awkah amah a biatu hna kha a hman hna.—Lamkaltu 11:28-30; Galati 6:10.A kan bawmh khawh. Baibal cu leiser ral ca, i timhchungnak caah ṭialmi a si lo nain mah ah bawmhnak a kan pe khomi phunglam pawl a um. Tahchunhnak ah: Leiser ral a chuah tikah zeidah tuah ding timi timhtuahnak ngei. “Mifim nih cun harnak a rat kha a hmuh tikah hrial khawhnak aa zuam” tiah Baibal nih a ti. (Phungthlukbia 22:3) Harnak kan ton hlanin zeidah tuah ding timi timhtuahnak ngeih cu fim a si. Mah i timhtuahnak ah i tlikpi khawh colh dingmi, a herhmi thil pawl sanhmi bag i chiah cia ding le i tonnak ding hmun chimh cianak aa tel. Thilri chawva nakin nunnak kha sunsak deuh. Baibal nih hitin a ti: “Zeidah vawlei ah hin kan hun i chuahpi? Zeihmanh kan i chuahpi lo. Cu bantukin hi vawlei in kan kal tik zongah zeihmanh kan i kalpi kho lai lo.” (1Timote 6:7,8) Lerser ral in kan luat nakhnga kan inn le thilri chawva pawl kha kaltak a hau men lai. Thilri chawva nakin kan nunnak cu a biapi deuh tukmi a si ti kha kan i cinken awk a si.—Matthai 6:25.Baibal nih donghnak caan ah zawtnak (pul rai i telin chawnh khawhmi zawtnak) a tlung lai tiah a chimchung. (Luka 21:11) Cu bantuk pul rai cu Pathian sinin a rami dantatnak a si lo. A tak ti ahcun a Pennak thawngin Pathian nih a rauhhlan ah pul rai i telin zawtnak vialte kha a hloh dih cang lai.Baibal nih pul rai he aa tlaiin a chimchung maw?Pathian nih zawtnak in mi kha dan a tat bal hna maw?Tuchan i pul rai cu Pathian sinin a rami dantatnak a si maw?Pul rai hi a dong te lai maw?Zawtnak he aa tlaimi Baibal caang hnaBaibal nih COVID-19, AIDS le Spain raifanh ti bantuk pul rai asiloah zawtnak he aa tlaiin cuset khaset in cun a chimchung lo. Asinain “ngal-eu zawtnak” le “rai” a tlung lai tiah a chimchung. (Luka 21:11; Biathlam 6:8) Mah cu “ni hmanung bik” asiloah “atu chan donghnak ding hmelchunhnak” lakah aa telmi an si.—2 Timote 3:1; Matthai 24:3.Thil sining cheukhat ah Pathian nih mi pawl dantat awkah zawtnak a hmannak kong kha Baibal nih a langhter. Tahchunhnak ah, mi cheukhat kha thinghmui zawtnak in dan a tat hna. (Nambar 12:1-16; 2Siangpahrang 5:20-27; 2Chanrelnak 26:16-21) Asinain cu bantuk dantatnak cu sualnak a ngei lomi hna cungah a tlung lo. Mah canah Pathian a ralchanhmi hna cung lawngah a tlungmi dantatnak a si.A si lo. Mi cheukhat nih mi pawl dantat awkah Pathian nih pul rai le a dang zawtnak hna a hman tiah an ti. Asinain Baibal nih cutin a chim lo. Zeicah?A ruang pakhat cu hlanlio ah siseh, atu ah siseh Pathian a biami cheukhat cu zawtfahnak an tong. Tahchunhnak ah, zumhfekmi Timote cu ‘a paw a fak lengmang.’ (1Timote 5:23) Asinain Baibal nih mah cu Pathian mithmaiṭha sunghnak hmelchunh a si tiah a chim lo. Cu bantukin tuchan i zumhfekmi Pathian salle cheukhat zong zawtfahnak an tong. Thil sining tam deuh ahcun aa tlak lomi caan le aa tlak lomi hmun i an um caah a si.—Phungchimtu 9:11.Mah lengah Pathian nih mi ṭhalo pawl dan a tat hna lainak caan cu a phan rih lo tiah Baibal nih a kan cawnpiak. Mah canah kannih cu “khamhnak hmuh ni” ah kan nung—mah cu Pathian nih amah he i naih awk le khamhnak hmuh awkah mi vialte a sawm hnanak caan kha a si. (2Korin 6:2) Cutin a sawm hnanak lamkhat cu vawleicung pumpi ah “Pennak kong Thawngṭha” chimnak thawngin a si.”—Matthai 24:14.A dong lai. Baibal nih zawtnak a um ti lai lonak caan a phan lai tiah a chimchung. A Pennak uknak tangah Pathian nih zawtnak vialte a hloh dih cang lai. (Isaiah 33:24; 35:5, 6) Ngaihchiatnak, fahnak le thihnak hna a hloh dih cang lai. (Biathlam 21:4) Cun a thimi hna zong kha a tlingmi uknak tang i hi vawlei ah ngandam tein an nun khawh nakhnga a thawhter ṭhan hna lai.—Salm 37:29; Lamkaltu 24:15.Matthai 4:23: “Jesuh cu Galili ram dihlak ah khan aa chawk i an pumhnak inn ah khan a cawnpiak hna i Vancung Pennak Thawngṭha Bia kha a chimh hna i zawtnak le fahnak a ingmi a phunphun kha a damter hna.”A sullam: Jesuh tuahmi khuaruahhar thil cu a rauhhlan ah Pathian Pennak nih minung caah a tuah hngami thil hna muithlam a si.Luka 21:11: “Ngal-eu zawtnak a tlung lai.”A sullam: Chawnh khawhmi zawtnak cu ni hmanung bik hmelchunhnak lakah aa tel ve.Biathlam 6:8: “Ka hun zoh i rang rau diapduap pakhat ka hmuh. A cung i aa citmi cu a min ah Thihnak a si i Hell nih a hnulei in a zulh. . . . uknak nawl kha pek an si i . . . rai in . . . mi thah khawhnak nawl kha pek an si.”A sullam: Biathlam cauk chung i rang aa citmi pali nih atu kan chan ah a tlung dingmi rai hna kha an langhter.Mah biahalnak a tuahmi hna cu sunghnak nganpi a tongmi an si caah a phi hngalh le hnemhnak a herhmi an si. Cheukhat nih mi tampi thahnak cu minung ṭhatlonak lakah a sang bikmi a si tiah an hmuh. Cucaah Pathian kha zumh awkah an i harh.A hmaan lomi ruahnak: Mi tampi thahnak hi zeicah Pathian nih umnak nawl a awnh ti biahalnak tuah cu a palh.A hmaanmi: Zumhfekmi hna zong nih zeicah Pathian nih ṭhatlonak umnak nawl a awnh timi biahalnak kha an rak tuah. Tahchunhnak ah, profet Habakkuk nih Pathian kha hitin a rak hal: “Zeicahdah ṭhatlonak hi vialte hi na ka hmuhter ... ? Rawhralnak le zaang-ennak nih an ka chuah hnawh.” (Habakkuk 1:3) Mah tikah Pathian nih Habakkuk kha sualphawt canah mah a biahalnak kha mi vialte nih rel khawh awkah Baibal ah a ṭialter. A hmaan lomi ruahnak: Minung tonmi sifah harnak hi Pathian nih zei ah a rel lo.A hmaanmi: Pathian nih ṭhatlonak le mah ruangah a chuakmi harnak hna kha a huat. (Phungthlukbia 6:16-19) Noah chan ah vawleicung i a karhmi ṭhatlonak ruangah Pathian cu “a ngaih a chia.” (Genesis 6:5, 6) Cucaah Mi Tampi Thahnak he aa tlai zongin Pathian cu a ngaih a chia tuk lai ti a fiang.—Malakhi 3:6. A hmaan lomi ruahnak: Mi Tampi Thahnak cu Pathian nih Judah mi dan a tat hnanak a si.A hmaanmi: Kumzabu pakhatnak ah Pathian nih Rom mi kha Jerusalem khua hrawhnak nawl a rak awnh hna. (Matthai 23:37–24:2) Mah caan thawkin Pathian nih miphun pakhat kha a hleiin mithmai ṭha a pe ti lo asiloah dan a tat ti lo. Pathian hmuhnak ah “Judah mi le Jentail mi tiin i thleidannak zeihmanh a um lo.”—Rom 10:12. A hmaan lomi ruahnak: Dawtnak le ṭhawnnak tling a ngeimi Pathian a um ahcun Mi Tampi Thahnak a um nakhnga lo a tuah ko lai.A hmaanmi: Pathian nih sifah harnak hi a chuahtermi a si lo nain a caan ah chikkhat umnak nawl a awnh.—Jeim 1:13; 5:11.Pathian nih minung tonmi sifah harnak umnak nawl a awnh caah Mi Tampi Thahnak zong umnak nawl a awnhmi a si. Mah cu a hramthawk minung hna sinin aa thawkmi a hmaan, hmaanlo kong tawnghthamnak caah a si. Baibal nih atu vawlei uktu cu Pathian si loin Satan a si tiah fiang tein a langhter. (Luka 4:1, 2, 6; Johan 12:31) Baibal nih a langhtermi a hrampi a kong pahnih nih Mi Tampi Thahnak Pathian nih umnak nawl a awnhnak a ruang kha a fianter. Pathian nih minung a ser tikah zalong tein thimnak nawl a pek. Pathian nih hmasa bik minung, Adam le Evi sinin zeidah aa ruahchan ti kha a chimh hna nain a nawl ngaih awkah a hnek hna lo. Anmah tein a ṭha le a chia kha an i thim. A ṭha lomi an i thim ruang—le minung tuanbia ah anmah bantukin a ṭhalomi aa thimmi hna ruangah harnak a chuak. (Genesis 2:17; 3:6; Rom 5:12) Cauk pakhat (Statement of Principles of Conservative Judaism) nih hitin a ti: “Vawleicung i a ummi sifah harnak tam deuh cu pek kan simi zalong tein thimnak nawl kha ningcang loin kan hman caah a si.” Pathian nih kan zalonnak kha lakpiak ṭhan canah amah tel loin minung kha mah tein i tlangtlak awkah caan a pek. Mi Tampi Thahnak ruangah a chuakmi sunghnak vialte kha Pathian nih a tawnghtham khawh i a tawngh zong a tawnghtham lai. Mi Tampi Thahnak ah thah a tongmi hna i telin mithi nuai tampi kha Pathian nih ka nunter ṭhan hna lai tiah bia aa kam. Mi Tampi Thahnak in a luatmi nih an tonmi ṭih a nung tukmi hmuhtonnak hna zong a philhter hna lai. (Isaiah 65:17; Lamkaltu 24:15) Minung cung i Pathian dawtnak nih mah biakam a tling lai ti kha a kan zumhter.—Johan 3:16.Mi Tampi Thahnak in a luatmi hna cu Pathian nih ṭhatlonak umnak a awnhnak a ruang le mah ruangah a chuakmi thil hna kha a tawnghtham lai timi hngalhnak nih zumhfek tein um peng awkah a bawmh hna.Aan bawmh khawh! Baibal cu “lung a dongmi lung ṭhawnnak a pe tawntu Pathian” sinin a rami a si. (2Korin 7:6) Baibal cu lungthinlei ngandamnak cauk a si lo nain mahle mah i thah duhnak lungput kha tei awkah aan bawmh khawh. Mah ah aa telmi zulh awk tlak ruahnak cheuhnak hna nih aan bawmh khawh.Baibal ah zulh awk a tlakmi zei ruahnak cheuhnak dah a um?Baibal nih thih a duhmi hna kong kha a langhter maw?Zei Baibal caang nih dah mahle mah i thah duhnak kha tei awkah aan bawmh?Kan hawi pakhat nih “thih ka duh” tiah a ti ah tah zeitin?Mahle mah i thah dingin aa tim balmi ka si ah tah zeitin?● Na intuarnak kha phuang.Baibal chimmi: “Hawikom nih cun zei tik paohah dawt zungzal a si, u le nau cu harnak i hrawm awkah hrin kan si.”—Phungthlukbia 17:17.A sullam: Lungthinlei in fahnak kan tuar tikah midang sinin bawmhnak kan herh.Kan intuarnak kha kan phuan lo ahcun inkhawh ti lo tiangin kan caah thilrit a hung si kho. Asinain na intuarnak kha na phuan ahcun na inmi fahnak a zor deuh lai i hrimhnak na hmu lai.Mah hi tuahchunh: Na chungkharmi asiloah na zumhmi na hawi pakhatkhat sinah tuni ah phuang colh.* Na intuarnak kong kha ca in ṭialnak thawng zongin cutin na tuah khawh.● Siilei in bawmhnak hal hna.Baibal chimmi: “A dammi nih cun siibawi an herh lo, a zawmi lawng nih khan an herh.”—Matthai 9:12.A sullam: Kan zawt tikah sii thlop kan hau.Mahle mah i thah duhnak lungput cu lungthinlei zawtnak hmelchunh a si. Pumsalei zawtnak bantuk a si caah ningzah awk a si lo. Lungthinlei zawtnak cu thlop khawh a si ko.Mah hi tuahchunh: A thiammi siibawi sinah a rannak in bawmhnak hal.● Pathian nih aan zohkhenh ti kha philh hlah.Baibal chimmi: “Pithlung panga cu pia hnih ah an zuar hna a si lo maw? Asinain an lak i pakhat hmanh khi Pathian nih a philhmi hna an um lo. Nan lu cung samfa hmanh kha a rel dih hna. Cucaah nan thinphang hlah u: pithlung tampi nakin pei nan sun deuh cu!”—Luka 12:6,7.A sullam: Pathian caah na sunglawi tuk.Na li a leng ko lai nain Pathian nih na tonmi thil kha a hmuh dih. Nun duhnak lungthin na ngeih ti lo hmanhah aan dawt. Salm 51:17 (NW) ah “a kekkuaimi lungthin hi na hlaw lai lo” tiah a ti. Pathian nih aan dawt caah nunter aan duh rih.Mah hi tuahchunh: Pathian nih aan dawt ti a langhtermi kong kha Baibal ah kawl. Tahchunhnak ah, Jehovah kha Naih timi cauk, ṭhen 24 [Kawl] kha zoh.● Pathian sinah thla cam.Baibal chimmi: “Amah nih aan zohkhenh hna caah nan lungretheihnak vialte kha amah cungah chia dih ko u.”—1Peter 5:7.A sullam: Pathian nih na intuarnak le na lungretheihnak vialte kha a sinah phuang seh ti aan duh.Pathian nih lungdaihnak le inkhawhnak ngeih awkah thazaang aan pek khawh. (Filipi 4:6, 7, 13) Cuticun lungtak tein amah a kawlmi hna kha a bawmh hna.—Salm 55:22.Mah hi tuahchunh: Tuni hrimhrim ah Pathian sinah thlacam. A min Jehovah kha hmang law na intuarnak vialte kha chim. (Salm 83:18) Inkhawhnak ngeih peng awkah bawmhnak hal.● Hmailei he aa tlaimi Baibal ruahchannak kong kha ruat.Baibal chimmi: “Hi ruahchannak hi kan nunnak caah a fekmi le a ṭhawngmi thir cangai bantuk a si.”—Hebru 6:19.A sullam: Na intuarnak cu thlichia nih khatlei, khatlei ah a choihmi tilawng bantuk a si kho, asinain Baibal ruahchannak nih lungdai tein um awkah aan bawmh khawh.Mah ruahchannak cu saduhthah men a si lo, fahnak kan inmi vialte kaan hlohpiak hna lai timi Pathian biakam cungah aa hngatmi a si.—Biathlam 21:4.Mah hi tuahchunh: Baibal ah aa telmi ruahchannak kong kha tam deuh hngalh awkah Pathian Sinin A Rami Thawngṭha brochure, ṭhen 5nak kha rel.● Aan nuamhtermi thil hna kha tuah.Baibal chimmi: “Lungthin lawmh hi siiṭha a si.”—Phungthlukbia 17:22.A sullam: A kan lawmhtermi thil kan tuah tikah lungthinlei asiloah ruahnaklei in ṭhatnak kan hmu.Mah hi tuahchunh: Nuamhnak aan pe kho hngami thil pakhatkhat kha tuah. Tahchunhnak ah, lungṭhawnnak a pemi music kha ngai, thazaang a pemi ca kha rel asiloah na huammi thil kha tuah. Cun thil hmete a si hmanhah midang na bawmh hna tikah naa nuam deuh ve lai.—Lamkaltu 20:35.● Pumsalei ah ngandam i zuam.Baibal chimmi: “Pum cawlcanghnak nih ṭhatnak tlawmpal a chuahter.”—1Timote 4:8, NW.A sullam: Pum cawlcanghnak kan tuah tik, kan mitku a vuai tik le ngandamnak a pemi rawl kan ei tikah ṭhatnak kan hmu.Mah hi tuahchunh: Minit 15 chung tal lam i chawk.● Kan intuarnak le kan sining cu aa thleng kho ti kha i cinken.Baibal chimmi: “Thaizing ah na nunnak cu zei a lawh lai hmanh na hngalh ṭung lo.”—Jeim 4:14.A sullam: Uk khawh dawh a si lomi lungretheihnak hna hmanh chikkhat lawng an um kho.Tuni ah na lung a dong tuk ko lai nain thaizing ah aa thleng kho. Cucaah tawnghtham khawhnak lam kha kawl. (2Korin 4:8) Lungretheihnak hna cu a caan a cut tikah aa thleng kho. Mahle mah i thahnak cu khirh ṭhan khawh a si ti lo.Mah hi tuahchunh: Baibal chung i langhtermi, an lung a dongh tuk caah thih hmanh a duhmi hna kong kha rel. An hngalh chung khawh lomi lam in a ṭhatnaklei in an sining aa thlen ning kha hlathlai. An lak i cheukhat kong hi zohhmanh.A langhter. Baibal nih “thih ka duh” tiah a chimmi kong cheukhat kha a langhter. Pathian nih a rak mawhchiat hna lo, bawmhnak tu a rak pek hna. Nangmah cung zongah cutin a tuah khawh ve. Elijah● Anih cu ahodah a si? Elijah cu a ral a ṭhami profet pakhat a si. Asinain a lung a rak dong tuk. Jeim 5:17 ah “Elijah kha kanmah bantuk minung a si ve ko” tiah a ti.● Zeicah thih a duh? Voikhat cu, Elijah nih keimah lawng ka si timi ruahnak, ṭihnak le man ka ngei lo timi lungput a ngei. Cucaah “Maw BAWIPA, ka nunnak kha la ko” tiah a rak ti.—1Siangpahrang 19:4.● Zeinihdah a bawmh? Elijah nih a intuarnak vialte kha Pathian sinah a phuan. Pathian nih zeitindah thazaang a pek? Pathian nih a cungah siaherhnak a ngeih le a ṭhawnnak zeitluk in dah a ngan ti kha a hmuhsak. Cun Elijah cu a caah man ngeimi a si kha a zumhter lengah bawmhnak zong a rak pek.▸ Elijah kong kha rel: 1Siangpahrang 19:2-18.Job● Anih cu ahodah a si? Job cu zumhfek tein Pathian a biami, chungkhar nganpi a ngeimi mirum pakhat a si.● Zeicah thih a duh? Job nunnak cu ruahlopi in a chiatnaklei ah aa thleng. A ngeihmi thil vialte a sung dih. Leiser ral ruangah a fale an dihlak in an thi. Amah theng fih a nungmi zawtnak nih a tlunh. A donghnak ah a tonmi harnak he aa tlaiin a hmaan loin sualphawt a si. Job nih hitin a ti: “Ka hnabei a dong, nun hi ka duh ti lo.”—Job 7:16.● Zeinihdah a bawmh? Job cu Pathian sinah thla a cam i midang kha bia a ruah hna. (Job 10:1-3) Zaangfahnak a ngeimi a hawi, Elihu nih thazaang a pek i a sining kha lamdang in hmuh awkah a bawmh. Mah lengah Job nih Pathian sinin a rami ruahnak cheuhnak le bawmhnak kha cohlang.▸ Job kong kha rel: Job 1:1-3, 13-22; 2:7; 3:1-13; 36:1-7; 38:1-3; 42:1, 2, 10-13.Moses● Anih cu ahodah a si? Moses cu hlanlio Israel mi hruaitu le zumhfekmi profet a si.● Zeicah thih a duh? Moses cu ṭuan ding rian tampi a ngeih lengah atu le atu an zaihnawh caah a lung a dong. Cucaah “hmakhatte ah ka that ko” tiah Pathian kha a rak nawl.—Nambar 11:11, 15.● Zeinihdah a bawmh? Moses nih a intuar ning kha Pathian a chimh. Pathian nih a retheihnak zanter awkah a rian kha a tlawmter deuh.▸ Moses kong kha rel: Nambar 11:4-6, 10-17.Aan bawmh khawh. Pathian nih a zawmi a salle kha a zohkhenh hna. Zumhfekmi a salle kong he aa tlaiin Baibal nih hitin a ti: “A zawt tikah BAWIPA nih a bawmh lai i a damter ṭhan lai.” (Salm 41:3) Caan saupi a zawmi na si ahcun inkhawh awkah a tanglei i a kong pathum nih aan bawmh khawh: Inkhawhnak ngeih awkah thla cam. “Pathian daihnak, minung hngalhnak a lonhtu” kha na hmuh lai, mah nih na lungretheihnak kha a zorter khawh i lungdaihnak aan pek khawh.—Filipi 4:6, 7. A ṭhatnak in hmuhnak ngei. Baibal nih hitin a ti: “Lungthin lawmh hi sii ṭha a si, sihmanhsehlaw lungthin ngaihchia nih ruh kha a roter.” (Phungthlukbia 17:22) Nuam tein um khawh i zuam, mah nih na ngaihchiatnak kha a zorter deuh lai i na ngandamnak zong a ṭhatter deuh lai. Hmailei naa ruahchannak kha fehter. A ṭhami ruahchannak nih caan saupi na zawt hmanhah i nuamh awkah aan bawmh khawh. (Rom 12:12) Baibal nih hmailei caan kong he aa tlaiin hitin a chimchung: “Kan ram i a ummi cu ka zaw tiah an zai ti lai lo.” (Isaiah 33:24) Chan thar science fimnak nih a damh khawh lomi zawtnak hna kha Pathian nih a hloh cang lai. Tahchunhnak ah, Baibal nih tar an no ṭhan lai timi he aa tlaiin hitin a ti: “Cu pa cu a tlanval lio nak khan a titsa a ṭha deuh lai i a ṭhawn siling te ah khan a kir ṭhan lai.”—Job 33:25.Cinken awk: Jehovah Tehte Hna nih Pathian bawmhnak kha an i bochan ko nain caan saupi zawtnak he aa tlaimi siithlopnak zong an cohlan. (Marka 2:17) Asinain siithlop ning pakhatkhat he aa tlaiin hnatlaknak kan tuahmi cu a um lo; pakhat cio nih mah tein biakhiahnak tuah awk a si ti kha kan hngalh.Biaknak vialte hi aa lo dih lo. Baibal ah Pathian nih a cohlan lomi biaknak tampi kong a langhter. Pathian nih a cohlan lonak a ruang pahnih a um.A ruang 1: A hmaan lomi pathian biaknakBaibal nih a hmaan lomi pathian biaknak kha “hlennak men,” “pakpalawng,” le “santlai lomi” timi biafang hna in a langhter. (Jeremiah 10:3-5; 16:19, 20) Jehovah* Pathian nih hlanlio Israel mi kha hitin nawl a pek hna: “Keimah hleiin pathian dang zeihmanh nan bia lai lo.” (Exodus 20:3, 23; 23:24) Israel mi nih pathian dang hna an biak tikah ‘BAWIPA thinhunnak cu an cungah a alh.’—Nambar 25:3; Levitikas 20:2; Biaceihtu 2:13, 14.Tuchan zongah “pathian timi” hna biaknak he aa tlaiin Pathian hmuhnak cu aa thleng rih lo. (1Korin 8:5,6; Galati 4:8) Amah a biami hna kha a hmaan lomi pathian a biami hna he i komh lo awkah nawl a pek hna i “annih cu nan kaltak hrimhrim hna lai i an sin cun nan i ṭhen hrimhrim lai” tiah a ti hna. (2Korin 6:14-17) Biaknak vialte cu aa lawh dih i Pathian nih a cohlan dih ahcun zeicah mah nawlbia cu a pek hna lai?A ruang 2: Pathian nih a cohlan lomi lam in biaknakA caan ah Israel mi nih a hmaan lomi biaknak in a rami zumhnak le phunglam hna kha hmangin Jehovah Pathian kha an biak. Asinain a hmaan lomi biaknak he i cawhkalh kha Pathian nih a duh lo. (Exodus 32:8; Deuteronomi 12:2-4) Jesuh nih a chan i biaknaklei hruaitu hna kha Pathian an biak ning he aa tlaiin a mawhchiat hna; biaknak a ṭanhmi bantukin nan i umter i “Nawlbia nih biapi taktak a si a timi dinnak le mi zaangfahnak le zumhtlakmi sinak hna cu zeihmanh ah nan rel ṭung lo” tiah a ti hna.—Matthai 23:23.Cu bantukin tuchan zongah Pathian nih biatak cungah hram aa bunhmi a hmaanmi biaknak pakhat lawng kha a cohlan. Mah biatak cu Baibal ah hmuh khawh a si. (Johan 4:24; 17:17; 2Timote 3:16, 17) Baibal he i ralkah in mi a cawnpiakmi biaknak hna nih mi pawl kha Pathian he a hlatter hna. Thumkomh pathian, a thi kho lomi thlarau le zungzal hremnak ti bantuk cawnpiaknak hna cu Baibal ah hram aa bunhmi a si tiah mi tampi nih an ruah. Asinain mah cu a hmaan lomi biaknak in a rami an si. Cutin a cawnpiakmi biaknak nih Pathian halmi kha si loin biaknaklei phungphai tu kha biapi an chiah caah an cawnpiaknak cu “zeihmanh a ṭhahnem lo.”—Marka 7:7,8.Pathian nih biaknaklei chungthu lengnal sinak kha a huat. (Titas 1:16) Biaknak nih phunglam le phungphai hna kha si loin nifa nunnak ah ṭhathnemhnak a pek hna awk le Pathian he i naih awkah a bawmh hna awk a si. Tahchunhnak ah, Baibal nih hitin a ti: “Mi pakhatkhat nih kei cu biaknaklei ah aa zuammi ka si, tiah aa ruat ko lai, sihmanhsehlaw a lei kha a uk khawh lo ahcun a biaknak cu pakpalawng a si i amahle amah aa hlengmi a si. Sihmanhsehlaw nuhmei ngakṭah ṭha tein zohkhenh le vawleicung ah thurhnawm lo tein um tu hi Pathian kan Pa nih biaknak thiang le biaknak taktak i a ruahmi cu a si.” (Jeim 1:26, 27) Thurhnawmhnak a um lomi biaknak kha Hakha Baibal ah “biaknak thiang” tiah a leh. A ruang cu a thiang i, i titernak a um lomi biaknak a si ruangah a si.A hau. Pathian nih hmunkhat te ah rak ka bia hna seh ti a duh. Baibal nih hitin a ti: “Pakhat le pakhat kan i dawt khawh nakhnga le thilṭha kan i tuahpiak khawh nakhnga, i bawm tliahmah u sih. Pakhat le pakhat hmunkhat i, i pumh lengmang kha ngol hlah u sih.”—Hebru 10:24, 25.Jesuh nih a zultu pawl cu phu pakhat in ṭha tein dirh an si lai ti kha mah bia a chimmi nih a langhter: “Pakhat le pakhat nan zawn nan i ruah ahcun mi vialte nih, hi hna hi amah a zultu kha an si, tiah an in hngalh hna lai.” (Johan 13:35) Khrih zultu hna nih cu bantuk dawtnak a bik in an langhter khawhnak lam cu hmunkhat ah i pumhṭi kha a si. Cucaah biaknak caah hmunkhat ah hmaan tein i pumhṭi khawh awkah Khrihfabu kha an dirh. (1Korin16:19) Khrihfabu dihlak fonh tikah vawleicung pumpi unau rual an hung si.—1Peter 2:17.Biaknak bu pakhat chungah umnak men in a za loMi pawl cu Pathian biak khawh awkah hmunkhat ah an i pumh awk a si tiah Baibal nih a ti. Asinain mi pakhat cu biaknak bu pakhat chungah umnak men in Pathian lung a tong tiah Baibal nih a kan cawnpiak lo. Pathian cohlanmi a si nakhnga biaknak phunglam kha nifa a nunnak ah a langhter a hau. Tahchunhnak ah, Baibal nih hitin a ti: “Nuhmei, ngakṭah ṭha tein zohkhenh le vawleicung ah thurhnawm lo tein um tu hi Pathian kan Pa nih biaknak thiang le biaknak taktak i a ruahmi cu a si.”—Jeim 1:27.A si lo. Baibal nih Jesuh min in Pathian sin lawngah thla kan cam awk a si tiah a ti. Jesuh nih a zultu kha hitin a ti hna: “Hi bantuk hin thla cu nan cam awk a si: ‘Vancung khua i a um kan Pa, Na min thiang cu upat si ko seh.’” (Matthai 6:9) Mithiang mi, vancungmi asiloah a dang pakhatkhat sinah thlacam dingin Jesuh nih a zultu pawl kha a cawnpiak bal hna lo.Jesuh nih a zultu pawl kha hitin zongin a ti hna: “Lam le biatak le nunnak cu keimah hi ka si; keimah sinin ti dah lo cun ahohmanh Pa sin an phan kho lo.” (Johan 14:6) Jesuh lawnglawng hi kan caah Pathian sinah a kan nawlpiak khotu a si.—Hebru 7:25.Pathian sin thla kan cam buin mithiang mi hna sinah thla kan cam ah tah?Nawlbia Pahra lakin pakhat ah Pathian nih hitin a ti: “Keimah hi BAWIPA nan Pathian cu ka si i nahchuah a ngeimi Pathian ka si.” (Exodus 20:5) Zeiti lam in dah Pathian cu ‘nahchuahnak a ngeih’? New American Bible i a tanglei fianternak nih Pathian cu “zumhawktlak tein um awkah a halmi” a si tiah a ti. Pathian nih a sinah direct in thlacamnak i telin lungthin dihlak in amah biak awkah a kan hal.—Isaiah 48:11.Mithiang mi, vancungmi asiloah pakhatkhat sinah thla kan cam ahcun Pathian a thin a hung lai. Lamkaltu Johan nih vancungmi pakhat kha biak dingin aa timh tikah vancungmi nih hitin a thlauh: “Bawk hlah. Keimah zong nangmah bantukin Pathian sal ka si ve, Jesuh nih a phuanmi biatak aa tlaihmi nan unau hna lak i pakhat ka si ve. Pathian tu bia tuah.”—Biathlam 19:10.Jesuh nih a nunnak kha raithawinak caah a pek i zumhfekmi minung kha a khamh hna. (Matthai 20:28) Cucaah Baibal nih Jesuh kha “vawlei Khamhtu” tiah a auh. (1 Johan 4:14) Cun hiti zongin a ti: “Amah thawng lawnglawng in khamhnak hi hmuh khawh a si.  Zeicahtiah vawleicung dihlak ah hin a kan khamh khotu ding min dang zeihmanh a um lo.”—Lamkaltu 4:12.Jesuh nih amah a zummi vialte caah ‘thihnak a in.’ (Hebru 2:9; Johan 3:16) Mah hnuah “Pathian nih mithi hna sinin a thawhter” i van ah thlarau pum in a kir ṭhan. (Lamkaltu 3:15) Cucaah Jesuh nih “amah thawngin Pathian a fuhmi hna paoh cu a khamh khawh zungzal ko hna; zeicahtiah zungzal in a nun caah Pathian kha a nawlpiak khawh zungzal hna.”—Hebru 7:25.Kan caah Jesuh nih nawlpiak cu zeicah a herh?Kan dihlak in misual kan si. (Rom 3:23) Sualnak cu Pathian le kan karah dawnkhantu a si i mah nih thihnak a chuahter. (Rom 6:23) Asinain Jesuh cu tlanhnak man a zummi hna caah Pathian ‘sinah bia a chimpiak hna.’ (1Johan 2:1) An thlacamnak ngaihpiak awk, Jesuh raithawinak cungah i hngat in an sualnak ngaihthiam awkah Pathian sinah a nawlpiak hna. (Matthai 1:21; Rom 8:34) Mah cu amah a duhning a si caah Jesuh nawlnak kha a ngaihpiak. Pathian nih Jesuh kha “vawlei Khamhtu” si awkah a rung thlah.—Johan 3:17.Jesuh zumhnak men in khamhnak hmuh a si lai maw?A si lo. Khamhnak kan hmuh nakhnga Jesuh zumhnak lawng in a za lo. (Lamkaltu 16:30, 31) Baibal nih hitin a ti: “Pum cu thlarau loin a thih bantukin zumhnak zong cu tuahnak loin a thi ve.” (Jeim 2:26) Khamhnak hmuh awkah mah hi kan tuah a hau:  Jesuh le a Pa Jehovah kong kan cawn a hau.—Johan 17:3.  Anmah kan zumh hnanak fehter a hau.—Johan 12:44; 14:1.  An nawlbia zulhnak thawngin kan zumhnak langhter a hau. (Luka 6:46; 1Johan 2:17) Jesuh nih “Bawipa, Bawipa,” tiah a ka timi paohin khamh an si lai lo, sihmanhsehlaw “vancung i a ummi ka Pa nih tuah hna seh ti a duhmi a tuahmi lawnglawng” khamh an si lai tiah a ti.—Matthai 7:21.  Harnak caan hmanhah kan zumhnak langhter peng a hau. Jesuh nih fiang tein hitin a ti: “A dongh tiangin a fekmi cu khamh an si lai.”—Matthai 24:13.Jesuh tlanhnak man cu minung kha sualnak le thihnak in Pathian khamhnak lam a si. Baibal nih Jesuh thletmi thisen kha tlanhnak man in a langhter. (Efesa 1:7; 1Peter 1:18, 19) Cucaah Jesuh nih ‘mi tampi tlanhnak ca ka nunnak pek awkah’ ka ra tiah a ti.—Matthai 20:28.Zeicah ‘mi tampi tlanhnak’ cu a herh?Hmasa bik mipa Adam cu mitling in ser a si i sualnak a ngei lo. Zungzal nun ding ruahchannak a ngei nain Pathian nawl a ngaih lo caah mah kha a rak sung. (Genesis 3:17-19) Fa a ngeih tikah sualnak ro a pek hna. (Rom 5:12) Cucaah Adam nih amah le a fale kha sualnak le thihnak sal ah a ‘zuar’ hna tiah Baibal nih a ti. (Rom 7:14) A tefa hna cu a tlingmi an si ti lo, cucaah Adam sunghmi thil kha ahohmanh nih an caw ṭhan kho ti lo.—Salm 49:7,8.Ruahchannak a ngei lomi Adam tefa hna kha Pathian nih a zaangfah hna. (Johan 3:16) Asinain a dingmi Pathian phunglam nih a fekmi a hrampi kong um loin an sualnak kha a ngaithiam hna lo. (Salm 89:14; Rom 3:23-26) Pathian nih minung kha a kan dawt tuk caah kan sualnak ngaihthiam lawng si loin hlohpiak awkah phung ningin a kan timhpiak. (Rom 5:6-8) Mah phung ningin sermi cu tlanhnak man kha a si.Tlanhnak man timi cu zeidah a si?Baibal ningin “tlanhnak man” timi biafang ah a kong pathum aa tel:               Pekmi a man kha a si.—Nambar 3:46, 47. Luatnak asiloah tlanhnak kha a si.—Exodus 21:30. A man aa khatmi asiloah a khuhmi kha a si.*Mah a kong pathum cu Jesuh tlanhnak man he zeitindah aa pehtlaih ti kha zohhmanh u sih. A man. Baibal nih Khrihfa hna cu “a man in cawkmi” an si tiah a ti. (1Korin 6:20; 7:23) Mah man cu Jesuh thi kha a si. Jesuh nih ‘hrin kip le chung kip le holh kip le phun kip chungin, minung cu Pathian [caah a thi in a cawk hna, NW] sinah a phakpi hna.’—Biathlam 5:8,9. Luatnak. Jesuh tlanhnak man thawngin sualnak in ‘luatnak’ kan hmu.—1Korin 1:30; Kolose 1:14; Hebru 9:15. A man aa khatmi. Jesuh tlanhnak man cu Adam nih a sunghmi, a tlingmi miung nunnak he aa khat. (1Korin 15:21, 22, 45, 46) Baibal nih hitin a ti: “Mipa [Adam] pakhat nawlngaih lo ruangah mi tampi kha misual i ser an si bantukin mipa [Jesuh] pakhat nawlngaih ruangah mi tampi cu miding ah ser an si lai.” (Rom 5:19) Mah nih mi pakhat thihnak nih mi tampi caah tlanhnak man zeitindah a pek khawh ti kha a kan hngalhter. A tak ti ahcun, Jesuh tlanhnak cu mah in ṭhatnak hmuh a duhmi “mi vialte caah aa khatmi tlanhnak” a si.—1Timote 2:5,6.Tipil in timi cu mi pakhat ti chungah hnim dih in rak chuah ṭhan kha a chim duhmi a si.* Mah nih a ngan pahmi tiva ah Jesuh tipil a innak a ruang kha a kan hngalhter. (Matthai 3:13, 16) Cu bantukin Ethiopia mi pa pakhat zong nih “ti tlawmpal” a umnak kha an phanh tikah tipil pek dingin a rak hal.—Lamkaltu 8:36-40.Tipil innak timi a sullamBaibal nih tipil innak kha vuinak he a tahchunh. (Rom 6:4; Kolose 2:12) Ti chungah tipil innak nih mi pakhat i hlanlio a nunning cu a thi i Pathian sinah aa pumpemi Khrihfa pakhat in a hun nunmi kha a chim duhmi a si. Tipil innak le tipil in hlanah tuahmi kehlan hna cu Pathian timhtuahnak an si i mah nih Jesuh Khrih raithawinak zumhnak cungah hram aa bunhmi, a thiangmi chiaṭha thleidannak lungthin a ngeihter. (1Peter 3:21) Cucaah Jesuh nih a zultu hna kha tipil in a hau tiah a cawnpiak hna.—Matthai 28:19, 20.Ti chungah tipil innak nih sualnak kha a thianh maw?A thianh lo. Baibal nih Jesuh thisen thawng lawngin sualnak in kan thiang kho tiah a kan cawnpiak. (Rom 5:8,9; 1Johan 1:7) Asinain Jesuh raithawinak in ṭhatnak hmuh awkah Jesuh kha zumh in a cawnpiaknak ningin nun a hau i tipil in a hau.—Lamkaltu 2:38; 3:19.Bawhte kha tipil pek awkah Baibal nih a kan cawnpiak maw?A kan cawnpiak lo, Baibal ah bawhte tipil peknak kong a langhtermi a um lo. Church cheukhat nih bawhte kha an lu ah ti thehnak in siseh, ti toihnak in siseh “tipil an pek” hna i min an pekmi hna kan hmuh. A tak ti ahcun tipil a ingmi hna cu “thawngṭha, Pathian Pennak kong” hngalhthiam awk le zumh awkah a cuzami an si a hau. (Lamkaltu 8:12) Mah cu Pathian bia ngaih, cohlan le thlennak tuah he aa pehtlai. Bawhte nih cun cutin an tuah kho lai lo.—Lamkaltu 2:22, 38, 41.Mah lengah Pathian nih Khrihfa nulepa hna i an zumhfehnak ruangah an fale kha a thiangmi in a hmuh hna tiah Baibal nih a langhter. (1Korin 7:14) Bawhte tipil peknak cu Baibal he aa tlakmi a si ahcun nulepa hna i an zumhfehnak ruangah an fale nih ṭhatnak an hmu tiah Baibal nih a langhter lai lo.*Khrihfa tipil innak he aa tlaimi, a hmaan lomi ruahnakA hmaan lomi ruahnak: Ti chungah hnim dih a hau lo, ti thehnak asiloah toihnak men in a za ko.A hmaanmi: Baibal ah a langhtermi tipil innak kong hna ah ti chung i hnim dihnak aa tel. Tahchunhnak ah, zultu Filip nih Ethiopia mi pa tipil a pek tikah an pahnih in ‘ti chungah khan an kal’ i tipil kha a rak pek.—Lamkaltu 8:36-39.*A hmaan lomi ruahnak: Chungkhar ningin tipil an in tikah bawhte zong an i telmi bantukin Baibal nih a langhter. Tahchunhnak ah, Filipi khua i thonginn bawi pakhat cu “amah le a innchungkhar dihlak in tipilnak an ing colh.”—Lamkaltu 16:31-34.A hmaanmi: Khrihfa a hung simi mah thonginn bawi kong nih tipil a ingmi hna cu “Bawipa bia” kha an hngalhthiam i “lunglawmhnak in an khat” tiah a langhter. (Lamkaltu 16:32, 34) Bawhte nih Jehovah Pathian bia kha an hngalthiam kho lo. Cucaah tipil a ingmi mah thonginn bawi chungkhar ah bawhte pakhat hmanh an i tel lo tiah kan ti khawh.A hmaan lomi ruahnak: Jesuh nih Vancung Pennak cu ngakchia ta a si tiah a ti tikah bawhte tipil peknak kong a kan cawnpiakmi a si.—Matthai 19:13-15; Marka 10:13-16.A hmaanmi: Jesuh nih mah bia a chim tikah tipil innak kong kha a langhter duhmi a si lo. Mah canah Pathian Pennak a co dingmi hna cu ngakchia bantukin aa toidormi le cawnpiak a fawimi an si a hau ti kha a langhtermi a si.—Matthai 18:4; Luka 18:16, 17.Adam le Evi cu hmasa bik sualnak a tuahmi minung an si. “A ṭha le a ṭhalo hngalhnak pe khotu thingkung a tlai” an einak thawngin Pathian nawl an rak buar. Mah tikah mi tampi nih sualnak hrampi* tiah auhmi sualnak kha an rak tuah. (Genesis 2:16, 17; 3:6; Rom 5:19) Mah thingkung i a tlai kha Adam le Evi nih einak nawl an ngei lo, zeicatiah minung caah a ṭha le ṭhalo he aa tlaiin Pathian nih biakhiahnak nawl a ngeihmi kha mah nih a aiawh caah a si. Adam le Evi nih mah thingkung a tlai an einak thawngin a ṭha le ṭhalo kong ah anmah tein biakhiahnak tuah dingin an i thim. Cutin an tuahmi cu Pathian nih a ṭha le ṭhalo kong i biakhiahnak nawl a ngeihmi kha an hlawt a si.“Sualnak hrampi” nih Adam le Evi kha zeitindah a hnorsuan hna?“Sualnak hrampi” nih zeitindah a kan hnorsuan?“Sualnak hrampi” ruangah a chuakmi thil in kan luat kho maw?“Sualnak hrampi” he aa tlaimi a hmaan lomi ruahnakAdam le Evi nih sualnak an tuah caah an hung tar i a donghnak ah an thi. Pathian he an i pehtlaihnak kha an hrawh i a tlingmi ngandamnak he zungzal nunnak kha an sung.—Genesis 3:19.Adam le Evi nih sualnak a ngeimi an sinak kha an tefa vialte sinah an roh hna. Mah cu nulepa nih cikor chambaunak an rohmi hna bantuk a si. (Rom 5:12) Cucaah mi vialte cu kan chuahka in “misual”* kan si, chim duhmi cu mitlinglo in hrin kan si caah thil ṭhalo tuah kha kan i fawih tinak a si.—Salm 51:5; Efesa 2:3.Ro kan comi sualnak le tlinlonak ruangah kan zaw, kan hung tar i kan thi. (Rom 6:23) Cun kanmah le midang tuahmi sualnak ruangah a chuakmi harnak zong kan tong.—Phungchimtu 8:9; Jeim 3:2.Kan luat kho. Jesuh nih “kan sualnak ngaihthiamnak ding caah” raithawinak in a nunnak a pek tiah Baibal nih a ti. (1 Johan 4:10) Jesuh raithawinak nih kan comi sualnak ruangah a chuakmi thilṭhalo in a kan luatter khawh i Adam le Evi nih an sunghmi, a tlingmi ngandamnak he zungzal nunnak kha a kan ngeihter ṭhan khawh.—Johan 3:16.*A hmaan lomi ruahnak: Sualnak hrampi ruangah Pathian he pehtlaihnak ṭha zeitikhmanh ah kan ngei kho lo.A hmaanmi: Adam le Evi nih an tuahmi thil ruangah Pathian nih a kan mawhchiat lo. Mitlinglo kan si kha a hngalhthiam i kan tuah khawhmi lengin kan sinin aa ruahchan lo. (Salm 103:14) Kan comi sualnak ruangah harnak kan ton hmanhah Pathian he pehtlaihnak ṭha ngeih dingin caanṭha le tinvo sung kan ngei.—Phungthlukbia 3:32.A hmaan lomi ruahnak: Tipil innak nih mi pakhat kha sualnak hrampi in a luatter caah bawhte zong tipil an in awk a si.A hmaanmi: Tipil innak cu khamhnak hmuhnak caah a biapi tukmi kehlan a si ko nain Jesuh raithawinak zumhnak lawng nih mi pakhat kha sualnak in a thianh khawh. (1 Peter 3:21; 1 Johan 1:7) A hmaanmi zumhnak cu hngalhnak cungah aa hngatmi a si caah bawhte nih cu bantuk zumhnak cu an ngei kho rih lo. Cucaah Baibal nih bawhte tipil innak kha a cohlang lo. Mah kha a hmasa Khrihfa hna kong in hngalh khawh a si. Bawhte pawl si loin Pathian Bia a zummi “nu he, pa he” tipil an ing.—Lamkaltu 2:41; 8:12.A hmaan lomi ruahnak: Evi nih thlauhmi thingthei kha a ei hmasa ruangah Pathian nih nu pawl kha chiat a serh hna.A hmaanmi: Nu pawl chiatserh canah Pathian nih Evi kha sualnak tuah dingin a hlengtu “rulpi tar, Khuachia, asiloah, Satan” kha chiat a serh. (Biathlam 12:9; Genesis 3:14) Mah lengah sualnak hrampi caah rian a ngeimi cu a nupi kha si loin Adam a si tiah Pathian nih a hmuh.—Rom 5:12.Adam nih a nupi kha a uk lai tiah Pathian nih zeicah a ti? (Genesis 3:16) Cutin a ti ruangah Pathian nih mah tuahsernak kha a ngaihthiam tinak a si lo. Sualnak ruangah a chuakmi thil ṭhalo kha a chimchungmi a si. Pa nih an nupile kha daw hna sehlaw hmaizah hna seh, cun nu pawl kha upatnak in pehtlaih hna seh tiah Pathian nih aa ruahchan.—Efesa 5:25; 1Peter 3:7.A hmaan lomi ruahnak: Nupa umṭinak cu sualnak hrampi a si.A hmaanmi: Nupa umṭinak cu sualnak hrampi a si lo ti kha mah a ruang hna nih an langhter:  Pathian nih Adam kha a ṭha le a ṭhalo hngalhnak pe khotu thingkung a tlai ei lo dingin nawl a pek lioah Adam cu amah lawng a rak si, a nupi a um rih lo.—Genesis 2:17, 18.  Pathian nih Adam le Evi kha “tefa tampi in ngei u,” tiah nawl a pek hna. (Genesis 1:28) Pathian nih a fialmi hna an tuah ruangah dantat an si ahcun Pathian cu a puarhrang tukmi a si lai.  Adam le Evi nih sualnak kha hmunkhat ah an tuahṭi lo—Evi nih sualnak a tuah hnuah a vapa nih a tuah ve.—Genesis 3:6.  Nuva nih nupa sinak an hmanmi kha Baibal nih a cohlan.—Phungthlukbia 5:18, 19; 1Korin 7:3.Sualnak timi cu Pathian phunglam he aa ralkahmi tuahsernak, intuarnak le ruahnak hna kha an si. Pathian mithmuh ah a hmaan lomi le a ding lomi thil tuahnak thawngin Pathian nawlbia buar zong aa tel. (1Johan 3:4; 5:17) A hmaanmi thil kha hngalh ko nain hramhram in buarmi sualnak kong zong Baibal nih a chim.—Jeim 4:17.A hrampi Baibal ah sualnak tiah lehmi biafang cu “hmuichon khen lo” timi sullam a ngei. Tahchunhnak ah, hlanlio Israel ralkap phukhat cu lungherh cheh a thiam tukmi an si caah an hmuichon kha ‘nganh loin’ an khen khawh. Mah kha a biafang ningin kan leh ahcun “sualnak tuah lo” timi sullam a ngei. (Biaceihtu 20:16) Cucaah sualnak timi cu a tlingmi Pathian phunglam in pial kha a si.Pathian cu Sertu a si caah minung caah phunglam sernak nawl a ngei. (Biathlam 4:11) Kan tuahsernak he aa tlaiin Pathian hmaiah biaceih kan si lai.—Rom 14:12.Sualnak pakhat hmanh tuah lo timi cu a si kho maw?A si kho lo. Baibal nih “mi vialte cu kan sual dih cio ko i Pathian sunparnak kha kan bau dih cio ko” tiah a ti. (Rom 3:23; 1Siangpahrang 8:46; Phungchimtu 7:20; 1Johan 1:8) Zeicah cutin a si?Hmasa bik minung, Adam le  Evi cu a hramthawk ah sualnak a ngei lomi an si. Mah cu Pathian muikeng in, mitling in ser an si caah a si. (Genesis 1:27) Asinain Pathian nawl an ngaih lo caah a tlingmi sinak kha an rak sung. (Genesis 3:5, 6, 17-19) Fa an hun ngeih tikah an fale kha sualnak le tlinlonak ro an vuih hna. (Rom 5:12) Israel Siangpahrang David nih “Ka chuahka in miṭhalo ka si” tiah a ti.—Salm 51:5.Sualnak cheukhat cu a dang nakin a ngan deuh maw?A ngan deuh. Tahchunhnak ah, hlanlio Sodom khua mi hna cu “miṭhalo,” “ṭhatlonak a tuahmi misual” an si caah “an sualnak cu a ngan ngaingai.” (Genesis 13:13; 18:20) Sualnak ngan tiah ti khawhmi a kong pathum kha zohhmanh u sih. A fakmi. Nupa sualnak, siasal biaknak, firnak, zuritnak, mi thil chuhnak, lainawnnak le khuachia thiamnak ti bantuk sualnak ngan kha hrial awkah Baibal nih ralrin a kan pek. (1Korin 6:9-11; Biathlam 21:8) Baibal nih mah sualnak hna kha ruatset loin le tinhnak ngei loin chimmi, tuahmi ruangah midang fahnak a pemi sualnak he aa dang in a langhter. (Phungthlukbia 12:18; Efesa 4:31, 32) Asinain zei bantuk sualnak hmanh kha zei rel loin um lo awkah Baibal nih a kan forh, zeicatiah mah nih Pathian nawlbia a kan buarter khawh caah a si.—Matthai 5:27, 28. Lungput. Sualnak cheukhat cu Pathian duhnak hngalh lo ruangah tuahmi a si. (Lamkaltu 17:30; 1Timote 1:13) Cu bantuk sualnak le Pathian nawlbia hngalh ko buin hramhram in buarmi sualnak kha Baibal nih aa dang in a langhter. (Nambar 15:30, 31) Hramhram in buarmi sualnak cu a ‘ṭhalomi’ lungput in a rami a si.—Jeremiah 16:12. A voi. Baibal nih voikhat lawng tuahmi sualnak le atu le atu tuahmi sualnak aa dannak zong kha a langhter. (1Johan 3:4-8) A hmaanmi thil tuah ding ti hngalh hnu hmanhah ‘sualnak a tuah pengmi’ cu Pathian nih bia a ceih hna lai.—Hebru 10:26, 27.Sualnak ngan a tuahmi cu a sualnak ruangah lung sivang in a um men lai. Tahchunhnak ah, Siangpahrang David nih hitin a ṭial: “Ka sualnak tilet chungah ka pil i ka sualnak cu an rih caah tang ah an ka hnuh.” (Salm 38:4) Asinain Baibal nih mah ruahchannak hi a kan pek: “Miṭhalo nih an zulhmi an lam kha hlaw hna seh law an ruahning kha thleng hna seh. BAWIPA kan Pathian leiah cun i mer hna seh, amah cu mi zaangfah a thiam i khulrang in mi a ngaithiam khotu a si.”—Isaiah 55:7.A kan bawmh khawh. Ka sual timi ruahnak tei awkah Baibal nih a kan bawmh khawh. (Salm 32:1-5) Palhnak kan tuah tikah lungtak tein kan i ngaihchih ahcun Pathian nih a kan ngaihthiam lai i a hmaanmi thil tuah awkah a kan bawmh lai. (Salm 86:5) A caan ah sualnak ka ngei timi ruahnak nih ṭhatnak a chuahter ti kha Baibal nih a langhter—zeicahtiah mah nih palhnak kha i remh awk le hmailei ah tuah ti lo awkah a kan forh khawh caah a si. (Salm 51:17; Phungthlukbia 14:9) A hleihluat tuk in sualnak ka ngei timi ruahnak ngeih lo awkah Baibal nih ruahnak a kan cheuh, zeicahtiah mah nih ruahchannak a ngei lomi asiloah Pathian hmaiah aa tlak lomi in a kan ruahter khawh caah a si. Cu bantuk ruahnak kan ngeih ahcun ‘kan lung a dong’ kho.—2Korin 2:7.Zeinihdah ka sual timi ruahnak a kan ngeihter khawh?Ka sual timi ruahnak kha zeitindah kan tawnghtham khawh?Sualnak le ngaihthiamnak he aa tlaimi Baibal caangKa sual timi ruahnak a kan ngeihter khomi a ruang tampi a um. Kan dawtmi hna an lung kan fahter hna tik asiloah kan tuah awk a simi thil kan tuah lo tikah cu bantuk ruahnak kan ngei kho. A caan ah sualnak kan tuah taktak lo nain ka sual timi ruahnak kan ngei kho. Tahchunhnak ah, aa tlak lomi, a sang tukmi phunglam kan i chiah i mah phunglam kha kan zulh khawh lo tikah ka sual timi ruahnak kan ngei kho. Mah ruangah Baibal nih kanmah le kanmah kha a tlari tein i hmuh awkah tha a kan pek.—Phungchimtu 7:16.Ka sual timi ruahnak ruangah lungdongh in um canah na tuah khawhmi thil kha tuah. Zeitin in dah? Na palhnak kha phuang. Jehovah* Pathian sin ah thlacamnak in ngaihthiam hal. (Salm 38:18; Luka 11:4) Lungtak tein naa ngaihchih i palhnak na tuah ti lo ahcun Pathian nih ka thlacamnak a ngaih lai ti kha na zumh khawh. (2Chanrelnak 33:13; Salm 34:18) Minung nih an hmuh khawh lomi kan chunglei minung kha Pathian nih a hmuh khawh. Pathian nih palhnak tuah ti lo awkah kan i zuammi kha a hmuh tikah anih cu “a dingmi le zumhawk tlakmi a si caah ... kan sualnak kha a kan ngaihthiam lai.”—1Johan 1:9; Phungthlukbia 28:13.Mi pakhat cungah palhnak na tuah ahcun na palhnak kha cohlang in ngaihthiamnak na hal a hau. Mah cu a fawi lai lo! Cutin tuah awkah ralṭhatnak le toidornak ngeih a hau. Lungtak tein ngaihthiam halnak nih ṭhatnak pahnih a chuahter: Na thilrit kha a zanter lai i daihnak a chuahter lai.—Matthai 3:8; 5:23, 24. Pathian zaangfahnak a langhtermi Baibal caang hna kha ruat. Tahchunhnak ah, 1Johan 3:19, 20 hi ruathmanh. ‘Kan lung nih sual a kan phawt’ khawh tiah Baibal nih a ti. Mah cu mahle mah a hleihluat tuk in sual i phawtnak nih Pathian dawtnak hmuh awkah kaa tlak lo timi ruahnak a kan ngeihter khawh tinak a si. Asinain mah cacaang nih “Pathian cu kan lung nakin a ngan deuh” ti zongin a ti. Zeitin in dah? Kan kong dihlak kha a hngalh i kan intuarnak le kan derthawmnak kha a hngalhthiam. Kan chuahka in mitlinglo kan si caah palhnak kan tuah kho ti zong a hngalh.* (Salm 51:5) Cucaah palhnak a tuah ko nain lungtak tein aa ngaichihmi kha a hlaw hna lo.—Salm 32:5. Hlanlio na palhnak kha ruat peng hlah. A hmasa ah palhnak a tuah ko nain a hnuah a nunning aa thlengmi nu le pa kong tampi Baibal ah a um. Tahchunhnak ah, lamkaltu Paul tiah hngalhmi, Tarsas khuami Saul kong hi ruathmanh. Farasi mi pakhat in Jesuh zultu hna kha fakpi in a rak hrem hna. (Lamkaltu 8:3; 9:1,2, 11) Asinain Pathian le Messiah asiloah Khrih ka ralchanhmi hna a si ti kha a hun hngalh tikah aa ngaichih i a nunning aa thleng, cun Khrihfa hna caah zohchunh awk ṭha pakhat a hung si. Paul cu a luanciami caan i a tuahsernak cungah lungtak tein aa ngaichih, asinain mah kong kha a ruat peng lo. Pathian zaangfahnak ka hmu ti kha a hngalh caah Paul cu lungthawhnak a ngeimi cawnpiaktu a hung si i zungzal nunnak ruahchannak a ngeihmi kha a thlau ti lo.—Filipi 3:13, 14.Salm 51:17: “Maw Pathian, toidornak lungthin le nawl ngaimi lungthin hi na hlaw lai lo.”A sullam: Palhnak na tuahmi cungah lungtak tein naa ngaihchih ahcun Pathian nih aan hlaw lai lo. Na cungah zaangfahnak a langhter lai.Phungthlukbia 28:13: “A palhnak kha a thupmi cu khua-awng a tong lai lo, sihmanhsehlaw a phuang i a hlawmi nih cun zaangfahnak a hmuh lai.”A sullam: Pathian cungah kan sualnak kha kan hngalh i kan i thlen ahcun a kan ngaihthiam lai.Jeremiah 31:34: “An ṭhatlonak kha ka ngaihthiam hna lai i an sualnak kha ka hngal camcin ti lai lo.”A sullam: Pathian nih kan sualnak a kan ngaihthiam hnu cun aa cinken ti lo. Zaangfahnak taktak a langhter.Baibal ah kuak zuk* le khuhsii hmannak kong he aa tlaiin a chimmi a um lo. Asinain kan ngandamnak a hnorsuangmi le Pathian nih a duh lomi a thiang lomi ziaza pawl a langhtermi phunglam hna cu a um. Cucaah kuak zuk cu sual a si ti kha kan hngalh khawh. Nunnak kha upat. ‘Pathian cu minung kha nunnak le thaw a petu a si.’ (Lamkaltu 17:24, 25) Nunnak cu Pathian nih a kan pekmi laksawng a si caah kuak zuk ti bantuk chan a tawiter khomi zeibantuk thil hmanh kha kan tuah awk a si lo. Kuak zuk cu vawleicung pumpi ah thihnak a chuahter khomi thil lakah pakhat a si ve, asinain mah cu kham khawh a si ko. Innpa kha daw hna. “Na innpa cu nangmah naa dawt bantukin na dawt lai.” (Matthai 22:39) Mi lakah kuak zuk cu dawtnak ngeih lo a si. Kuak a zumi pawngah a ummi hna nih kuak khu kha an dawp ve caah kuak a zumi hna nih an ngeihmi zawtnak bantuk kha an ngei ve. Thiang tein um. “Pathian sinah a nungin pekchanhmi raithawinak bantukin i pe tuah u ... cohlan awk tlakmi si tuah u.” (Rom 12:1) “Pum siseh, thlarau siseh, a thurhnomhtertu paohpaoh kha i thenh u sihlaw Pathian ṭih bu tein um u sih.” (2Korin 7:1) Kuak zuk cu thiannak he aa ralchanhmi a si. Khuhsii a hmangmi hna cu an pum fakpi in a hnorsuang khomi ṭih a nungmi siivai hramhram in a hmangmi an si.Weed asiloah pot tiah auhmi sahdah kong le a dang ritnak siivai kong kha Baibal ah an min in a chimmi a um lo. Asinain mi a leem khomi mah bantuk thil hna kha nuamhnak sawhsawh in hman awk a si lonak kong a langhtermi phunglam tu cu a um. A cunglei i phunglam hna lengah mah lamhruainak hna zong hi hman khawh an si: Lungthinlei thil ti khawhnak kha uk khawh a hau. “Bawipa na Pathian cu na lungthin dihlak ... in na dawt lai.” (Matthai 22:37, 38) “Ralring tein um u.” (1Peter 1:13) Ritnak siivai a hmangmi pakhat nih cun a lungthin kha ṭha tein aa uk kho lo. Ritnak siivai nih a leemmi mi tampi an um. A ṭhami thil kha an ruat kho ti lo i ritnak siivai hmuh khawhnak lam lawng kha an kawl.—Filipi 4:8. Upadi zul. “Bawi le nawlngeitu pawl kha an nawl nan ngaih hna lai.” (Titus 3:1) Ram tampi ah ritnak siivai cheukhat kha fakpi in an khenkham. Pathian mithmai ṭha hmuh kan duh ahcun cozah pawl nawl kha kan ngaih a hau.—Rom 13:1.‘Holh theih loin holh’ timi cu a hmasa Khrihfa cheukhat nih an hmuhmi khuaruahhar thil ti khawhnak a si i voikhat hmanh cawn bal loin holh pakhat chim khawhnak kha a si. (Lamkaltu 10:46) Phungchimtu nih a chimmi bia kha mah holh a theimi paoh nih an hngalhthiam. (Lamkaltu 2:4-8) Holh theih loin holhnak cu Pathian nih kumzabu pakhatnak i Khrihfa cheukhat a pekmi hna thiang thlarau laksawng a si.—Hebru 2:4; 1Korin 12:4, 30.Holh theih loin holhnak cu khoika ah le zeitik in dah aa thawk?Holh theih loin holhnak i aa tinhnak cu zeidah a si?Holh theih loin holhnak cu a um zungzal maw?Holh theih loin holhnak cu zeitik ah dah a dongh lai?Tuchan i holh theih loin holhnak he aa tlaiin tah zeitin?A hmaanmi Khrihfa hna cu zeitindah thleidan khawh an si?Mah khuaruahhar thil cu AD 33, Judah mi hna tuahmi Pentekos Puai ni i zinglei, Jerusalem khua ah aa thawkmi a si. Jesuh zultu 120 hrawng cu hmunkhat i an i pumh lioah “Thiang Thlarau in an khat i Thlarau nih chim khawhnak a pek hna caah khan holh dang in an holh.” (Lamkaltu 1:15; 2:1-4) “Vawleicung khuazakip in a rami” mibu nganpi cu an i pum i “kanmah holh in an holh tiin an rak theih cio.”—Lamkaltu 2:5,6.Khrihfa pawl cu Pathian nih a umpi hna ti langhternak caah a si. Hlan ah Moses ti bantuk zumhfekmi hna kha Pathian nih a umpi hna ti langhternak caah khuaruahhar thil tuah khawhnak a pek hna. (Exodus 4:1-9, 29-31; Nambar 17:10) Holh theih loin holhnak i aa tinhnak zong cutin a si ve. Dirhkami Khrihfabu cu Pathian nih a umpi ti langhternak caah a si. Lamkaltu Paul nih hitin a ṭial: “Holh theih loin holh cu Pathian a zummi hna caah si loin a zum lomi hna ca i hmelchunhnak a si.”—1Korin 14:22. Khrihfa hna nih felfai tein thawngṭha an chim khawh nakhnga caah a si. Pentekos ni i Jesuh zultu pawl bia a theimi hna nih hitin an ti: “Pathian nih thil lianngan a tuahmi hna kha an chim tikah an chimmi cu kan holh in an chim tiin kan theih cio hna.” (Lamkaltu 2:11) Cucaah mah khuaruahhar thil i aa tinhnak a dang pakhat cu Khrihfa pawl nih felfai tein “thawngṭha chim awk” le Jesuh nawlpeknak ningin ‘miphun vialte zultu ser’ awkah a si. (Lamkaltu 10:42; Matthai 28:19) Mah ni ah khuaruahhar thil a hmu i thawngṭha a ngaimi 3,000 hrawng cu zultu an hung si.—Lamkaltu 2:41.A um zungzal lo. Holh theih loin holhnak i telin thiang thlarau laksawng hna cu chikkhat ca lawng an si. Baibal nih hitin a chimchung: “Profet an um maw? An rian cu a dih ko lai. Holh theih loin a holhmi an um maw? Cu hna cu an dong lai.”—1Korin 13:8.Lamkaltu hna chan ah thiang thlarau laksawng kha a dang Khrihfa hna zong pek an si ve. Thil sining tam deuh ah lamkaltu hna nih zumtu hna cungah an kut an chuannak thawngin pek an si. (Lamkaltu 8:18; 10:44-46) Lamkaltu hna sinin thiang thlarau laksawng a hmumi hna nih midang kha an pe chin kho hna lo. (Lamkaltu 8:5-7, 14-17) Tahchunhnak ah, cozah bawi nih mi pakhat kha mawṭaw mawnghnak license a pek khawh nain mah license a ngeimi nih midang kha license peknak nawl a ngei lo. Lamkaltu hna le lamkaltu hna sinin mah laksawng a hmumi hna an thih hnuah holh theih loin holhnak cu rak dongh dawh a si.Kumzabu pakhatnak a donghnaklei hrawngah khuaruahhar laksawng a simi holh theih loin holhnak cu a rak dong. Tuchan ah ahohmanh nih Pathian ṭhawnnak thawngin holh theih loin kan holh tiah fiang tein an chim kho lo.*Jesuh nih mah zawn ruat lo dawtnak cu a zultu pawl i hmelchunhnak a si tiah a ti. (Johan 13:34, 35) Lamkaltu Paul zong nih dawtnak cu a hmaanmi Khrihfa hna i zungzal hmelchunhnak a si tiah a kan cawnpiak. (1Korin 13:1,8) Pathian thiang thlarau nih “a chuahtermi” Khrihfa ziaza hna a langhter tikah dawtnak kha hmasa bik ah a langhter.—Galati 5:22, 23.Baibal nih midang thil ṭhenh awk le a ruang ṭha a um caah cutin tuah awkah timhcia tein um u tiah a kan forh. Mah nih a hmutu lawng si loin a petu zong peknak in ṭhatnak hmuh khawh a si ti kha a langhter. (Phungthlukbia 11:25; Luka 6:38) Jesuh nih “pek leiah hin hmuh lei nakin lunglawmhnak a um deuh” tiah a ti.”—Lamkaltu 20:35.Peknak nih zeitik ah dah Pathian lung a lawmhter?Peknak nih zeitik ah dah Pathian lung a lawmhter lo?Peknak he aa tlaimi Baibal caang hnaLungtho tein peknak nih ṭhatnak a chuahter. Baibal nih hitin a ti: “Cucaah nanmah le nan lungthin nan i thleh ning cio in rak tho u, nan thawh tikah i ngaihchih bu le hnekchom in si hlah seh, lunglawm tein a thomi kha Pathian nih a dawt hna.”—2Korin 9:7.Lungtho tein peknak cu Pathian cohlanmi “biaknak” phunkhat a si. (Jeim 1:27) A chambaumi hna siang ngaiin a bawmmi cu Pathian nih an cungah leiba a ngeimi bantukin aa ruah. (Phungthlukbia 19:17) Cucaah Pathian nih a cham ṭhan lai tiah Baibal nih a kan cawnpiak.—Luka 14:12-14.Mah ca ṭhatnak in siannak langhter tikah. Tahchunhnak ah:  Midang lungthin lak awkah.—Matthai 6:2.  Pakhatkhat hmuh ṭhan awkah.—Luka 14:12-14.  Khamhnak cawk awkah.—Salm 49:6, 7.Mah nih Pathian duh lomi tuahsernak asiloah lungput hna a hlorh tikah. Tahchunhnak ah, mi pakhat kha phe kahnak caah, ritnak sii asiloah zu ningcang loin hmannak caah tangka pek cu a palh lai. (1Korin 6:9, 10; 2Korin 7:1) Cun rian ṭuan a huam lo caah amah tein aa cawm kho lomi bawmh zong aa tlak lomi a si.—2Thesalon 3:10.Mah innchungkhar kha zei rel loin midang tu tampi pek tikah. Chungkharlu nih a innchungkhar herhbaumi kha a zohkhenh awk a si tiah Baibal nih a kan cawnpiak. (1Timote 5:8) Chungkharlu nih a innchungkhar hnorsuang tiangin midang kha tam tuk a pek hna ahcun a palh lai. Cu bantukin an ngeihmi thilri kha “Pathian ta a si” tiin kum upa a simi an nu le an pa zohkhenh a duh lomi hna kha Jesuh nih a mawtchiat hna.—Marka 7:9-13.Baibal ah Jesuh chuah nithla a langhtermi a um lo i a chuah ni puai tuah ding a si ti zongin a chim lo. McClintock le Strong i Cyclopedia timi cauk nih hitin a ti: “Christmas puai tuah dingin Pathian nih a kan fial lo i Biakam Thar zongah a um lo.”Christmas puai kong hlathlai tikah a hmaan lomi biaknak phungphai hna in a rami a si ti kha kan hngalh khawh. Pathian nih a duh lomi lam in amah biak awkah kan i zuam ahcun Pathian kan serhsatmi bantuk a si tiah Baibal nih a langhter.—Exodus 32:5-7.Jesuh chuah ni puai tuahnak: “A hmasa Khrihfa hna nih [Jesuh] chuah ni puai an tuah lo. Zeicatiah mi pakhatkhat i a chuah ni puai tuah cu a hmaan lomi biaknak phunglam a si tiah an ruah caah a si.”—The World Book Encyclopedia. December 25: Mah ni ah Jesuh a chuak timi langhtertu zeihmanh a um lo. Church hruaitu hna nih khuasik thla i ni a tawi bik caan ah tuahmi a hmaan lomi biaknak puai hna he aa khah nakhnga mah ni kha an thimmi a si kho men. Laksawng peknak, rawldanghnak le party puai: The Encyclopedia Americana nih hitin a ti: “Christmas puai phungphai tam deuh cu December thla lai ah tuahmi, Saturnalia tiah auhmi Rom mi hna puai in a rami a si. Tahchunhnak ah, rawldanghnak puai sunglawi taktak in tuahnak, laksawng i peknak le phazawngdaing vannak hna cu mah puai in a rami a si.” Saturnalia puai an tuah lioah “rian le chawlehnak vialte kha an ngol chung” tiah Encyclopædia Britannica nih a langhter. Christmas mei vannak: The Encyclopedia of Religion timi cauk ningin Europe mi hna cu khuasik thla i ni a tawi bik caan ah puai tuah awk le khuachia ṭhawl awkah an inn ah “mei an van i a hring pengmi thingkung a phunphun” in an ṭamh. Mistletoe le holly kung: Mah kung hi Christmas ṭamhnak caah hman tawnmi a si. “Mistletoe kung ah khuaruahhar a simi thil ti khawhnak a um tiah celtic siangbawi pawl nih an zumh. Nika a rak kir ṭhannak puai caah a zungzal in a hring pengmi holly kung kha an biak.”—The Encyclopedia Americana. Christmas thingkung: “A hmaan lomi biaknak ah a ummi Europe mi hna Khrihfa biaknak i an luh hnu hmanhah thingkung biaknak cu a um rih.” Thingkung biaknak lakah atu tiang a um peng rihmi phungphai pakhat cu “khuasik thla lai ah tuahmi puai hna caah innka luhnak asiloah innchung ah Christmas thingkung an chiahmi” hi a si.—Encyclopædia Britannica.Jesuh Khrih cu mah ni, mah thla ah a chuak tiah langhtermi Baibal ah a um lo. Cherhchanmi cauk cheukhat ah hitin a langhter:  “Khrih a chuah ni taktak cu hngalh a si lo.”—New Catholic Encyclopedia.  “Khrih a chuah ni cu fiang tein hngalh a si lo.”—Encyclopedia of Early Christianity.‘Jesuh cu zeitikah dah a chuah?’ timi biahalnak i a phi cu Baibal ah direct in a um lo nain Jesuh a chuah laite ah a cangmi thil pahnih a um. Mah thil sining kha zoh in mi tampi nih Jesuh cu December 25 ah a chuah lo tiah an ti.Khuasik caan ah a si lo Min thlaknak. Jesuh a chuah hlanah Caesar Augustus nih “ram chung i a ummi vialte nih milu relnak caah nan min nan i thla dih lai” tiah nawl a chuah. Cucaah mikip nih “anmahle an khua cio ah” kal in min an i thlak a hau. An khua cio i an kir ṭhan tikah zarhkhat asiloah mah nak tam an rau kho. (Luka 2:1-3) Ngunkhuai kholhnak le ralkap tlaknak ti bantuk caah bawmtu a si nakhnga cutin nawl a chuahmi a si kho men. Mi pawl nih cu bantuk kongkau ruangah khual tlawn kha an duh lo. Cucaah Augustus nih a ukmi mi pawl kha khuasik caan ah hramhram in khual tlawnter in an thinhun dingin cun a tuah theng lai lo. Tuu. “An tuurun a zohkhenh i ramlak i a riakmi” tuukhal pawl an um. (Luka 2:8) Tuurun pawl cu “Lanhtak Puai [March thla donghlei] a phak hlan zarhkhat” in November thla lai tiang hrawng ramlak ah an um tiah cauk pakhat (Daily Life in the Time of Jesus) nih a ti. Hitin a ti chap: “Tuurun pawl cu khuasik caan ah cungkhuh a ummi thlam tangah an um. Asinain tuukhal pawl cu ramlak ah an um tiah Thawngṭha cauk nih a ti caah khuasik caan ah Christmas puai an tuahmi hi hmaan dawh a si lo.”Khuasik thla thawkJesuh a thih nithla AD 33, ṭhal caan, Nisan 14, Lanhtak Puai in hnulei ah kan rel ṭhan ahcun Jesuh zeitik ah dah a chuah ti kha hngalh khawh a si. (Johan 19:14-16) Kum thum le cheu a raumi phungchim rian a thawk lioah Jesus cu kum 30 hrawng a si. Cucaah Jesuh cu BC 2, khuasik thla thawk ah a chuak.—Luka 3:23.Jesuh Khrih cu December 25 ah a chuak timi langhtertu a um lo nain zeicah mah ni ah Christmas puai an tuah? Encyclopædia Britannica ningin biaknaklei hruaitu hna nih khuasik thla i ni a tawi bik caan ah “siasal a biami Rom mi hna nih tuahmi ‘teinak a hmu pengmi nika pathian chuah ni puai’ he khahter” dingin mah ni kha an thimmi a si. The Encyclopedia Americana ningin “a hmaan lomi biaknak in Khrihfa biaknak ah a rak lutmi hna caah cohlan a fawi deuh nakhnga” cutin an tuahmi a si tiah Baibal lei mifim tampi nih an zumh.Pathian nih “nu le pa sualnak aa summi” si hna seh ti a kan duh tiah Baibal nih a ti. (1 Thesalon 4:3) Baibal ah a hmanmi “nu le pa sualnak” timi biafang ah zuanzamnak, nulenu palepa sualnak le aa ṭhium rih lomi nu le pa umṭinak ti bantuk hna aa tel.Ṭhitumnak an tuah maw, tuah lo ti cu zeicah Pathian caah a biapit?Nuam tein kan umṭi kho lai maw ti hngalh awkah ṭhitum hlanin umṭinak he aa tlaiin tah zeitin?Nuva hna nih a fekmi chungkhar kha zeitindah an dirh khawh?Ṭhitumnak cu Pathian nih a dirhmi a si. Pathian nih hmasa bik nuva a fonh hna lioah ṭhitumnak kha a hram a rak thawk. (Genesis 2:22-24) Pathian nih ṭhitum biakamnak tuah loin nu le pa umṭi ding kha a timhmi a si lo.  Pathian nih minung caah zeidah a ṭha bik ti kha a hngalh. Pathian nih nu pakhat le pa pakhat a funtomtu ṭhitumnak kha zungzal ca in a timh. Mah thawngin chungkhar mi vialte nih ṭhathnemnak le huhphenhnak an hmuh lai. Tahchunhnak pakhat hi ruathmanh. Thilri sertu ṭialmi lamhruainak nih thilri pawl zeitindah hmaan tein bunh ding ti kha a langhter, cu bantukin Pathian lamhruainak nih chungkhar pehtlaihnak ah hlawhtlinnak hmuh khawh ning kha a kan chimh. Pathian phunglam a zulmi hna cu ṭhathnemhnak an hmu zungzal.—Isaiah 48:17, 18.Thilri sertu ṭialmi lamhruainak nih thilri pawl zeitindah hmaan tein bunh ding ti kha a langhter, cu bantukin Pathian lamhruainak nih chungkhar pehtlaihnak ah hlawhtlinnak hmuh khawh ning kha a kan chimh  I ṭhitum loin nupa sualnak tuahnak nih ṭih a nungmi thil tampi a chuahter. Tahchunhnak ah, duh loin fapawinak, nupa ihṭinak in chawnh khawhmi zawtnak le lungfahnak hna a chuahter khawh.*  Pathian nih nupa umṭinak thawngin fa ngeih khawhnak a pek hna. Pathian nih nunnak kha a sunsak tuk i fa ngeih khawhnak cu a sunglawi tukmi laksawng a si. Ṭhitumnak he aa tlaiin Pathian timhtuahnak kha kan upatnak thawngin Pathian nih mah laksawng kha sunsak hna seh ti a kan duh.—Hebru 13:4.A hlawh a tlingmi chungkhar ngeih khawh awkah ṭhitum biakamnak tuah hlanin hmunkhat ah umṭi hmasa a hau lo. Mah canah an pahnih ningin a fekmi biakamnak an tuah tik le buaibainak hna an tawnghthamṭi tikah an i pehtlaihnak cu a fek chin lai.* Ṭhitumnak nih biakamnak kha a fehter chin lai.—Matthai 19:6.A tlingmi chungkhar a um lo. Asinain nuva hna nih Baibal ruahnak cheuhnak an zulhnak thawngin a hlawh a tlingmi chungkhar an ser khawh. Tahchunhnak cheukhat hi zohhmanh:  Nanmah nakin nan innchunghawi herhmi kha biapi deuh ah chia u.—1 Korin 7:3-5; Filipi 2:3, 4.  Pakhat le pakhat i daw u law i upat zungzal u.—Efesa 5:25, 33.  Nan biachim kha i ralring u.—Phungthlukbia 12:18.  Lungsaunak ngei u law i ngaithiam colh u.—Kolose 3:13, 14.A cuza cangmi fale nih kum upa a simi nulepa zohkhenh awkah a biapi tukmi rian an ngei. Baibal nih hitin a ti: “An innchungkhar zohkhenh le an pa si hna seh, an pi si hna seh, cawm ṭhan ve cu an rian pakhatnak ah an chiah awk a si i cucu biaknaklei in an rian, Pathian nih tuah hna seh ti a duhmi rian cu a si.” (1Timote 5:4) A cuza cangmi fale nih kum upa a simi nulepa an zohkhenhmi hna cu na nu le na pa upat hna timi Baibal nawlbia an zulhmi a si.—Efesa 6:2,3.Kum upa a simi nulepa zohkhenhnak he aa tlaiin Baibal ah cuset khaset timi lamhruainak a um lo. Asinain nulepa a zohkhenhmi, zumhnak a ngeimi nu le pa cheukhat kong cu a langhter. Mah lengah nulepa a zohkhenhmi hna caah bawmtu a simi a ṭhami ruahnak cheuhnak zong a langhter.Baibal chan ah chungkharmi cheukhat nih kum upa a simi nulepa kha zeitindah an zohkhenh hna?Zei bantuk Baibal ruahnak cheuhnak nih dah nulepa a zohkhenhmi kha a bawmh khawh hna?Baibal nih kum upa a simi nulepa kha inn ah umter in zohkhenh awk a si tiah a ti maw?Thil sining cungah i hngat in lam tampi in an rak zohkhenh hna. Josef cu kum upa a simi a pa, Jakob he aa hlatnak hmun ah a um. Josef nih caanṭha a hmuh tikah a pa kha a pawngah rak i ṭhial dingin a timhtuah. A pa a rak phanh tikah umnak inn le rawl a pek lengah a rak huhphenh.—Genesis 45:9-11; 47:11, 12. Ruth cu a vapa nu i a ram ah a rak i ṭhial ve i a va nu zohkhenh awkah rian fakpi in a ṭuan.—Ruth 1:16; 2:2, 17, 18, 23. Jesuh nih a thih lai te ah nuhmei si dawh a simi a nu, Mary a zohkhenhtu ding kha a rak thim.—Johan 19:26, 27.*Kum upa a simi nulepa zohkhenhnak ah pumsalei le lungthinlei batnak ti bantuk zuamcawhnak a um khawh caah Baibal phunglam hna nih a kan bawmh khawh. Nulepa kha upat hna.Baibal chimmi: “Nan nu le nan pa kha upat hna u.”—Exodus 20:12.Baibal phunglam zulh khawh ning: A si khawh ahcun an nunnak he aa tlaiin anmah tein khuakhanternak thawngin upatnak kha langhter. Cun zohkhenhnak he aa tlai zongin anmah tein biakhiak hna seh. Mah lengah na bawmh khawhmi thil hna kha a tlari tein tuahpiaknak thawngin upatnak kha langhter. Theihthiampiak hna law ngaithiam hna.Baibal chimmi: “Lungsau thinfual hi fim a si, palhnak i maimilh cio hi minung sunparnak a si.”—Phungthlukbia 19:11.Baibal phunglam zulh khawh ning: Kum upa a simi nulepa nih na zohkhenh hnanak kha zei rel loin le zaangfahnak ngei loin bia an chim tikah hitin i hal, ‘Anmah bantukin ri ka ngeih i zeihmanh ka tuah khawh lo tikah zeitindah ka um lai?’ Theihthiampiak ding le ngaihthiam dingin naa zuam ahcun thil sining a chiat chin nakhnga lo na hrial khawh lai. Midang kha ruahnak cheuhnak hal hna.Baibal chimmi: “Ruahnak i cheuhnak a um lo ahcun khuakhannak kha a pingah a kal tawn, sihmanhsehlaw ruahnak cheutu an tam ahcun a hlawh a tling tawn.”—Phungthlukbia 15:22.Baibal phunglam zulh khawh ning: Na nu le na pa nih an ngeihmi zawtnak tawnghtham ning kha hlathlainak tuah. Nan hmunhma ah a ummi zohkhenhnak he aa tlaiin zei bantuk bawmhnak dah hmuh khawh a si ti kha hlathlai. Nulepa a zohkhenhmi hna he bia i ruah u. Unau na ngeih ahcun nulepa i an herhmi, zohkhenh ning, rian i phawtnak ti bantuk kha chungkhar ningin i ruah u.Kum upa a simi nulepa zohkhenhnak kong kha chungkhar ningin i ruah u Toidornak ngei u.Baibal chimmi: “Mi toidor te i um a ṭha deuh.”—Phungthlukbia 11:2.Baibal phunglam zulh khawh ning: Ri ka ngei ti kha cohlang. Tahchunhnak ah, mikip nih a caan le thazaang he aa tlaiin ri kan ngei. Mah cu na nu le na pa zeitluk in dah na zohkhenh khawh hna timi cungah huham a ngei. A hleiin zohkhenh a herhmi nulepa kha na zohkhenh hnanak ah na bat a si ahcun chungkharmi a dang le siibawi pawl kha bawmhnak hal hna. Nangmahle nangmah zong i zohkhenh.Baibal chimmi: “Ahohmanh nih mah pum kha an hua bal lo. ... Ahohmanh nih a pum cu a zoh, a khenh i a cawm.”—Efesa 5:29.Baibal phunglam zulh khawh ning: Nulepa zohkhenhnak rian na ngeih buin nangmah herhmi le innchunghawi a ngeimi na si ahcun na chungkhar herhmi zohkhenh awk zongah rian na ngei ko lai. Ngandamnak a pemi rawl ei a hau. I dinhnak le ihnak caah a caan a za in pek a hau. (Phungchimtu 4:6) A si khawh tik paohah chikkhat i din. Cutin na tuah ahcun nulepa zohkhenhnak ah lungthinlei le pumsalei in timhcia na si lai.Fale nih nulepa kha inn ah umter in zohkhenh a hau timi lamhruainak Baibal ah a um lo. Cheukhat nih cun kum upa a simi nulepa kha a si khawh chung inn ah umter in zohkhenh awkah bia an khiah. Asinain thil sining cheukhat ahcun tar zohkhenhnak inn i chiah ah a ṭha deuh tiah bia an khiah men lai. Zeitin tuah ah dah a ṭhat bik lai ti kha chungkharmi dihlak in an i ruahceih awk a si.—Galati 6:4,5.Baibal nih thi ei hlah u tiah nawlbia a kan pek. Cucaah thi le thi cheubang pawl kha ei asiloah rawnh ti bantuk kan cohlang lo. A tanglei Baibal caang hna hi hlathlai: Genesis 9:4. Pathian nih Noah le a chungkhar kha buanchukcho a dih hnuah saram pawl kha rawl caah einak nawl a pek hna. Asinain thi cu ei hlah u tiah nawl a pek hna. Pathian nih Noah kha hitin a ti: “Sa kha a chung i thi a um lioah cun nan ei lai lo.” Kan dihlak in Noah tefa kan si caah mah caan thawkin mah nawlbia cu minung dihlak he pehtlaihnak a ngei. Levitikas 17:14. “Zei sa thi hmanh nan ei lai lo, zeitintiah titsa vialte nunnak cu an thi cu a si; a eitu paoh cu hlonh a si lai.” Nunnak cu thi a si i amah ta in Pathian nih a hmuh. Mah nawlbia cu Israel miphun lawng a pekmi hna a si ko nain thi ei thlauhnak nawlbia cu Pathian nih biapi tuk ah a chiah ti a lang. Lamkaltu 15:20. “Zei thi hmanh ei nan i sum lai.” Pathian nih Noah a pekmi nawlbia kha Khrihfa pawl zong a pek ve hna. Hmasa Khrihfa hna nih thi ei asiloah sii thlopnak caah thi hman an duh lo ti kha tuanbia nih a langhtermi a um.Pathian nih thi ei hlah u tiah zeicah nawl a kan pek?Thi rawnh cu ngandamnak caah ṭihnung a si ti kha siilei fimthiamnak nih a langhtermi a um. A biapi deuhmi cu thi nih Pathian caah a sunglawi tukmi thil kha a aiawh. Cucaah Pathian nih thi kha ei hlah u tiah nawl a kan peknak a si.—Levitikas 17:11; Kolose 1:20.Nausem chuah asiloah “nau hrawhnak” timi biafang cu Baibal ah a um lo. Asinain a chuak rih lomi naute i telin minung nunnak kha Pathian nih zeitindah a hmuh ti a langhtermi Baibal caang tampi a um.Nunnak cu Pathian sinin hmuhmi laksawng a si. (Genesis 9:6; Salm 36:9) Nu paw chungah a ummi naute i telin nunnak vialte kha Pathian nih a sunsak. Cucaah a chuak rih lomi naute a thih nakhnga hramhram in tuah cu lainawn a si.Israel mi sin pekmi Pathian Nawlbia nih hitin a ti: “I vuak i velhnak hmun ah fapawi nu pakhatkhat kha pa pakhatkhat nih a tuk i a mah cu a thi lo nain a fa kha a rawh ahcun a tutu pa kha a tukmi nu i a va nih ka liamh seh a ti zat paohin dantat a si lai i biaceihtu hna nih cawi seh an timi zat in a cawi lai. Sihmanhsehlaw a thih ahcun dantatnak cu nunnak caah nunnak ve ... a si lai.”—Exodus 21:22, 23.*Minung nunnak cu zeitik in dah aa thawk?Nau aa hrawk balmi kha Pathian nih a ngaithiam lai maw?A nu asiloah naute nunnak caah ṭih a nun tikah nau hrawh cu a palh maw?Nau aa sem cangka in Pathian nih nunnak a ngeimi in a hmuh cang. A chuak rih lomi naute kha mi pakhat in Pathian Bia, Baibal nih a langhter tawn. Nu paw chung i naute nunnak le a chuak cangmi naute nunnak cu aa khat in Pathian nih a hmuh ti a langhtermi tahchunhnak cheukhat kha zohhmanh u.  Thiang thlarau forhfialnak thawngin Siangpahrang David nih hitin a ti: “Ka chuah hlanin na rak ka hmuh diam cang.” (Salm 139:16) Pathian nih David kha a chuah hlanin mi pakhat in a hmuh cang.   Jeremiah cu a chuah hlanin profet a si lai ti kha Pathian nih a hngalh cang. Pathian nih hitin a ti: “Paw chung i kaan ser hlanah kaan hngalh i na chuah hlanah kaan thianter cang; nangmah cu miphun hna ca i profet ah kaan chiah cang.”—Jeremiah 1:5.  Baibal ṭialtu siibawi Luka nih a chuak rih lomi naute ca le a chuak kami naute caah Greek biafang pakhat kha a hman.—Luka 1:41; 2:12, 16.Nau aa hrawk balmi hna nih Pathian ngaihthiamnak kha an hmuh khawh. Nunnak kha Pathian hmuh ningin an hun hmuh tikah sualnak ka ngei timi ruahnak an ngeih awk a si ti lo. “BAWIPA cu zaangfahnak le dawtnak in a khat. ... Nichuahlei le nitlaklei an i hlat tluk khin kan sualnak cu kanmah he i hlat ah a kan ṭhialpiak.” (Salm 103:8-12) Nau hrawhnak i telin hlanah rak tuahmi sualnak caah lungtak in aa ngaichihmi hna kha Jehovah nih a ngaihthiam hna lai.—Salm 86:5.A chuak rih lomi naute nunnak he aa tlaiin Baibal chimmi kha na hngalh cang ahcun a nu asiloah naute nunnak caah ṭih a nung timi ruang men ah nau naa hrawk lai lo.Nau hrin lioah a nu nunnak le naute nunnak ah pakhatkhat thim a hau timi lakhruak in a cang khomi thil sining nan ton ah tah zeitin? Cu bantuk thil sining a tongmi hna nih anmah tein biakhiahnak an tuah awk a si.Baibal ah kuak zuk* le khuhsii hmannak kong he aa tlaiin a chimmi a um lo. Asinain kan ngandamnak a hnorsuangmi le Pathian nih a duh lomi a thiang lomi ziaza pawl a langhtermi phunglam hna cu a um. Cucaah kuak zuk cu sual a si ti kha kan hngalh khawh. Nunnak kha upat. ‘Pathian cu minung kha nunnak le thaw a petu a si.’ (Lamkaltu 17:24, 25) Nunnak cu Pathian nih a kan pekmi laksawng a si caah kuak zuk ti bantuk chan a tawiter khomi zeibantuk thil hmanh kha kan tuah awk a si lo. Kuak zuk cu vawleicung pumpi ah thihnak a chuahter khomi thil lakah pakhat a si ve, asinain mah cu kham khawh a si ko. Innpa kha daw hna. “Na innpa cu nangmah naa dawt bantukin na dawt lai.” (Matthai 22:39) Mi lakah kuak zuk cu dawtnak ngeih lo a si. Kuak a zumi pawngah a ummi hna nih kuak khu kha an dawp ve caah kuak a zumi hna nih an ngeihmi zawtnak bantuk kha an ngei ve. Thiang tein um. “Pathian sinah a nungin pekchanhmi raithawinak bantukin i pe tuah u ... cohlan awk tlakmi si tuah u.” (Rom 12:1) “Pum siseh, thlarau siseh, a thurhnomhtertu paohpaoh kha i thenh u sihlaw Pathian ṭih bu tein um u sih.” (2Korin 7:1) Kuak zuk cu thiannak he aa ralchanhmi a si. Khuhsii a hmangmi hna cu an pum fakpi in a hnorsuang khomi ṭih a nungmi siivai hramhram in a hmangmi an si.Weed asiloah pot tiah auhmi sahdah kong le a dang ritnak siivai kong kha Baibal ah an min in a chimmi a um lo. Asinain mi a leem khomi mah bantuk thil hna kha nuamhnak sawhsawh in hman awk a si lonak kong a langhtermi phunglam tu cu a um. A cunglei i phunglam hna lengah mah lamhruainak hna zong hi hman khawh an si: Lungthinlei thil ti khawhnak kha uk khawh a hau. “Bawipa na Pathian cu na lungthin dihlak ... in na dawt lai.” (Matthai 22:37, 38) “Ralring tein um u.” (1Peter 1:13) Ritnak siivai a hmangmi pakhat nih cun a lungthin kha ṭha tein aa uk kho lo. Ritnak siivai nih a leemmi mi tampi an um. A ṭhami thil kha an ruat kho ti lo i ritnak siivai hmuh khawhnak lam lawng kha an kawl.—Filipi 4:8. Upadi zul. “Bawi le nawlngeitu pawl kha an nawl nan ngaih hna lai.” (Titus 3:1) Ram tampi ah ritnak siivai cheukhat kha fakpi in an khenkham. Pathian mithmai ṭha hmuh kan duh ahcun cozah pawl nawl kha kan ngaih a hau.—Rom 13:1.Baibal nih midang thil ṭhenh awk le a ruang ṭha a um caah cutin tuah awkah timhcia tein um u tiah a kan forh. Mah nih a hmutu lawng si loin a petu zong peknak in ṭhatnak hmuh khawh a si ti kha a langhter. (Phungthlukbia 11:25; Luka 6:38) Jesuh nih “pek leiah hin hmuh lei nakin lunglawmhnak a um deuh” tiah a ti.”—Lamkaltu 20:35.Peknak nih zeitik ah dah Pathian lung a lawmhter?Peknak nih zeitik ah dah Pathian lung a lawmhter lo?Peknak he aa tlaimi Baibal caang hnaLungtho tein peknak nih ṭhatnak a chuahter. Baibal nih hitin a ti: “Cucaah nanmah le nan lungthin nan i thleh ning cio in rak tho u, nan thawh tikah i ngaihchih bu le hnekchom in si hlah seh, lunglawm tein a thomi kha Pathian nih a dawt hna.”—2Korin 9:7.Lungtho tein peknak cu Pathian cohlanmi “biaknak” phunkhat a si. (Jeim 1:27) A chambaumi hna siang ngaiin a bawmmi cu Pathian nih an cungah leiba a ngeimi bantukin aa ruah. (Phungthlukbia 19:17) Cucaah Pathian nih a cham ṭhan lai tiah Baibal nih a kan cawnpiak.—Luka 14:12-14.Mah ca ṭhatnak in siannak langhter tikah. Tahchunhnak ah:  Midang lungthin lak awkah.—Matthai 6:2.  Pakhatkhat hmuh ṭhan awkah.—Luka 14:12-14.  Khamhnak cawk awkah.—Salm 49:6, 7.Mah nih Pathian duh lomi tuahsernak asiloah lungput hna a hlorh tikah. Tahchunhnak ah, mi pakhat kha phe kahnak caah, ritnak sii asiloah zu ningcang loin hmannak caah tangka pek cu a palh lai. (1Korin 6:9, 10; 2Korin 7:1) Cun rian ṭuan a huam lo caah amah tein aa cawm kho lomi bawmh zong aa tlak lomi a si.—2Thesalon 3:10.Mah innchungkhar kha zei rel loin midang tu tampi pek tikah. Chungkharlu nih a innchungkhar herhbaumi kha a zohkhenh awk a si tiah Baibal nih a kan cawnpiak. (1Timote 5:8) Chungkharlu nih a innchungkhar hnorsuang tiangin midang kha tam tuk a pek hna ahcun a palh lai. Cu bantukin an ngeihmi thilri kha “Pathian ta a si” tiin kum upa a simi an nu le an pa zohkhenh a duh lomi hna kha Jesuh nih a mawtchiat hna.—Marka 7:9-13.
